const express = require('express'); const { createClient } = require('@supabase/supabase-js'); const Anthropic = require('@anthropic-ai/sdk'); const { Resend } = require('resend'); const cors = require('cors'); const multer = require('multer'); const PDFDocument = require('pdfkit'); const webpush = require('web-push'); const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit'); const crypto = require('crypto'); const helmet = require('helmet'); const upload = multer({ storage: multer.memoryStorage(), limits: { fileSize: 15 * 1024 * 1024 } }); // INFRA 1 — Sentry error monitoring let Sentry = null; if (process.env.SENTRY_DSN) { try { Sentry = require('@sentry/node'); Sentry.init({ dsn: process.env.SENTRY_DSN, tracesSampleRate: 0.1 }); log('info', 'sentry.initialized'); } catch (e) { console.warn('Sentry init failed:', e.message); } } const app = express(); app.use(helmet({ // A4a: HSTS — forces HTTPS for 2 years, preload-eligible hsts: { maxAge: 63072000, includeSubDomains: true, preload: true }, // A4b: CSP — locks down script/style/connect sources contentSecurityPolicy: { directives: { defaultSrc: ["'self'"], scriptSrc: ["'self'", 'https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com', 'https://js.stripe.com', "'unsafe-inline'"], styleSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'", 'https://fonts.googleapis.com'], fontSrc: ["'self'", 'https://fonts.gstatic.com'], imgSrc: ["'self'", 'data:', 'https:'], connectSrc: ["'self'", 'https://*.supabase.co', 'wss://*.supabase.co', 'https://api.anthropic.com'], frameSrc: ["'none'"], frameAncestors: ["'none'"], objectSrc: ["'none'"], baseUri: ["'self'"] } }, // A4c: Additional hardening crossOriginEmbedderPolicy: false, // Allow CDN resources referrerPolicy: { policy: 'strict-origin-when-cross-origin' } })); app.use(cors()); // ── STRUCTURED JSON LOGGING ──────────────────────────────────── // Tier 4 — every log line is a searchable JSON object in Railway logs // Query examples: grep '"status":"error"' | grep '"endpoint":"/visit/checkin"' function log(level, event, data = {}) { const entry = { ts: new Date().toISOString(), level, // info | warn | error event, // human-readable label e.g. "checkin.failed" ...data // operator_id, endpoint, duration_ms, psw_name, error, etc }; if (level === 'error') { console.error(JSON.stringify(entry)); } else if (level === 'warn') { console.warn(JSON.stringify(entry)); } else { console.log(JSON.stringify(entry)); } } // ── TORONTO TIME HELPERS ────────────────────────────────────────── // Railway servers run in UTC. now.toTimeString() returns UTC HH:MM, // which when written to time_in/time_out causes a 4-5 hour skew on // PSW portal display. These helpers always return Toronto local time. const TZ_TORONTO = 'America/Toronto'; function torontoHM(date = new Date()) { // Returns "HH:MM" in 24-hour Toronto time, accounting for DST automatically const parts = new Intl.DateTimeFormat('en-CA', { timeZone: TZ_TORONTO, hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit', hour12: false }).formatToParts(date); const h = parts.find(p => p.type === 'hour').value.padStart(2, '0'); const m = parts.find(p => p.type === 'minute').value.padStart(2, '0'); return `${h === '24' ? '00' : h}:${m}`; } function torontoDate(date = new Date()) { // Returns "YYYY-MM-DD" in Toronto local date return new Intl.DateTimeFormat('en-CA', { timeZone: TZ_TORONTO, year: 'numeric', month: '2-digit', day: '2-digit' }).format(date); } // ── PHASE A1: AUDIT LOG ───────────────────────────────────────────── // PHIPA s.12 "reasonable safeguards" — immutable append-only audit trail // Hash-chained: each row signs prev_hash so tampering is detectable // Writes to: audit_log table (Supabase — INSERT only, no UPDATE/DELETE) // ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── const AUDIT_HMAC_KEY = process.env.AUDIT_HMAC_KEY || 'proximity-audit-key-2026'; // In-memory last-hash cache per operator (avoid extra DB read on every write) const _auditLastHash = new Map(); async function auditLog(req, { action, entity_type, entity_id, actor_type, actor_name, changes } = {}) { try { const operator_id = req?.hqOperatorId || req?.body?.operator_id || 'proximity-care'; const cacheKey = operator_id; // Get previous hash — try cache first, then DB let prev_hash = _auditLastHash.get(cacheKey); if (!prev_hash) { const { data: last } = await supabase .from('audit_log') .select('row_hash') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .order('id', { ascending: false }) .limit(1) .single(); prev_hash = last?.row_hash || 'GENESIS'; } const occurred_at = new Date().toISOString(); const row = { operator_id, actor_type: actor_type || 'system', actor_name: actor_name || 'server', action: action || 'unknown', entity_type: entity_type || 'unknown', entity_id: entity_id ? String(entity_id) : null, changes: changes || null, ip: req?.ip || null, user_agent: req?.headers?.['user-agent'] || null, occurred_at, prev_hash }; // HMAC-SHA256 hash chain: sign (prev_hash + canonical row) const canonical = JSON.stringify(row, Object.keys(row).sort()); const row_hash = require('crypto') .createHmac('sha256', AUDIT_HMAC_KEY) .update(prev_hash + '|' + canonical) .digest('hex'); const { error } = await supabase .from('audit_log') .insert({ ...row, row_hash }); if (!error) { _auditLastHash.set(cacheKey, row_hash); } else { log('warn', 'audit_log.write_failed', { error: error.message, operator_id }); } } catch (e) { // Audit log must NEVER crash the main request log('warn', 'audit_log.exception', { error: e.message }); } } // ── D3: HCN FIELD ENCRYPTION (AES-256-GCM) ───────────────────────── // PHIPA s.12 — Health Card Numbers are PHI and must be encrypted at rest // Key stored in Railway env var HCN_ENCRYPTION_KEY (32-byte hex) // Envelope: iv(12B) + authTag(16B) + ciphertext — base64 stored in DB // If key not set, falls back to storing plaintext with a warning (dev mode) const HCN_KEY_HEX = process.env.HCN_ENCRYPTION_KEY; const HCN_KEY = HCN_KEY_HEX ? Buffer.from(HCN_KEY_HEX, 'hex') : null; if (!HCN_KEY) { log('warn', 'hcn.no_key', { note: 'HCN_ENCRYPTION_KEY not set — health card numbers stored unencrypted. Set env var in Railway.' }); } function encryptHCN(plaintext) { if (!plaintext) return null; if (!HCN_KEY) return plaintext; // dev fallback const iv = require('crypto').randomBytes(12); const cipher = require('crypto').createCipheriv('aes-256-gcm', HCN_KEY, iv); const enc = Buffer.concat([cipher.update(String(plaintext), 'utf8'), cipher.final()]); const tag = cipher.getAuthTag(); return Buffer.concat([iv, tag, enc]).toString('base64'); } function decryptHCN(ciphertext) { if (!ciphertext) return null; if (!HCN_KEY) return ciphertext; // dev fallback try { const buf = Buffer.from(ciphertext, 'base64'); const iv = buf.slice(0, 12); const tag = buf.slice(12, 28); const enc = buf.slice(28); const dec = require('crypto').createDecipheriv('aes-256-gcm', HCN_KEY, iv); dec.setAuthTag(tag); return Buffer.concat([dec.update(enc), dec.final()]).toString('utf8'); } catch { return null; // decryption failed — key mismatch or corrupted } } // ── WATCHDOG PIN ────────────────────────────────────────────────── const WATCHDOG_PIN = process.env.WATCHDOG_PIN || 'proximity-watchdog-2026'; // ── PHASE A3: PSW PIN HEADER AUTH ─────────────────────────────────── // PIN should come from x-psw-pin header, not query string (visible in logs) // Backward compatible: still accepts body.pin and query.pin // PSW portal will migrate to header-first in Phase A3 HTML pass function getPSWPin(req) { if (req.headers['x-psw-pin']) return req.headers['x-psw-pin']; if (req.body?.pin) return req.body.pin; if (req.query?.pin) { log('warn', 'psw.pin_in_querystring', { path: req.path, ip: req.ip, note: 'PIN sent in URL — should use x-psw-pin header' }); return req.query.pin; } return null; } // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // HQ SESSION TOKEN SYSTEM // In-memory token store: { token -> { operator_id, expires } } // Tokens expire after 8 hours, cleaned up every 6 hours // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // ── HQ SESSIONS — Supabase-backed ────────────────────────────────── // Stored in hq_sessions table so sessions survive Railway restarts/deploys. // Previously used an in-memory Map which was wiped on every restart. function generateToken() { const chars = 'ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789'; let token = ''; for (let i = 0; i < 48; i++) token += chars[Math.floor(Math.random() * chars.length)]; return token; } async function createHQSession(operator_id) { const token = generateToken(); const now = new Date(); const expiresAt = new Date(now.getTime() + 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000); // 8-hour ceiling await supabase.from('hq_sessions').insert({ token, operator_id, created_at: now.toISOString(), last_activity: now.toISOString(), expires_at: expiresAt.toISOString() }); return token; } const SESSION_IDLE_MS = 60 * 60 * 1000; // 60 minutes — PHIPA s.12 applies to patient portals; HQ is operator admin async function validateHQToken(req) { const token = req.headers['x-hq-token'] || req.query._hqt; if (!token) return null; // Token format check — real tokens are 48-char alphanumeric from generateToken() // Rejects malformed/spoofed tokens before hitting the DB if (!/^[A-Za-z0-9]{48}$/.test(token)) return null; const { data: session } = await supabase .from('hq_sessions') .select('operator_id, last_activity, expires_at') .eq('token', token) .maybeSingle(); if (!session) return null; const now = Date.now(); const expires = new Date(session.expires_at).getTime(); const lastActivity = new Date(session.last_activity).getTime(); // A2a: Absolute expiry (8 hours) if (now > expires) { await supabase.from('hq_sessions').delete().eq('token', token); return null; } // A2b: Idle timeout (15 minutes of inactivity) if (now - lastActivity > SESSION_IDLE_MS) { await supabase.from('hq_sessions').delete().eq('token', token); return null; } // Refresh last_activity on every valid request (fire-and-forget) supabase.from('hq_sessions') .update({ last_activity: new Date().toISOString() }) .eq('token', token) .then(() => {}).catch(() => {}); return session.operator_id; } async function requireHQAuth(req, res, next) { // Allow watchdog bypass if (req.headers['x-watchdog-pin'] === WATCHDOG_PIN) return next(); if (req.body?.watchdog_pin === WATCHDOG_PIN) return next(); if (req.query?.watchdog_pin === WATCHDOG_PIN) return next(); const operator_id = await validateHQToken(req); if (!operator_id) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'HQ session required. Please log in.' }); // Operator isolation: token must belong to the operator being queried // Prevents a valid token from one operator querying another operator's data const reqOp = req.query.operator_id || req.body?.operator_id; if (reqOp && reqOp !== operator_id) { return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Token does not match operator.' }); } // Attach operator_id to request so endpoints can use it req.hqOperatorId = operator_id; next(); } // Request middleware — tags every request with trace ID + captures duration + status app.use((req, res, next) => { req._traceId = crypto.randomBytes(6).toString('hex'); req._startMs = Date.now(); res.on('finish', () => { const duration_ms = Date.now() - req._startMs; const level = res.statusCode >= 500 ? 'error' : res.statusCode >= 400 ? 'warn' : 'info'; // Only log non-trivial requests (skip health pings and static) if (req.path !== '/' && !req.path.startsWith('/system/status')) { log(level, 'http.request', { trace_id: req._traceId, method: req.method, endpoint: req.path, status_code: res.statusCode, duration_ms, operator_id: req.body?.operator_id || req.query?.operator_id || undefined, psw_name: req.body?.psw_name || req.query?.psw_name || undefined, }); } }); next(); }); // BUILD 27 — Stripe webhook needs raw body for signature verification // Must be before express.json() app.use('/webhook/stripe', express.raw({ type: 'application/json' })); app.use(express.json({ limit: '100kb' })); // INFRA 3 — Rate limiting on public-facing endpoints const publicLimiter = rateLimit({ windowMs: 60 * 60 * 1000, // 1 hour max: 100, standardHeaders: true, legacyHeaders: false, message: { error: 'Too many requests — please try again later.' } }); const checkinLimiter = rateLimit({ windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 min max: 30, message: { error: 'Too many checkin attempts — please wait before trying again.' } }); app.use('/careers', publicLimiter); app.use('/intake', publicLimiter); // Lead intake — strict 3 submissions/hour per IP to prevent spam const leadLimiter = rateLimit({ windowMs: 60 * 60 * 1000, max: 3, standardHeaders: true, legacyHeaders: false, message: { error: 'Too many lead submissions — please try again later.' }, keyGenerator: (req) => req.ip || 'unknown' }); app.use('/webhook/lead', leadLimiter); app.use('/family/verify-pin', publicLimiter); app.use('/visit/checkin', checkinLimiter); app.use('/visit/checkout', checkinLimiter); // HQ PIN rate limiter — 10 attempts per hour per IP const hqPinLimiter = rateLimit({ windowMs: 60 * 60 * 1000, // 1 hour max: 10, standardHeaders: true, legacyHeaders: false, message: { error: 'Too many HQ login attempts — try again in 1 hour.' }, keyGenerator: (req) => req.ip || 'unknown' }); // Family portal actions — message, PDF, notifications (50/hour per IP) const familyLimiter = rateLimit({ windowMs: 60 * 60 * 1000, max: 50, standardHeaders: true, legacyHeaders: false, message: { error: 'Too many requests. Please wait before trying again.' } }); // PSW onboarding flow (20/hour per IP) const onboardLimiter = rateLimit({ windowMs: 60 * 60 * 1000, max: 20, standardHeaders: true, legacyHeaders: false, message: { error: 'Too many requests. Please wait before trying again.' } }); // Invoice generation (5/hour per IP) const invoiceLimiter = rateLimit({ windowMs: 60 * 60 * 1000, max: 5, standardHeaders: true, legacyHeaders: false, message: { error: 'Too many invoice requests. Try again later.' } }); // Internal cron endpoints — 30/hour, prevents external abuse const cronLimiter = rateLimit({ windowMs: 60 * 60 * 1000, max: 30, standardHeaders: true, legacyHeaders: false, message: { error: 'Rate limit reached.' } }); // AI endpoint rate limiter — 10 requests/hour per IP on any endpoint calling Anthropic const aiLimiter = rateLimit({ windowMs: 60 * 60 * 1000, max: 10, standardHeaders: true, legacyHeaders: false, message: { error: 'AI rate limit reached — max 10 requests per hour. Try again later.' }, keyGenerator: (req) => req.ip || 'unknown' }); app.use('/chat', aiLimiter); app.use('/crystal/chat', aiLimiter); app.use('/family/chat', aiLimiter); // System prompt lock — strip system_override and system keys from all incoming request bodies // System prompts must only come from server-side code, never from the client app.use((req, res, next) => { if (req.body && typeof req.body === 'object') { delete req.body.system_override; delete req.body.system; } next(); }); app.use('/hq/verify-pin', hqPinLimiter); // Note: /hq/auth has hqPinLimiter applied inline in the route handler // ── HQ AUTH MIDDLEWARE — all /hq/* routes require valid session token ── // Exceptions: /hq/auth (login), /hq/logout, /hq/branding (needed for white label lock screen) app.use('/hq', (req, res, next) => { const path = req.path; // Allow unauthenticated access to login, logout, and branding endpoints if (path === '/auth' || path === '/logout' || path === '/branding') return next(); // Allow watchdog/health console if (req.headers['x-watchdog-pin'] === WATCHDOG_PIN) return next(); if (req.body?.watchdog_pin === WATCHDOG_PIN) return next(); if (req.query?.watchdog_pin === WATCHDOG_PIN) return next(); // All other /hq/* require valid session token return requireHQAuth(req, res, next); }); // Family portal app.use('/family/message', familyLimiter); app.use('/family/care-plan-pdf', familyLimiter); app.use('/notify/visit-complete', familyLimiter); // PSW onboarding app.use('/psw/onboard', onboardLimiter); app.use('/psw/confirm-interview', onboardLimiter); // Invoice app.use('/invoice/generate', invoiceLimiter); // Internal cron endpoints app.use('/followup/run', cronLimiter); app.use('/hq/noshow-check', cronLimiter); app.use('/hq/daily-digest', cronLimiter); app.use('/hq/shift-reminder-today', cronLimiter); app.use('/visit/checklist-check', cronLimiter); app.use('/invoice/auto-monthly', cronLimiter); // ── validateRequired helper — consistent 400 errors across all endpoints ── function validateRequired(body, fields) { const missing = fields.filter(f => body[f] === undefined || body[f] === null || body[f] === ''); if (missing.length) { return { valid: false, error: `Missing required fields: ${missing.join(', ')}` }; } return { valid: true }; } // Clients const supabase = createClient( process.env.SUPABASE_URL, process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_KEY ); const anthropic = new Anthropic({ apiKey: process.env.ANTHROPIC_API_KEY }); const pushEnabled = !!(process.env.VAPID_PUBLIC_KEY && process.env.VAPID_PRIVATE_KEY && process.env.VAPID_SUBJECT); if (pushEnabled) { webpush.setVapidDetails(process.env.VAPID_SUBJECT, process.env.VAPID_PUBLIC_KEY, process.env.VAPID_PRIVATE_KEY); } else { console.warn('Web push disabled — VAPID_PUBLIC_KEY / VAPID_PRIVATE_KEY / VAPID_SUBJECT env vars not set'); } async function sendPush(subjectType, subjectId, payload) { if (_watchdogRunning) return; // suppress push notifications during health console scans if (!pushEnabled || !subjectId) return; try { const { data: subs } = await supabase .from('push_subscriptions') .select('id, endpoint, p256dh, auth') .eq('subject_type', subjectType) .eq('subject_id', subjectId); if (!subs || subs.length === 0) return; const body = JSON.stringify(payload); await Promise.all(subs.map(async s => { try { await webpush.sendNotification( { endpoint: s.endpoint, keys: { p256dh: s.p256dh, auth: s.auth } }, body ); } catch (e) { if (e.statusCode === 404 || e.statusCode === 410) { try { await supabase.from('push_subscriptions').delete().eq('id', s.id); } catch {} } else { log('error', 'Push send failed', { error: e.message || String(e), trace_id: req?._traceId }); } } })); } catch (e) { log('error', 'sendPush error', { error: e.message || String(e), trace_id: req?._traceId }); } } async function getOperator(operator_id) { const { data } = await supabase .from('operators') .select('*') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .single(); return data; } // Global flag set by /system/run-tests to suppress all outbound emails during watchdog scans let _watchdogRunning = false; let _watchdogStartedAt = null; // timestamp when scan started // ── CASL UNSUBSCRIBE FOOTER ──────────────────────────────────── // Canada's Anti-Spam Legislation requires business address + unsubscribe on all commercial email const CASL_FOOTER = `
Proximity Care Services Inc. · 7075 Rexwood Rd, Mississauga, ON L4T 4L3 · 647-382-8047
You are receiving this email because you have a care relationship with Proximity Care Services.
Unsubscribe
`; async function sendEmail({ to, subject, html, attachments }) { if (_watchdogRunning) { log('info', 'email.suppressed', { to, subject, reason: 'watchdog_running' }); return; // suppress all emails during health console scans } // CASL: append unsubscribe footer before closing or at end let compliantHtml = html; if (html.includes('')) { compliantHtml = html.replace('', CASL_FOOTER + ''); } else { compliantHtml = html + CASL_FOOTER; } const resend = new Resend(process.env.RESEND_API_KEY); const payload = { from: process.env.RESEND_FROM || 'Proximity HQ ', to: Array.isArray(to) ? to : [to], subject, html: compliantHtml, bcc: process.env.BCC_EMAIL || 'healthcareproximity@gmail.com' }; if (attachments) payload.attachments = attachments; await resend.emails.send(payload); } // ── PHIPA NAME ANONYMIZER ────────────────────────────────────── // Strips real client/PSW names from all Anthropic API prompts. // Returns { anonymized, deAnonymize(text) } so responses can be restored. function phipaAnonymize(text, names) { // names = [{ real: 'Rosetta Ferrari', code: 'CLIENT-A' }, ...] const map = {}; const reverseMap = {}; let result = text; (names || []).forEach(({ real, code }) => { if (!real || !code) return; map[real] = code; reverseMap[code] = real; // Replace full name result = result.split(real).join(code); // Replace first name only (if 2+ words) const first = real.split(' ')[0]; if (first && first.length > 2) { result = result.split(first).join(code.replace(/-[A-Z]$/, '') || code); } }); return { anonymized: result, deAnonymize: (responseText) => { let out = responseText; Object.entries(reverseMap).forEach(([code, real]) => { out = out.split(code).join(real); const shortCode = code.replace(/-[A-Z]$/, ''); if (shortCode !== code) out = out.split(shortCode).join(real.split(' ')[0]); }); return out; } }; } // Build name map from visit/invoice context for PHIPA compliance function buildNameMap(clientName, pswName) { const names = []; if (clientName) names.push({ real: clientName, code: 'CLIENT-A' }); if (pswName) names.push({ real: pswName, code: 'PSW-1' }); return names; } async function generateWithClaude(prompt, systemPrompt, nameMap) { // PHIPA: anonymize names before sending to Anthropic const { anonymized, deAnonymize } = phipaAnonymize(prompt, nameMap || []); const msg = await anthropic.messages.create({ model: 'claude-sonnet-4-20250514', max_tokens: 500, system: systemPrompt || 'You are a helpful assistant for a home care agency.', messages: [{ role: 'user', content: anonymized }] }); // PHIPA: restore real names in response for internal use return deAnonymize(msg.content[0].text); } app.get('/', (req, res) => { res.json({ status: 'Proximity Agent running', version: '1.0.0' }); }); app.post('/webhook/visit', async (req, res) => { try { console.log('Visit webhook payload:', JSON.stringify(req.body)); const operator_id = req.body.operator_id || 'proximity-care'; const psw_name = req.body.psw_name || req.body.PSW_Name; const psw_email = req.body.psw_email || req.body.PSW_Email; const client_name = req.body.Client_Name || req.body.client_name || ''; const client_first_name = req.body.client_first_name || client_name.split(' ')[0] || ''; const client_last_name = req.body.client_last_name || client_name.split(' ').slice(1).join(' ') || ''; const visit_date = req.body.visit_date || req.body.Date_of_Visit; const time_in = req.body.time_in || req.body.Time_In; const time_out = req.body.time_out || req.body.Time_Out; const tasks_completed = req.body.tasks_completed || req.body.Visit_Notes; const client_mood = req.body.client_mood || req.body.Client_Mood; const incident_reported = req.body.incident_reported || req.body.Incidents ? true : false; const incident_notes = req.body.incident_notes || req.body.Incidents; const operator = await getOperator(operator_id); const { data: client } = await supabase .from('clients') .select('id') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .eq('first_name', client_first_name) .eq('last_name', client_last_name) .single(); const summary = await generateWithClaude( `Write a brief 2-sentence professional care visit summary. Plain prose only — no markdown, no asterisks, no bold, no bullet points. PSW: ${psw_name}, Client: ${client_first_name} ${client_last_name} Date: ${visit_date}, Time: ${time_in} to ${time_out} Tasks: ${tasks_completed}, Mood: ${client_mood} Incident: ${incident_reported} ${incident_notes || ''}`, 'You write concise professional care visit summaries. Be factual and brief. Never use markdown, asterisks, bold, or any formatting — plain prose only.', buildNameMap(`${client_first_name} ${client_last_name}`, psw_name) ); const { data: visit, error } = await supabase.from('visits').insert({ operator_id, client_id: client?.id || null, psw_name, psw_email, visit_date, time_in, time_out, tasks_completed, client_mood, incident_reported: incident_reported === 'true' || incident_reported === true, incident_notes, visit_summary: summary }).select().single(); if (error) throw error; const hoursWorked = ((new Date(`1970-01-01T${time_out}`) - new Date(`1970-01-01T${time_in}`)) / 3600000).toFixed(2); const pswRate = operator?.psw_hourly_rate || 19; const invoiceRate = operator?.invoice_hourly_rate || 22; const pswCost = (hoursWorked * pswRate).toFixed(2); const invoiceTotal = (hoursWorked * invoiceRate).toFixed(2); const profit = (invoiceTotal - pswCost).toFixed(2); const incidentBool = incident_reported === 'true' || incident_reported === true; await sendEmail({ to: operator?.notification_email || process.env.GMAIL_USER, subject: `Visit Log — ${client_first_name} ${client_last_name} — ${visit_date}`, html: `
📋 New Visit Completed
PROXIMITY CARE SERVICES — PSW VISIT LOG
✓ AUTO-LOGGED TO SUPABASE
VISIT DETAILS
PSW${psw_name}
Client${client_first_name} ${client_last_name}
Date${visit_date}
Time In${time_in}
Time Out${time_out}
HOURS WORKED
${hoursWorked}
PSW COST
$${pswCost}
INVOICE TOTAL
$${invoiceTotal}
YOUR PROFIT
$${profit}
VISIT NOTES
${tasks_completed || 'No notes provided.'}
CARE SUMMARY
${summary}
CLIENT MOOD
Mood${client_mood || '—'}
Incidents${incidentBool ? `Yes — ${incident_notes || 'see notes'}` : 'None reported'}
proximitycares.ca
` }); res.json({ success: true, visit_id: visit.id, summary }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'Visit error', { error: String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); app.post('/webhook/lead', async (req, res) => { try { const { operator_id = 'proximity-care', lead_type = 'family', first_name, last_name, email, phone, city, care_needed_for, care_type_interest, urgency, source = 'lead_form', utm_source, utm_medium, utm_campaign, demo_mode = false, _hp = null // honeypot — bots fill it, humans don't } = req.body; // HONEYPOT — silent reject if filled if (_hp) return res.json({ success: true }); // Block security test submissions and script injection attempts // These come from watchdog scans, pen tests, and form abuse — must not generate real emails const _nameRaw = ((first_name || '') + ' ' + (last_name || '')).toLowerCase();     ` } }); function renderTemplate(str, vars) { let out = str; for (const [k, v] of Object.entries(vars || {})) { out = out.split(`{{${k}}}`).join(v == null ? '' : String(v)); } return out; } // POST /followup/run — Railway cron hits this every 5 minutes app.post('/followup/run', async (req, res) => { // Auth guard — Railway cron sends WATCHDOG_PIN in body if (req.body.pin && req.body.pin !== WATCHDOG_PIN) { return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid PIN' }); } const startedAt = new Date().toISOString(); let processed = 0; let sent = 0; const errors = []; try { const { data: rows, error } = await supabase .from('scheduled_emails') .select('*') .eq('sent', false) .lte('send_at', new Date().toISOString()) .limit(50); if (error) { log('error', 'S04 query error', { error: error.message || String(error), trace_id: req?._traceId }); return res.status(500).json({ ok: false, error: error.message, processed, sent, errors }); } for (const row of (rows || [])) { processed++; try { const tpl = FOLLOW_UP_TEMPLATES[row.template_key]; if (!tpl) { errors.push({ id: row.id, error: `unknown template_key: ${row.template_key}` }); await supabase .from('scheduled_emails') .update({ sent: true, sent_at: new Date().toISOString() }) .eq('id', row.id); continue; } const firstName = (row.recipient_name && row.recipient_name.split(' ')[0]) || 'there'; let metadata = {}; try { metadata = row.metadata ? JSON.parse(row.metadata) : {}; } catch(e) {} const vars = { name: firstName, operator_id: row.operator_id || 'your agency', agency_name: metadata.agency_name || row.operator_id || 'your agency', agency_phone: metadata.agency_phone || '647-382-8047', client_name: metadata.client_name || '', family_name: metadata.family_name || firstName, assigned_psw: metadata.assigned_psw || '', portal_url: metadata.portal_url || 'https://proximitycares.ca/family.html', portal_pin: metadata.portal_pin || '', psw_code: metadata.psw_code || '', pin: metadata.pin || '', invoice_total: metadata.invoice_total || '', invoice_id: metadata.invoice_id || '', builder_url: metadata.builder_url || 'https://proximitysystems.ca', owner_name: metadata.owner_name || firstName }; const subject = renderTemplate(tpl.subject, vars); const html = renderTemplate(tpl.html, vars); // ── OPTIMISTIC LOCK: mark sent BEFORE sending ── // This prevents the loop: if sendEmail() succeeds but the UPDATE below fails, // the row would stay sent=false and re-fire every 5 minutes. // By marking it first, a send failure becomes a missed email (recoverable) // not an infinite duplicate storm (not recoverable). const { error: lockErr } = await supabase .from('scheduled_emails') .update({ sent: true, sent_at: new Date().toISOString() }) .eq('id', row.id) .eq('sent', false); // only update if still false — concurrent safety if (lockErr) { log('warn', 'S04.lock.failed', { id: row.id, error: lockErr.message }); errors.push({ id: row.id, error: `lock failed: ${lockErr.message}` }); continue; // skip this row — will not send, avoids dupe } await sendEmail({ to: row.recipient_email, subject, html }); sent++; console.log(`S04: sent ${row.template_key} → ${row.recipient_email}`); } catch (e) { log('error', 'S04.send.failed', { email: row.recipient_email, error: e.message }); errors.push({ id: row.id, recipient: row.recipient_email, error: e.message }); // Row is already marked sent=true from optimistic lock above // Email failed to deliver but we do NOT reset sent=false — prevents loop } } console.log(`S04: run complete — processed:${processed} sent:${sent} errors:${errors.length}`); // Heartbeat: one row per run regardless of work-found — used by /system/run-tests cron audit try { await supabase.from('system_logs').insert({ operator_id: 'proximity-care', event_type: 'followup_run', event_source: '/followup/run', payload: { processed, sent, errors: errors.length }, status: 'complete', created_at: new Date().toISOString() }); } catch {} res.json({ ok: true, started_at: startedAt, processed, sent, errors }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'S04: fatal /followup/run error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ ok: false, error: err.message, processed, sent, errors }); } }); // GET /followup/health — Railway cron health check app.get('/followup/health', async (req, res) => { res.status(200).json({ status: 'ok', time: new Date().toISOString() }); }); // ── INVOICE PREVIEW — read-only, no emails, no DB write ──────────────────── // Returns visit count / hours / totals for a custom date range so HQ can // confirm before generating. Called from the invoice picker sheet in hq.html. app.post('/invoice/preview', async (req, res) => { try { const { client_name, psw_name, start_date, end_date, client_rate, psw_rate, operator_id } = req.body; if (!client_name || !psw_name || !start_date || !end_date) { return res.status(400).json({ error: 'client_name, psw_name, start_date, and end_date are all required' }); } if (start_date > end_date) { return res.status(400).json({ error: 'start_date must be on or before end_date' }); } const clientRate = parseFloat(client_rate) || 22; const pswRate = parseFloat(psw_rate) || 19; const opId = operator_id || 'proximity-care'; const { data: visits, error } = await supabase .from('visits') .select('id, visit_date, time_in, time_out, hours_worked, manual_hours_override') .eq('operator_id', opId) .eq('psw_name', psw_name) .gte('visit_date', start_date) .lte('visit_date', end_date) .order('visit_date', { ascending: true }); if (error) throw error; if (!visits || visits.length === 0) { return res.json({ visits_count: 0, total_hours: 0, client_total: 0, psw_total: 0, visit_dates: [] }); } // P4 — same joint-visit dedup as /invoice/generate const groups = {}; const order = []; visits.forEach(v => { const key = v.joint_visit_id || ('solo_' + v.id); if (!groups[key]) { groups[key] = []; order.push(key); } groups[key].push(v); }); const billingVisits = order.map(key => { const g = groups[key]; if (g.length === 1) return g[0]; return g.reduce((best, v) => { const vH = parseFloat(v.manual_hours_override ?? v.hours_worked ?? 0); const bH = parseFloat(best.manual_hours_override ?? best.hours_worked ?? 0); return vH > bH ? v : best; }, g[0]); }); const totalHours = billingVisits.reduce((sum, v) => sum + parseFloat(v.manual_hours_override ?? v.hours_worked ?? 0), 0); const roundedHours = Math.round(totalHours * 100) / 100; const clientTotal = Math.round(roundedHours * clientRate * 100) / 100; const pswTotal = Math.round(roundedHours * pswRate * 100) / 100; res.json({ visits_count: billingVisits.length, total_hours: roundedHours, client_total: clientTotal, psw_total: pswTotal, client_rate: clientRate, psw_rate: pswRate, visit_dates: visits.map(v => v.visit_date) }); } catch (err) { log('error', '/invoice/preview error', { error: err.message || String(err) }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message || 'Preview failed' }); } }); app.post('/invoice/generate', async (req, res) => { try { const { client_name, client_email, psw_name, psw_email, month, year, client_rate, psw_rate } = req.body; const clientRate = parseFloat(client_rate) || 22; const pswRate = parseFloat(psw_rate) || 19; const monthNames = ['January','February','March','April','May','June','July','August','September','October','November','December']; const monthNum = monthNames.indexOf(month) + 1; const startDate = req.body.start_date || `${year}-${String(monthNum).padStart(2,'0')}-01`; const endDate = req.body.end_date || new Date(parseInt(year), monthNum, 0).toISOString().slice(0, 10); // EC-5 — Duplicate invoice detection const { data: existingInvoice } = await supabase .from('invoices') .select('id, status, sent_at') .eq('operator_id', req.body.operator_id || 'proximity-care') .eq('client_name', client_name) .eq('month', month) .eq('year', parseInt(year)) .maybeSingle(); if (existingInvoice && !req.body.force_generate) { return res.status(409).json({ error: `Invoice already exists for ${client_name} — ${month} ${year}`, duplicate: true, existing_invoice_id: existingInvoice.id, existing_status: existingInvoice.status, sent_at: existingInvoice.sent_at, hint: 'Pass force_generate: true to regenerate and overwrite' }); } const invoiceOpId = req.body.operator_id || 'proximity-care'; const { data: visits, error } = await supabase .from('visits') .select('*') .eq('operator_id', invoiceOpId) .eq('psw_name', psw_name) .gte('visit_date', startDate) .lte('visit_date', endDate) .order('visit_date', { ascending: true }); if (error) throw error; if (!visits || visits.length === 0) { return res.status(404).json({ error: `No visits found for ${psw_name} in ${month} ${year}` }); } // EC-15 — Hospitalization cross-check ($9.7M NY OIG finding) // Flag visits where client was marked hospitalized during the visit period let hospitalizedVisits = 0; try { const { data: clientStatus } = await supabase .from('clients') .select('status, first_name, last_name') .eq('operator_id', req.body.operator_id || 'proximity-care') .ilike('first_name', client_name.split(' ')[0]) .maybeSingle(); if (clientStatus?.status === 'hospitalized') { hospitalizedVisits = visits.length; return res.status(409).json({ error: `${client_name} is currently marked as hospitalized. Billing for visits during hospitalization may constitute fraud. Resolve client status before generating invoice.`, hospitalized: true, hospitalized_visit_count: hospitalizedVisits, hint: 'Update client status to active before invoicing, or contact your compliance officer.' }); } } catch (ec15Err) { log('error', 'EC-15 hospitalization check error', { error: ec15Err.message || String(ec15Err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); } // P4 — Joint visit billing: group by joint_visit_id, take max hours per group // Prevents double-billing when 2 PSWs both log hours for the same visit const billingVisits = (() => { const groups = {}; const order = []; visits.forEach(v => { const key = v.joint_visit_id || ('solo_' + v.id); if (!groups[key]) { groups[key] = []; order.push(key); } groups[key].push(v); }); return order.map(key => { const g = groups[key]; if (g.length === 1) return g[0]; // Joint visit — use the row with max billable hours (prefer manual_hours_override over generated hours_worked) return g.reduce((best, v) => { const vH = parseFloat(v.manual_hours_override ?? v.hours_worked ?? 0); const bH = parseFloat(best.manual_hours_override ?? best.hours_worked ?? 0); return vH > bH ? v : best; }, g[0]); }); })(); // BILLING: always prefer manual_hours_override — hours_worked is GENERATED and ignores HQ edits const totalHours = billingVisits.reduce((sum, v) => sum + parseFloat(v.manual_hours_override ?? v.hours_worked ?? 0), 0); const roundedHours = Math.round(totalHours * 100) / 100; const clientTotal = Math.round(roundedHours * clientRate * 100) / 100; const pswTotal = Math.round(roundedHours * pswRate * 100) / 100; const profit = Math.round((clientTotal - pswTotal) * 100) / 100; const formatTime = (t) => t ? String(t).slice(0,5) : ''; const formatDate = (d) => { if (!d) return ''; const date = new Date(d + 'T12:00:00'); return date.toLocaleDateString('en-CA', { weekday:'short', month:'short', day:'numeric' }); }; const visitRowsClient = visits.map(v => ` ${formatDate(v.visit_date)} ${formatTime(v.time_in)} ${formatTime(v.time_out)} ${parseFloat(v.manual_hours_override ?? v.hours_worked ?? 0).toFixed(2)} `).join(''); const visitRowsPsw = visits.map(v => ` ${formatDate(v.visit_date)} ${formatTime(v.time_in)} ${formatTime(v.time_out)} ${parseFloat(v.manual_hours_override ?? v.hours_worked ?? 0).toFixed(2)} `).join(''); const clientFirstName = client_name.split(' ')[0]; const pswFirstName = psw_name.split(' ')[0]; // Lookup client record for invoice PDF — address, phone, email + greeting name // operator_id scoped — prevents cross-tenant match; maybeSingle never throws on no-match let familyGreetingName = clientFirstName; let familyContactFullName = null; let clientAddress = ''; let clientPhone = ''; let clientRecEmail = ''; try { const clientFullSplit = client_name.trim().split(/\s+/); const lookupFirst = clientFullSplit[0]; const lookupLast = clientFullSplit.slice(1).join(' '); const lookupOperatorId = req.body.operator_id || 'proximity-care'; const { data: clientRec } = await supabase.from('clients') .select('family_contact_name, first_name, address, phone, email, family_email') .eq('operator_id', lookupOperatorId) .eq('first_name', lookupFirst) .eq('last_name', lookupLast) .maybeSingle(); if (clientRec?.family_contact_name) { familyGreetingName = clientRec.family_contact_name.split(' ')[0]; familyContactFullName = clientRec.family_contact_name; } else if (clientRec?.first_name) { familyGreetingName = clientRec.first_name; } if (clientRec?.address) clientAddress = clientRec.address; if (clientRec?.phone) clientPhone = clientRec.phone; if (clientRec?.email || clientRec?.family_email) clientRecEmail = clientRec.family_email || clientRec.email || ''; } catch(e) { /* retain fallbacks */ } const visitNotes = visits.map(v => v.visit_notes || v.tasks_completed || '').filter(Boolean).join(' '); const moodList = visits.map(v => v.client_mood || '').filter(Boolean); const incidents = visits.map(v => v.incident_notes || '').filter(Boolean); // PHIPA: build comprehensive name map BEFORE injecting visitNotes into prompt // visitNotes is free-text typed by PSWs and can contain any family member name (e.g. "Connie came by") const invoiceNames = buildNameMap(client_name, psw_name); // Add family contact name to map so names like "Connie" in visit notes get replaced if (familyContactFullName) { invoiceNames.push({ real: familyContactFullName, code: 'FAMILY-1' }); } // Pre-scrub visitNotes through PHIPA anonymizer before embedding in prompt const { anonymized: safeVisitNotes } = phipaAnonymize(visitNotes.slice(0, 1000), invoiceNames); const summaryPrompt = `Write a warm monthly care summary for a family. Plain English. Grade 5 reading level. Casual and human. 3 to 4 sentences max. No bullet points. No medical language. Just tell them how their loved one did this month like a friend would. IMPORTANT: Do not reproduce any names from the visit notes — refer to individuals only by their assigned codes (CLIENT-A, PSW-1, FAMILY-1) or generic terms like "your loved one."\n\nPSW name: PSW-1\nClient name: CLIENT-A\nMonth: ${month} ${year}\nTotal visits: ${visits.length}\nTotal hours: ${roundedHours}\nVisit notes: ${safeVisitNotes}\nMoods recorded: ${moodList.join(', ')}\nIncidents: ${incidents.length > 0 ? incidents.join(', ') : 'none'}`; const { anonymized: anonPrompt, deAnonymize: deAnonInvoice } = phipaAnonymize(summaryPrompt, invoiceNames); const summaryResponse = await anthropic.messages.create({ model: 'claude-sonnet-4-20250514', max_tokens: 200, messages: [{ role: 'user', content: anonPrompt }] }); const careSummary = deAnonInvoice(summaryResponse.content[0].text); const clientHtml = `

    Proximity Care Services

    Monthly Invoice · ${month} ${year}

    Hi ${familyGreetingName},

    I hope you're doing well. Please find below the ${month} ${year} in-home care summary for ${clientFirstName} with ${pswFirstName}.

    ${visitRowsClient}
    Date Time In Time Out Hours
    Total Hours ${roundedHours.toFixed(2)}

    How ${clientFirstName} Is Doing

    ${careSummary}

    Invoice Summary

    ${roundedHours.toFixed(2)} hours × $${clientRate}/hr = $${clientTotal.toFixed(2)}

    Payment Instructions

    E-transfer to: lancesalazar56@yahoo.ca

    As always, thank you for your continued trust. I hope ${pswFirstName} has been doing a great job keeping everything steady and consistent for ${clientFirstName}.

    If you have any questions or need anything for your records, please don't hesitate to reach out.

    Warm regards,

    Lance Salazar

    Founder and Operator · Proximity Care Services Inc.

    "The Right Care, Right at Home"

    healthcareproximity@gmail.com · www.proximitycares.ca

    Proximity Care Services Inc. · Mississauga, Ontario · 647-382-8047

    `; // ── CLIENT INVOICE PDF — Professional layout ───────────────────────────── const pdfBufferClient = await new Promise((resolve, reject) => { const doc = new PDFDocument({ margin: 0, size: 'A4' }); const chunks = []; doc.on('data', c => chunks.push(c)); doc.on('end', () => resolve(Buffer.concat(chunks))); doc.on('error', reject); const W = doc.page.width; // 595pt const H = doc.page.height; // 842pt const L = 52, R = W - 52; // left/right margin x-coords const CW = R - L; // content width // ── COLOUR PALETTE ────────────────────────────────────────────────────── const INK = '#0d1f2d'; // almost-black for body text const TEAL = '#1a6b5a'; // Proximity green const TEAL_LT = '#eaf4f1'; // light teal fill const GOLD = '#b87010'; // accent const MUTED = '#6b7280'; // labels / secondary text const BORDER = '#dde3e7'; // table rule const STRIPE = '#f7faf9'; // alt row fill const WHITE = '#ffffff'; // ── HELPER FUNCTIONS ──────────────────────────────────────────────────── const line = (x1, y1, x2, y2, color = BORDER, w = 0.5) => doc.moveTo(x1, y1).lineTo(x2, y2).strokeColor(color).lineWidth(w).stroke(); const label = (text, x, y, opts = {}) => doc.fillColor(opts.color || MUTED).font('Helvetica').fontSize(opts.size || 7.5) .text(text, x, y, opts); const body = (text, x, y, opts = {}) => doc.fillColor(opts.color || INK).font(opts.bold ? 'Helvetica-Bold' : 'Helvetica') .fontSize(opts.size || 9.5).text(text, x, y, opts); // ── SECTION 1: HEADER BAND ────────────────────────────────────────────── // Full-width teal band doc.rect(0, 0, W, 72).fill(TEAL); ty += 17; }); // Total hours row doc.rect(L, ty, CW, 24).fill(TEAL_LT); line(L, ty, R, ty, TEAL, 0.8); doc.fillColor(INK).font('Helvetica-Bold').fontSize(9) .text('TOTAL HOURS', cDate + 6, ty + 7); doc.fillColor(TEAL).fontSize(11) .text(roundedHours.toFixed(2), cHrs - cHrsW, ty + 6, { align: 'right', width: cHrsW }); We are honoured to support your family.', L, footY + 24, { align: 'center', width: CW } ); doc.end(); }); // Save client invoice PDF to Supabase Storage const pdfFilename = `invoices/${client_name.replace(/\s/g,'-')}-${month}-${year}.pdf`; // S04: Schedule invoice follow-up sequence Day 3, 7, 14 if client email exists if (client_email) { try { const now = Date.now(); const dayMs = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000; const invoiceTotal = `$${clientTotal.toFixed(2)}`; } } log('info', 'invoice.sent', { operator_id: invoiceOpId, client_name, month, year, total: clientTotal }); res.json({ success: true, total_hours: roundedHours, client_total: clientTotal, psw_total: pswTotal, profit, visits_count: visits.length }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'Invoice generate error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ── /paystub/generate — Send PSW pay stub independently ─────────────────── // Separate from /invoice/generate. Uses start_date/end_date from the picker. // Authoritative hours: manual_hours_override ?? hours_worked (never raw GPS only). app.post('/paystub/generate', async (req, res) => { try { const { operator_id, psw_name, psw_email, start_date, end_date, psw_rate, client_name, month, year, force_send } = req.body; if (!operator_id || !psw_name || !start_date || !end_date) { return res.status(400).json({ error: 'operator_id, psw_name, start_date, end_date required' }); } const opId = operator_id; const pswRate = parseFloat(psw_rate) || 19; // Lookup PSW record — column is full_name, not name const { data: pswRec } = await supabase.from('psws') .select('full_name, email, psw_rate, phone, address') .eq('operator_id', opId) .eq('full_name', psw_name) .maybeSingle(); const sendTo = psw_email || pswRec?.email || ''; if (!sendTo) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No email on file for PSW and none provided' }); const effectivePswRate = pswRate || parseFloat(pswRec?.psw_rate) || 19; // Query visits — AUTHORITATIVE: manual_hours_override ?? hours_worked const { data: visits, error: vErr } = await supabase .from('visits') .select('id, visit_date, time_in, time_out, hours_worked, manual_hours_override, client_name, status') .eq('operator_id', opId) .eq('psw_name', psw_name) .gte('visit_date', start_date) .lte('visit_date', end_date) .order('visit_date', { ascending: true }); if (vErr) throw vErr; if (!visits || visits.length === 0) { return res.status(404).json({ error: `No visits found for ${psw_name} between ${start_date} and ${end_date}` }); } const totalHours = visits.reduce((s, v) => s + parseFloat(v.manual_hours_override ?? v.hours_worked ?? 0), 0); const roundedHours = Math.round(totalHours * 100) / 100; const pswTotal = Math.round(roundedHours * effectivePswRate * 100) / 100; const monthNames = ['January','February','March','April','May','June','July','August','September','October','November','December']; const endDt = new Date(end_date + 'T12:00:00'); const monthStr = month || monthNames[endDt.getMonth()]; const yearStr = year || endDt.getFullYear(); const periodStr = `${start_date} to ${end_date}`; const fmtTime = t => t ? String(t).slice(0, 5) : '—'; const fmtDate = d => { if (!d) return '—'; return new Date(d + 'T12:00:00').toLocaleDateString('en-CA', { weekday: 'short', month: 'short', day: 'numeric' }); }; const dayLabels = ['Sun','Mon','Tue','Wed','Thu','Fri','Sat']; // Build visit rows HTML for email const visitRowsHtml = visits.map((v, i) => { const hrs = parseFloat(v.manual_hours_override ?? v.hours_worked ?? 0).toFixed(2); const bg = i % 2 === 0 ? 'rgba(61,122,138,0.04)' : 'transparent'; return ` ${fmtDate(v.visit_date)} ${fmtTime(v.time_in)} ${fmtTime(v.time_out)} ${hrs} `; }).join(''); const pswFirstName = psw_name.split(' ')[0]; const emailHtml = `

    Proximity Care Services

    Pay Statement · ${monthStr} ${yearStr}

    Hi ${pswFirstName},

    Here is your pay statement for the period ${periodStr}. All visit hours reflect any corrections made by HQ.

    ${visitRowsHtml}
    Date Time In Time Out Hours
    Total Hours ${roundedHours.toFixed(2)}

    Your Pay

    ${roundedHours.toFixed(2)} hrs × $${effectivePswRate}/hr = $${pswTotal.toFixed(2)}

    Payment

    E-transfer · Lance will send by the 5th of next month

    Thank you for your great work this period, ${pswFirstName}. If anything looks off, reply to this email or call Lance at 647-382-8047.

    Lance Salazar
    Proximity Care Services · 647-382-8047

    Proximity Care Services Inc. · Mississauga, Ontario

    `; // ── PSW PAY STUB PDF ───────────────────────────────────────────────────── const pdfBuffer = await new Promise((resolve, reject) => { const doc = new PDFDocument({ margin: 0, size: 'A4' }); const chunks = []; doc.on('data', c => chunks.push(c)); doc.on('end', () => resolve(Buffer.concat(chunks))); doc.on('error', reject); const W = doc.page.width, H = doc.page.height; const L = 48, R = W - 48, CW = R - L; const DARK = '#0d1117', TEAL = '#3d8a7a', GOLD = '#c8a96e'; const MUTED = 'rgba(232,220,200,0.45)', DIM = 'rgba(232,220,200,0.3)'; const TEAL2 = '#5aada0', CREAM = '#e8dcc8', GREY = '#a8a098'; // Header band doc.rect(0, 0, W, 96).fill(DARK); Called from HQ Onboard tab. // ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── app.post('/psw/activate', async (req, res) => { try { const { operator_id, psw_name, psw_email, psw_phone, psw_pin } = req.body; if (!psw_name) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'PSW name is required' }); if (!psw_email) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'PSW email is required' }); const opId = operator_id || 'proximity-care'; const pin = psw_pin || String(Math.floor(1000 + Math.random() * 9000)); // Generate human-readable PSW code (PC-P001, HG-P001 etc) const prefix = opId.replace(/-/g,'').toUpperCase().slice(0,2); const { count: pswCount } = await supabase.from('psws').select('*', { count: 'exact', head: true }).eq('operator_id', opId); const psw_code = `${prefix}-P${String((pswCount||0)+1).padStart(3,'0')}`; // Get applicant record if exists (to pull extended fields) const { data: applicantRec } = await supabase.from('psw_applicants') .select('*').eq('operator_id', opId) .or(`email.eq.${psw_email},phone.eq.${psw_phone||''}`) .order('created_at', { ascending: false }).limit(1).maybeSingle(); // Upsert into psws table (handles both new activation and reactivation) const { data: psw, error: upsertErr } = await supabase .from('psws') .upsert( { operator_id: opId, full_name: psw_name, email: psw_email, phone: psw_phone || null, pin, status: 'active', psw_code, first_name: req.body.first_name || psw_name.split(' ')[0], last_name: req.body.last_name || psw_name.split(' ').slice(1).join(' ') || null, city: req.body.city || applicantRec?.city || null, languages: req.body.languages || applicantRec?.languages || null, vehicle: req.body.vehicle || applicantRec?.vehicle || null, years_experience: applicantRec?.years_experience || null, care_types: applicantRec?.certifications || null, availability_days: applicantRec?.availability ? applicantRec.message.split('Transfers:')[1]?.trim().split('|')[0]?.trim() : null, // Copy documents if applicant had them psw_cert_url: applicantRec?.psw_cert_url || null, psw_cert_expiry: applicantRec?.psw_cert_expiry || null, psw_cert_status: applicantRec?.psw_cert_url ?     From the portal you can log visits, see your schedule, view client care plans, and message me directly. Everything in one place on your phone.

} catch (err) { log('error', 'hq.psw.approve.error', { error: err.message }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // PSW PIN cache — avoids redundant Supabase queries at 50+ PSW scale // Key: `${operator_id}:${psw_name}`, Value: { pins: {pin, psw_pin}, expires: timestamp } const _pswPinCache = new Map(); const PSW_CACHE_TTL = 15 * 60 * 1000; // 15 minutes async function verifyPSW(psw_name, pin, operator_id = 'proximity-care') { if (!psw_name || !pin) return false; const trimmedName = psw_name.trim(); // trim whitespace — common source of silent 401s const cacheKey = `${operator_id}:${trimmedName}`; const now = Date.now(); // Check cache first const cached = _pswPinCache.get(cacheKey); if (cached && cached.expires > now) { if (cached.psw_pin != null && cached.psw_pin !== '') return String(cached.psw_pin) === String(pin); return String(cached.pin) === String(pin); } // Cache miss — hit Supabase const { data, error } = await supabase .from('psws') .select('pin, psw_pin') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .eq('full_name', trimmedName) .ilike('status', 'active') // case-insensitive status check .maybeSingle(); if (error || !data) { // Fallback: try without psw_pin in case column doesn't exist on this operator's schema const { data: d2, error: e2 } = await supabase .from('psws').select('pin') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .eq('full_name', trimmedName) .ilike('status', 'active') .maybeSingle(); if (e2 || !d2) return false; _pswPinCache.set(cacheKey, { pin: d2.pin, psw_pin: null, expires: now + PSW_CACHE_TTL }); return String(d2.pin) === String(pin); // String() coercion — handles numeric PIN in DB } // Store in cache _pswPinCache.set(cacheKey, { pin: data.pin, psw_pin: data.psw_pin, expires: now + PSW_CACHE_TTL }); // Check psw_pin (individual) first, fall back to pin (global) for backward compat // Empty string psw_pin treated as "no individual pin" — prevents false 0000 match if (data.psw_pin != null && data.psw_pin !== '') return String(data.psw_pin) === String(pin); return String(data.pin) === String(pin); // String() coercion — handles numeric PIN in DB } // Invalidate cache for a PSW when their PIN changes (call after any PIN update) function invalidatePSWCache(psw_name, operator_id = 'proximity-care') { _pswPinCache.delete(`${operator_id}:${psw_name}`); } async function getPSWEmail(psw_name) { if (!psw_name) return null; const { data, error } = await supabase .from('psws') .select('email') .eq('operator_id', 'proximity-care') .eq('full_name', psw_name) .single(); if (error || !data) return null; return data.email || null; } // POST /psw/message-hq — PSW sends a message to HQ operator // Stores in psw_notes with direction='psw_to_hq'. } }); // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // B. /webhook/purchase — logs all purchases to Supabase // Handles WooCommerce, Thrivecart, Stripe, manual entry // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ app.post('/webhook/purchase', async (req, res) => { try { const body = req.body; let operator_id, buyer_name, buyer_email, buyer_phone, product_name, product_label, amount_usd, source, source_order_id; if (body.billing && body.line_items) { source = 'woocommerce'; source_order_id = String(body.id || ''); amount_usd = parseFloat(body.total || 0); product_label = 'book'; operator_id = 'lcm-experts'; } else if (body.thrivecart || body.event) { source = 'thrivecart'; const customer = body.customer || {}; source_order_id = String(body.order_id || ''); buyer_name = `${customer.first_name || ''} ${customer.last_name || ''}`.trim(); buyer_email = customer.email || ''; buyer_phone = customer.phone || ''; product_name = body.product?.name || 'Course'; amount_usd = parseFloat(body.order?.total || 0); product_label = 'course'; operator_id = 'lcm-experts'; } else if (body.type?.startsWith('payment_intent') || body.object === 'checkout.session') { source = 'stripe'; const session = body.data?.object || body; source_order_id = session.id || ''; buyer_email = session.customer_details?.email || ''; buyer_name = session.customer_details?.name || ''; buyer_phone = session.customer_details?.phone || ''; product_name = session.metadata?.product_name || 'Stripe Purchase'; amount_usd = (session.amount_total || 0) / 100; product_label = session.metadata?.product_label || 'other'; operator_id = session.metadata?.operator_id || 'proximity-care'; } else { source = 'manual'; operator_id = body.operator_id || 'proximity-care'; buyer_name = body.buyer_name || ''; buyer_email = body.buyer_email || ''; buyer_phone = body.buyer_phone || ''; product_name = body.product_name || ''; product_label = body.product_label || 'other'; amount_usd = parseFloat(body.amount_usd || 0); source_order_id = body.source_order_id || ''; } if (!buyer_email || !product_name) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Missing buyer_email or product_name' }); const { data, error } = await supabase.from('purchases').insert({ operator_id, buyer_name, buyer_email, buyer_phone, product_name, product_label, amount_usd, source, source_order_id, status: 'completed' }).select().single(); } catch {} res.json({ success: true, purchase: data }); } catch (err) { res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // C. HQ DASHBOARD DATA ENDPOINTS // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // POST /hq/auth — verify HQ PIN and issue session token // Body: { operator_id, pin } // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ app.post('/hq/auth', hqPinLimiter, async (req, res) => { try { const { operator_id, pin } = req.body; if (!operator_id || !pin) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'operator_id and pin required' }); const { data: config } = await supabase.from('operator_config') .select('hq_pin, active, agency_name').eq('operator_id', operator_id).maybeSingle(); if (!config) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Operator not found' }); if (!config.active) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Operator account inactive' }); if (String(config.hq_pin) !== String(pin)) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid PIN' }); const token = await createHQSession(operator_id); log('info', 'hq.auth.success', { operator_id }); auditLog(req, { action:'login', entity_type:'hq_session', entity_id:operator_id, actor_type:'hq', actor_name:operator_id, changes:{ ip:req.ip } }); res.json({ success: true, token, operator_id, agency_name: config.agency_name || operator_id }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'hq.auth.error', { error: err.message || String(err) }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // POST /hq/logout — invalidate session token // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ app.post('/hq/logout', async (req, res) => { const token = req.headers['x-hq-token']; if (token) await supabase.from('hq_sessions').delete().eq('token', token); res.json({ success: true }); }); // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // POST /operator/onboard-verify — onboard.html PIN auth (stateless) // Body: { operator_id, hq_pin } // Returns: { success, agency_name, owner_name, onboarding_step } // Rate limited via hqPinLimiter (10/hr per IP) // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ app.post('/operator/onboard-verify', hqPinLimiter, async (req, res) => { try { const { operator_id, hq_pin } = req.body; if (!operator_id || !hq_pin) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'operator_id and hq_pin required' }); const { data: op, error } = await supabase .from('operator_config') .select('agency_name, owner_name, hq_pin, active, onboarding_step') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .maybeSingle(); log('info', 'onboard.verify.success', { operator_id }); res.json({ success: true, agency_name: op.agency_name || operator_id, owner_name: op.owner_name || '', onboarding_step: op.onboarding_step || 0 }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'onboard.verify.error', { error: err.message || String(err) }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); app.get('/hq/overview', async (req, res) => { try { const operator_id = req.query.operator_id || 'proximity-care'; const [leadsResult, clientsResult, bookingsResult, purchasesResult, messagesResult, logsResult, pswsResult, opConfigResult, revenueResult] = await Promise.all([ supabase.from('leads').select('id,first_name,last_name,email,phone,status,care_type_interest,source,created_at').eq('operator_id', operator_id).order('created_at', { ascending: false }).limit(50), supabase.from('clients').select('id,first_name,last_name,email,phone,portal_slug,portal_pin,status,assigned_psw,client_rate,psw_rate,family_email,family_contact_name,start_date,care_notes,care_type,mobility_level,cognitive_status,medications,emergency_contact_1_name,emergency_contact_1_phone,emergency_contact_1_relation,emergency_contact_2_name,emergency_contact_2_phone,emergency_contact_2_relation,created_at,consent_given,consent_date,consent_version,referral_source,date_of_birth,address,physician_name,physician_phone,allergies,dnr_status,poa_name,poa_phone,home_access_instructions,insurance_provider,insurance_policy,service_agreement_url,assessment_date,reassessment_due,client_photo_url,requires_two_psw,two_psw_reason').eq('operator_id', operator_id).eq('status', 'active').order('created_at', { ascending: false }), supabase.from('bookings').select('*').eq('operator_id', operator_id).gte('scheduled_date', (() => { const d = new Date(); d.setDate(d.getDate() - 30); return d.toLocaleDateString('en-CA', { timeZone: 'America/Toronto' }); })()).order('scheduled_date', { ascending: true }), supabase.from('purchases').select('*').eq('operator_id', operator_id).order('purchased_at', { ascending: false }).limit(20), supabase.from('system_logs').select('*').eq('operator_id', operator_id).eq('event_type', 'family_message').order('created_at', { ascending: false }).limit(10), supabase.from('system_logs').select('event_type,event_source,contact_name,contact_email,status,created_at').eq('operator_id', operator_id).order('created_at', { ascending: false }).limit(20), supabase.from('psws').select('id,full_name,email,phone,pin,status,psw_rate,psw_code,psw_cert_expiry,probation_end,availability_days,availability_shifts,created_at,nacc_number,nacc_expiry,hscpoa_number,hscpoa_status,vsc_date,vsc_expiry,tb_test_date,covid_vax_status,address,emergency_contact,employment_agreement_url,start_date,police_check_expiry,cpr_cert_expiry,first_aid_expiry,psw_cert_url,police_check_url,cpr_cert_url,first_aid_url').eq('operator_id', operator_id).order('full_name', { ascending: true }), supabase.from('operator_config').select('onboarding_step,onboarding_completed_at').eq('operator_id', operator_id).maybeSingle(), supabase.from('invoices').select('client_total, psw_total').eq('operator_id', operator_id).gte('sent_at', (() => { const n = new Date(); return new Date(n.getFullYear(), n.getMonth(), 1).toISOString(); })()).lte('sent_at', (() => { const n = new Date(); return new Date(n.getFullYear(), n.getMonth()+1, 0, 23, 59, 59).toISOString(); })()) ]); res.json({ success: true, operator_id, leads: leadsResult.data || [], clients: clientsResult.data || [], bookings: bookingsResult.data || [], purchases: purchasesResult.data || [], messages: messagesResult.data || [], recent_activity: logsResult.data || [], psws: pswsResult.data || [], onboarding_step: opConfigResult.data?.onboarding_step ?? 0, onboarding_completed_at: opConfigResult.data?.onboarding_completed_at ?? null, counts: { leads: leadsResult.data?.length || 0, clients: clientsResult.data?.length || 0, bookings_upcoming: bookingsResult.data?.length || 0, purchases_total: purchasesResult.data?.length || 0, revenue_month: (revenueResult?.data || []).reduce((s, r) => s + (parseFloat(r.client_total) || 0), 0), psw_cost_month: (revenueResult?.data || []).reduce((s, r) => s + (parseFloat(r.psw_total) || 0), 0), margin_month: (revenueResult?.data || []).reduce((s, r) => s + ((parseFloat(r.client_total)||0) - (parseFloat(r.psw_total)||0)), 0) } }); } catch (err) { res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // GET /hq/suggest-psw — S35 — Scheduling AI: score and rank PSWs for a given client + date // Scoring: visit history (0-50pts) + avg rating (0-30pts) + continuity bonus (+15) + day avail (+5) // Hard blocks: time-off on date, existing booking on date app.get('/hq/suggest-psw', async (req, res) => { try { const { operator_id, client_name, date } = req.query; if (!operator_id || !client_name || !date) { return res.status(400).json({ error: 'operator_id, client_name, and date are required' }); } const dayOfWeek = new Date(date + 'T12:00:00').toLocaleDateString('en-CA', { timeZone: 'America/Toronto', weekday: 'long' }); // Fetch all active PSWs for this operator const { data: psws } = await supabase.from('psws') .select('id, full_name, availability_days, availability_shifts, status') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .eq('status', 'active'); if (!psws || !psws.length) return res.json({ top_suggestions: [], blocked_psws: [], assigned_psw: null }); // Fetch visit history for this client (last 90 days) — score visit count + avg rating const ninetyAgo = new Date(); ninetyAgo.setDate(ninetyAgo.getDate() - 90); const { data: visits } = await supabase.from('visits') .select('psw_name, satisfaction_rating, visit_date') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .eq('client_name', client_name) .in('status', ['complete', 'completed']) .gte('visit_date', ninetyAgo.toLocaleDateString('en-CA', { timeZone: 'America/Toronto' })); // Fetch existing bookings on this date — hard block const { data: bookingsOnDate } = await supabase.from('bookings') .select('assigned_to') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .eq('scheduled_date', date) .not('status', 'eq', 'cancelled'); const bookedPSWs = new Set((bookingsOnDate || []).map(b => b.assigned_to).filter(Boolean)); // Fetch time-off blocks covering this date — hard block const { data: timeOff } = await supabase.from('psw_time_off') .select('psw_name, type, note') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .lte('from_date', date) .gte('to_date', date); const timeOffMap = {}; (timeOff || []).forEach(t => { timeOffMap[t.psw_name] = t; }); // Fetch currently assigned PSW for this client — split name and match by parts const nameParts = client_name.trim().split(' '); const _cfirst = nameParts[0] || ''; const _clast = nameParts.slice(1).join(' ') || ''; let _cq = supabase.from('clients').select('assigned_psw').eq('operator_id', operator_id); if (_cfirst) _cq = _cq.ilike('first_name', _cfirst); if (_clast) _cq = _cq.ilike('last_name', _clast); const { data: clientRec } = await _cq.maybeSingle(); const assignedPSW = clientRec?.assigned_psw || null; // Build per-PSW visit stats from history const statsByPSW = {}; (visits || []).forEach(v => { if (!statsByPSW[v.psw_name]) statsByPSW[v.psw_name] = { count: 0, ratingSum: 0, ratedCount: 0 }; statsByPSW[v.psw_name].count++; if (v.satisfaction_rating) { statsByPSW[v.psw_name].ratingSum += v.satisfaction_rating; statsByPSW[v.psw_name].ratedCount++; } }); const suggestions = []; const blocked = []; for (const psw of psws) { const name = psw.full_name; // Hard block: time-off if (timeOffMap[name]) { const t = timeOffMap[name]; blocked.push({ psw_name: name, block_reason: `${t.type === 'vacation' ? 'On vacation' : t.type === 'sick' ? 'Sick leave' : 'Time off'}${t.note ? ': ' + t.note : ''}` }); continue; } // Hard block: already booked that day (different client) if (bookedPSWs.has(name)) { blocked.push({ psw_name: name, block_reason: 'Already scheduled on this date' }); continue; } const stats = statsByPSW[name] || { count: 0, ratingSum: 0, ratedCount: 0 }; const avgRating = stats.ratedCount > 0 ? stats.ratingSum / stats.ratedCount : 0; // Score const visitScore = Math.min(50, stats.count * 5); // 0-50: 10 visits = max const ratingScore = avgRating > 0 ? Math.round((avgRating / 5) * 30) : 0; // 0-30 const continuity = name === assignedPSW ? 15 : 0; const availDays = (psw.availability_days || '').toLowerCase(); const dayAvail = availDays.includes(dayOfWeek.toLowerCase().slice(0, 3)) || availDays.includes('all') || availDays === '' ? 5 : 0; const score = visitScore + ratingScore + continuity + dayAvail; // Human-readable reason const parts = []; if (stats.count > 0) parts.push(`${stats.count} visit${stats.count !== 1 ? 's' : ''}`); if (avgRating > 0) parts.push(`${avgRating.toFixed(1)}★`); if (continuity) parts.push('assigned PSW'); if (dayAvail) parts.push('available ' + dayOfWeek); const reason = parts.length ? parts.join(' · ') : 'No prior history'; suggestions.push({ psw_name: name, score, visit_count: stats.count, avg_rating: avgRating > 0 ? Math.round(avgRating * 10) / 10 : null, reason }); } suggestions.sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score); res.json({ success: true, top_suggestions: suggestions.slice(0, 5), blocked_psws: blocked, assigned_psw: assignedPSW, date, day_of_week: dayOfWeek }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'hq/suggest-psw error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // POST /hq/onboarding-step — BUILD 31 — advance operator onboarding checklist app.post('/hq/onboarding-step', async (req, res) => { try { const { operator_id, step } = req.body; if (!operator_id || step === undefined) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Missing operator_id or step' }); const stepNum = parseInt(step); const updates = { onboarding_step: stepNum }; if (stepNum >= 6) updates.onboarding_completed_at = new Date().toISOString(); const { error } = await supabase.from('operator_config').update(updates).eq('operator_id', operator_id); if (error) throw error; res.json({ success: true, onboarding_step: stepNum }); } catch (err) { res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); app.post('/hq/lead-status', async (req, res) => { try { const { lead_id, id, status, operator_id } = req.body; const lid = lead_id || id; if (!lid || !status) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Missing id or status' }); const validStatuses = ['new','cold','contacted','demo','call','closed','converted','dead','booked']; if (!validStatuses.includes(status)) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid status' }); const { error } = await supabase.from('leads').update({ status, updated_at: new Date().toISOString() }).eq('id', lid); if (error) throw error; if (status === 'converted') { const { data: lead } = await supabase.from('leads').select('email').eq('id', lid).single(); if (lead?.email) { await supabase.from('onboarding_sequences') .update({ converted: true, converted_at: new Date().toISOString(), status: 'completed', updated_at: new Date().toISOString() }) .eq('operator_id', operator_id || 'proximity-care').eq('contact_email', lead.email).eq('sequence_type', 'lead'); } } res.json({ success: true }); } catch (err) { res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); app.patch('/hq/lead-status', async (req, res) => { try { const { lead_id, id, status, operator_id } = req.body; const lid = lead_id || id; if (!lid || !status) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Missing id or status' }); const validStatuses = ['new','cold','contacted','demo','call','closed','converted','dead','booked']; if (!validStatuses.includes(status)) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid status' }); const { error } = await supabase.from('leads').update({ status, updated_at: new Date().toISOString() }).eq('id', lid); } }); // GET /hq/branding — WHITE LABEL — returns operator branding for portal injection app.get('/hq/branding', async (req, res) => { try { const { operator_id } = req.query; if (!operator_id) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'operator_id required' }); Please log in.' }); const { operator_id, client_name, client_email, client_phone, booking_type, scheduled_date, scheduled_time, duration_minutes, assigned_to, location, notes, series_id, joint_booking_id } = req.body; if (!operator_id || !client_name || !scheduled_date || !scheduled_time || !booking_type) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Missing required fields' }); // Operator isolation — token must belong to the operator being written to if (operator_id !== _bookingAuth) return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Token does not match operator.' }); // Build 18 — Conflict detection: check if assigned PSW already has a booking within ±30min if (assigned_to && scheduled_date && scheduled_time) { const [h, m] = scheduled_time.split(':').map(Number); const slotMins = h * 60 + m; const { data: existingBookings } = await supabase .from('bookings') .select('id, client_name, scheduled_time, duration_minutes') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .eq('assigned_to', assigned_to) .eq('scheduled_date', scheduled_date) .neq('status', 'cancelled') .is('deleted_at', null); if (existingBookings && existingBookings.length > 0) { for (const b of existingBookings) { const [bh, bm] = (b.scheduled_time || '00:00').split(':').map(Number); const bSlotMins = bh * 60 + bm; const bDuration = b.duration_minutes || 60; const newDuration = duration_minutes || 60; const overlap = slotMins < bSlotMins + bDuration && slotMins + newDuration > bSlotMins; if (overlap) { return res.status(409).json({ error: 'Scheduling conflict', conflict: { psw: assigned_to, existing_client: b.client_name, existing_time: b.scheduled_time, existing_duration: bDuration }, message: `${assigned_to} is already booked for ${b.client_name} at ${b.scheduled_time} on ${scheduled_date}` }); } } } } const { data, error } = await supabase.from('bookings').insert({ operator_id, client_name, client_email, client_phone, booking_type, scheduled_date, scheduled_time, duration_minutes: duration_minutes || 60, assigned_to, location, notes, status: 'scheduled', series_id: series_id || null, joint_booking_id: joint_booking_id || null }).select().single();     Proximity Care

    New Shift

    Hi ${pswFirst},

    A new shift has been assigned to you:

    Client: ${client_name}

    Date: ${scheduled_date}

    ${scheduled_time ? `

    Time: ${scheduled_time}

    ` : ''} ${duration_minutes ? `

    Duration: ${duration_minutes} min

    ` : ''}

    Log in to your portal to view client details and care plan. Questions? Call Lance at 647-382-8047.

    Proximity Care Services Inc. · Mississauga, Ontario

    ` }).catch(e => log('warn', 'new booking PSW notify failed', { error: e?.message || String(e) })); } } catch (pswNotifyErr) { log('warn', 'POST /hq/booking PSW notify error', { error: pswNotifyErr.message }); } } res.json({ success: true, booking: data }); } catch (err) { res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // GET /hq/visits — visit log with summary stats // PATCH /hq/visit/:id/verify — Build 9+9B+9C+11 // Verifies a visit, optionally corrects time, logs audit trail, fires family summary email // PATCH /hq/visit/:id — HQ manual edit // POST /hq/visits/bulk-edit — Edit multiple visits in one call (pre-payday corrections) // Body: { operator_id, edited_by, visits: [{ id, time_in, time_out, manual_hours, notes }] } // Each visit uses same logic as PATCH /hq/visit/:id — writes manual_hours_override. app.post('/hq/visits/bulk-edit', async (req, res) => { try { const _auth = await validateHQToken(req); } const now = new Date().toISOString(); const results = []; for (const edit of editList) { const { id, time_in, time_out, manual_hours, notes } = edit; if (!id) { results.push({ id, success: false, error: 'Missing visit id' }); continue; } const { data: visit, error: fetchErr } = await supabase .from('visits').select('*').eq('id', id).single(); if (fetchErr || !visit) { results.push({ id, success: false, error: 'Visit not found' }); continue; } const updatePayload = { hq_edited: true, hq_edited_at: now, hq_edited_by: edited_by }; if (time_in) { updatePayload.original_time_in = visit.time_in; updatePayload.time_in = time_in; } if (time_out) { updatePayload.original_time_out = visit.time_out; updatePayload.time_out = time_out; } if (manual_hours != null) updatePayload.manual_hours_override = parseFloat(manual_hours); if (notes) updatePayload.hq_notes = notes; const { error: updateErr } = await supabase.from('visits').update(updatePayload).eq('id', id); if (updateErr) { results.push({ id, success: false, error: updateErr.message }); continue; } // Notify PSW if hours changed if (visit.psw_name && (time_in || time_out || manual_hours != null)) { const msg = manual_hours != null ? `Your hours for ${visit.client_name} on ${visit.visit_date} were updated to ${manual_hours}h by HQ (bulk edit). Pay summary updated.`; await supabase.from('psw_notes').insert({ operator_id, psw_name: visit.psw_name, sender: 'HQ', message: msg, created_at: now }).catch(() => {}); } results.push({ id, success: true, visit_date: visit.visit_date, manual_hours_override: updatePayload.manual_hours_override }); } const succeeded = results.filter(r => r.success).length; log('info', 'visits.bulk_edit', { operator_id, edited_by, total: editList.length, succeeded }); res.json({ success: true, total: editList.length, succeeded, failed: editList.length - succeeded, results }); } catch (err) { log('error', '/hq/visits/bulk-edit error', { error: err.message || String(err) }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // PATCH /hq/visit/:id — single visit edit (existing) app.patch('/hq/visit/:id', async (req, res) => { try { const _auth = await validateHQToken(req); 'Your hours for ' + visit.client_name + ' on ' + visit.visit_date + ' were updated to ' + manual_hours + 'h by HQ.' : 'Your visit times for ' + visit.client_name + ' on ' + visit.visit_date + ' were corrected by HQ.'; await supabase.from('psw_notes').insert({ operator_id, psw_name: visit.psw_name, sender: 'HQ', message: mn + ' Your pay summary has been updated.', created_at: now }).catch(function(){}); } // Notify family when visit times or hours are corrected — transparency on record changes if (time_in || time_out || manual_hours != null) { try { const nameParts = (visit.client_name || '').trim().split(/\s+/); const { data: clientRec } = await supabase.from('clients') .select('family_email, family_contact_name, first_name') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .eq('first_name', nameParts[0] || '') .eq('last_name', nameParts.slice(1).join(' ') || '') .maybeSingle(); if (clientRec?.family_email) { const greet = clientRec.family_contact_name ? clientRec.family_contact_name.split(' ')[0] : (clientRec.first_name || 'Family'); const changeDesc = manual_hours != null ? `The recorded hours for the visit on ${visit.visit_date} have been updated to ${manual_hours}h.` : `The visit times for ${visit.visit_date} have been corrected in our records.`; await sendEmail({ to: clientRec.family_email, subject: `Visit record updated — ${visit.client_name} · ${visit.visit_date}`, html: `
