    ${changeDesc} This is a routine administrative correction and does not affect care quality.

    Questions? Call Lance at 647-382-8047.

    Proximity Care Services Inc. · Mississauga, Ontario · 647-382-8047

    ` }).catch(() => {}); } } catch (famErr) { log('warn', 'visit.edit family notify failed', { error: famErr.message }); } } log('info', 'visit.hq_edit', { operator_id, id, edited_by }); res.json({ success: true, visit_id: id }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'PATCH /hq/visit/:id error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req && req._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // POST /hq/visit — manual visit entry app.post('/hq/visit', async (req, res) => { try { const _auth = await validateHQToken(req); if (!_auth) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'HQ session required' }); const { operator_id = 'proximity-care', psw_name, client_name, visit_date, time_in, time_out, manual_hours, status = 'completed', visit_summary = '', entry_reason = '', entered_by = 'lance' } = req.body; if (!psw_name || !client_name || !visit_date) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'psw_name, client_name, visit_date required' }); const now = new Date().toISOString(); const { data: newVisit, error } = await supabase.from('visits').insert({ operator_id, psw_name, client_name, visit_date, time_in: time_in || null, time_out: time_out || null, status, visit_summary, entry_type: 'manual', manual_hours_override: manual_hours ? parseFloat(manual_hours) : null, hq_edited: true, hq_edited_at: now, hq_edited_by: entered_by, hq_notes: entry_reason, checkin_time: now, checkout_time: now }).select().single(); if (error) throw error; await supabase.from('psw_notes').insert({ operator_id, psw_name, sender: 'HQ', message: 'A visit for ' + client_name + ' on ' + visit_date + ' was manually added to your record by HQ' + (entry_reason ? ': ' + entry_reason : '') + '. Check your pay summary.', created_at: now }).catch(function(){}); log('info', 'visit.manual_entry', { operator_id, psw_name, client_name, visit_date, entered_by }); res.json({ success: true, visit_id: newVisit.id }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'POST /hq/visit error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req && req._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); app.patch('/hq/visit/:id/verify', async (req, res) => { try { const { id } = req.params; const { operator_id = 'proximity-care', verified_by = 'lance', corrected_time_in, corrected_time_out } = req.body; // Fetch the visit first const { data: visit, error: fetchErr } = await supabase .from('visits').select('*').eq('id', id).single(); updatePayload.time_in = corrected_time_in; } if (corrected_time_out) { updatePayload.original_time_out = visit.time_out; updatePayload.time_out = corrected_time_out; } updatePayload.time_corrected_by = verified_by; updatePayload.time_corrected_at = now; // EC-8 — flag invoice as needs_review if visit was corrected after invoice sent try { const visitDate = new Date(visit.visit_date + 'T12:00:00'); const monthNames = ['January','February','March','April','May','June','July','August','September','October','November','December']; const month = monthNames[visitDate.getMonth()]; const year = visitDate.getFullYear(); const { data: relatedInvoice } = await supabase .from('invoices') .select('id, status, visit_ids') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .eq('client_name', visit.client_name) .eq('month', month) .eq('year', year) .in('status', ['sent', 'paid']) .maybeSingle(); } } catch (_) {} } const { error: updateErr } = await supabase .from('visits').update(updatePayload).eq('id', id); if (updateErr) throw updateErr; // Fetch updated visit for email const { data: updatedVisit } = await supabase .from('visits').select('*').eq('id', id).single(); const tasks = Array.isArray(updatedVisit.tasks_completed) ? updatedVisit.tasks_completed.join(', ') : ''; const mood = updatedVisit.client_mood || 'not recorded'; const hours = parseFloat(updatedVisit.hours_worked || 0).toFixed(2); const rating = updatedVisit.satisfaction_rating ? `${updatedVisit.satisfaction_rating}/5` : 'not rated'; await sendEmail({ to: clientRow.family_email, subject: `Visit summary — ${updatedVisit.client_name} · ${updatedVisit.visit_date}`, html: `

    Proximity Care Services · Visit Summary

    ${updatedVisit.client_name}

    Hi ${familyName},

    Here is the summary for today's visit with ${updatedVisit.psw_name}.

    ${note ? `

    ${note}

    ` : ''} ${tasks ? `` : ''}
    Visit date${updatedVisit.visit_date}
    Hours${hours}h
    Mood${mood}
    Tasks${tasks}
    Rating${rating}

    Questions? Reply to this email or call 647-382-8047.

    Proximity Care Services Inc. · 647-382-8047

    ` }); } } catch (emailErr) { log('error', 'verify: family summary email error', { error: emailErr.message || String(emailErr), trace_id: req?._traceId }); } // Notify PSW via psw_notes if times were corrected if ((corrected_time_in || corrected_time_out) && visit.psw_name) { try { await supabase.from('psw_notes').insert({ operator_id, psw_name: visit.psw_name, sender: 'HQ', message: `Your visit times for ${visit.client_name} on ${visit.visit_date} were corrected by HQ: ${corrected_time_in||visit.time_in} → ${corrected_time_out||visit.time_out}. Your records have been updated.`, created_at: now }); } catch {} // Log to system_logs try { await supabase.from('system_logs').insert({ operator_id, event_type: 'visit.time_corrected', event_source: 'hq', contact_name: visit.psw_name, status: 'complete', notes: JSON.stringify({ visit_id: id, client: visit.client_name, date: visit.visit_date, original_in: visit.time_in, corrected_in: corrected_time_in, original_out: visit.time_out, corrected_out: corrected_time_out }), created_at: now }); } catch {} } log('info', 'visit.verify', { operator_id, id, verified_by, time_corrected: !!(corrected_time_in || corrected_time_out) }); res.json({ success: true, visit_id: id, verified: true, time_corrected: !!(corrected_time_in || corrected_time_out) }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'PATCH /hq/visit/:id/verify error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); app.get('/hq/visits', async (req, res) => { try { const opId = req.query.operator_id || 'proximity-care'; let query = supabase .from('visits') .select('*') .eq('operator_id', opId) .order('visit_date', { ascending: false }) .limit(limitVal); if (fromDate) query = query.gte('visit_date', fromDate); if (toDate) query = query.lte('visit_date', toDate); if (pswFilter) query = query.eq('psw_name', pswFilter); const { data: visits, error } = await query; if (error) throw error; const today = torontoDate(); const todayVisits = (visits || []).filter(v => v.visit_date === today); const hoursToday = todayVisits.reduce((sum, v) => sum + parseFloat(v.hours_worked || 0), 0); const pswsToday = [...new Set(todayVisits.map(v => v.psw_name).filter(Boolean))]; // Monthly totals (current calendar month) const monthStr = today.slice(0, 7); const monthVisits = (visits || []).filter(v => (v.visit_date || '').startsWith(monthStr)); const hoursMonth = monthVisits.reduce((sum, v) => sum + parseFloat(v.hours_worked || 0), 0); res.json({ visits: visits || [], summary: { today_count: todayVisits.length, hours_today: Math.round(hoursToday * 100) / 100, psws_active_today: pswsToday.length, total_count: (visits || []).length, month_count: monthVisits.length, hours_month: Math.round(hoursMonth * 100) / 100, } }); } catch (err) { res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // GET /psw/clients/:psw_name — clients assigned to a PSW app.get('/psw/clients/:psw_name', async (req, res) => { try { const { psw_name } = req.params; if (missed.length === 0) { console.log(`S01 missed-check: all visits logged for ${today}`); return res.json({ success: true, checked: clients.length, missed: 0 }); } // Fire alert email to Lance const missedList = missed.map(c => `${c.assigned_psw} → ${c.first_name} ${c.last_name}` ).join('
    '); await sendEmail({ to: 'healthcareproximity@gmail.com', subject: `⚠ Missed visit alert — ${missed.length} PSW${missed.length > 1 ? 's' : ''} not logged today`, html: `

} }); // GET /psw/applicants — HQ reads the pipeline app.get('/psw/applicants', async (req, res) => { try { // Requires valid HQ session token const tokenOp = await validateHQToken(req); if (!tokenOp && req.query.watchdog_pin !== WATCHDOG_PIN) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'HQ session required' }); const operator_id = req.query.operator_id || tokenOp || 'proximity-care'; const { data, error } = await supabase .from('psw_applicants') .select('*') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .order('created_at', { ascending: false }); if (error) throw error; res.json({ success: true, applicants: data || [] }); } catch (err) { res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // DELETE /psw/applicants/:id — dismiss/remove an applicant from HQ view app.delete('/psw/applicants/:id', async (req, res) => { try { const { id } = req.params; const { operator_id } = req.query; if (!id || !operator_id) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Missing id or operator_id' }); // Delete onboard tokens first (foreign key constraint) await supabase.from('psw_onboard_tokens').delete().eq('applicant_id', id); } }); // ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── // CSV BULK IMPORT — PSWs and Clients // ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── // POST /operator/import-psws — CSV upload activates all PSWs in bulk app.post('/operator/import-psws', upload.single('file'), async (req, res) => { try { const operator_id = req.body.operator_id || 'proximity-care'; if (!req.file) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No CSV file uploaded' }); // Parse CSV — expected columns: first_name, last_name, email, phone, city, languages const csv = req.file.buffer.toString('utf8'); const lines = csv.split('\n').map(l => l.trim()).filter(Boolean); if (lines.length < 2) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'CSV must have header row + at least one data row' }); // Parse header const headers = lines[0].split(',').map(h => h.trim().toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z_]/g, '')); const required = ['first_name', 'last_name']; const missing = required.filter(r => !headers.includes(r)); if (missing.length) return res.status(400).json({ error: `Missing required columns: ${missing.join(', ')}` }); const results = { activated: [], failed: [], skipped: [] }; // Get current PSW count for code generation const { count: startCount } = await supabase.from('psws') .select('*', { count: 'exact', head: true }).eq('operator_id', operator_id); let pswIndex = (startCount || 0); for (let i = 1; i < lines.length; i++) { const vals = lines[i].split(',').map(v => v.trim().replace(/^"|"$/g, '')); if (vals.length < 2) continue; const row = {}; headers.forEach((h, idx) => { row[h] = vals[idx] || ''; }); const firstName = row.first_name || ''; const lastName = row.last_name || ''; const fullName = `${firstName} ${lastName}`.trim(); const email = row.email || ''; const phone = row.phone || ''; const city = row.city || ''; const languages = row.languages || ''; if (!fullName || fullName === ' ') { results.skipped.push(`Row ${i}: empty name`); continue; } if (!email) { results.skipped.push(`Row ${i}: ${fullName} — no email`); continue; } try { pswIndex++; const pin = String(Math.floor(1000 + Math.random() * 9000)); const prefix = operator_id.replace(/-/g, '').toUpperCase().slice(0, 2); const psw_code = `${prefix}-P${String(pswIndex).padStart(3, '0')}`; const { error: upsertErr } = await supabase.from('psws').upsert({ operator_id, full_name: fullName, first_name: firstName, last_name: lastName, email, phone: phone || null, pin, status: 'active', psw_code, city: city || null, languages: languages || null, onboarding_complete: true }, { onConflict: 'operator_id,email' }); if (upsertErr) throw upsertErr; // Send welcome email const portalUrl = `https://psw.proximitycares.ca?op=${operator_id}`; await sendEmail({ to: email, subject: `Welcome to the team — your portal access`, html: `

    Welcome to the team.

    Hi ${firstName},

    Your portal access is ready. Use the details below to log in and start logging your visits.

    Your Login Details

    Portal: ${portalUrl}

    PSW ID: ${psw_code}

    PIN: ${pin}

    After each visit, open the portal on your phone, enter your PIN, and log your visit. Takes under 2 minutes.

    Questions? Call 647-382-8047.

    Keep your PIN private. Do not share it with anyone.

    ` }); results.activated.push({ name: fullName, email, psw_code, pin }); } catch (rowErr) { results.failed.push({ name: fullName, email, error: rowErr.message }); } } // Notify Lance await sendEmail({ to: 'healthcareproximity@gmail.com', subject: `CSV Import complete — ${results.activated.length} PSWs activated for ${operator_id}`, html: `

    ${results.activated.length} PSWs activated · ${results.failed.length} failed · ${results.skipped.length} skipped

    Activated: ${results.activated.map(p => `${p.name} (${p.psw_code})`).join(', ')}

    ${results.failed.length ? `

    Failed: ${results.failed.map(p => `${p.name}: ${p.error}`).join(', ')}

    ` : ''} ${results.skipped.length ? `

    Skipped: ${results.skipped.join(', ')}

    ` : ''}` }); res.json({ success: true, operator_id, ...results, total: results.activated.length }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'import-psws error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // POST /operator/import-clients — CSV upload onboards all clients in bulk app.post('/operator/import-clients', upload.single('file'), async (req, res) => { try { const operator_id = req.body.operator_id || 'proximity-care'; if (!req.file) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No CSV file uploaded' }); const csv = req.file.buffer.toString('utf8'); const lines = csv.split('\n').map(l => l.trim()).filter(Boolean); if (lines.length < 2) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'CSV must have header + data rows' }); const headers = lines[0].split(',').map(h => h.trim().toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z_]/g, '')); const results = { onboarded: [], failed: [], skipped: [] }; const { count: startCount } = await supabase.from('clients') .select('*', { count: 'exact', head: true }).eq('operator_id', operator_id); let clientIndex = (startCount || 0); for (let i = 1; i < lines.length; i++) { const vals = lines[i].split(',').map(v => v.trim().replace(/^"|"$/g, '')); if (vals.length < 2) continue; const row = {}; headers.forEach((h, idx) => { row[h] = vals[idx] || ''; }); const firstName = row.first_name || row.client_first_name || ''; const lastName = row.last_name || row.client_last_name || ''; const familyEmail = row.family_email || row.email || ''; const familyPhone = row.family_phone || row.phone || ''; const familyName = row.family_name || row.family_contact || ''; const assignedPSW = row.assigned_psw || ''; const careNotes = row.care_notes || row.notes || ''; const clientRate = parseFloat(row.client_rate || row.rate || '28') || 28; const pswRate = parseFloat(row.psw_rate || '22') || 22; if (!firstName) { results.skipped.push(`Row ${i}: empty name`); continue; } try { clientIndex++; const prefix = operator_id.replace(/-/g, '').toUpperCase().slice(0, 2); const client_code = `${prefix}-C${String(clientIndex).padStart(3, '0')}`; const portalSlug = `${firstName.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z]/g, '')}-${lastName.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z]/g, '')}-${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2,6)}`; const portalPin = String(Math.floor(1000 + Math.random() * 9000)); const { error: insertErr } = await supabase.from('clients').upsert({ operator_id, first_name: firstName, last_name: lastName, family_email: familyEmail || null, family_phone: familyPhone || null, family_name: familyName || null, assigned_psw: assignedPSW || null, care_notes: careNotes || null, client_rate: clientRate, psw_rate: pswRate, portal_slug: portalSlug, portal_pin: portalPin, client_code, status: 'active' }, { onConflict: 'operator_id,portal_slug' }); if (insertErr) throw insertErr; // Send family portal welcome email if email exists if (familyEmail) { const portalUrl = `https://proximitycares.ca/family.html?c=${portalSlug}`; await sendEmail({ to: familyEmail, subject: `Your family portal is ready — ${firstName} ${lastName}`, html: `

    Your Family Portal

    Hi ${familyName || 'there'},

    Your family portal for ${firstName} ${lastName} is ready. Use the details below to check visit updates, care notes, and stay connected with your care team.

    Your Portal Access

    Portal: https://proximitycares.ca/family.html?c=${portalSlug}

    PIN: ${portalPin}

    Questions? Call 647-382-8047.

    Proximity Care Services Inc. · Mississauga · proximitycares.ca

    ` }); } results.onboarded.push({ name: `${firstName} ${lastName}`, client_code, portal_pin: portalPin }); // S04: Schedule family onboarding sequence Day 1, 3, 7 if (familyEmail) { try { const now = Date.now(); const dayMs = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000; const famRows = [ { send_at: new Date(now + 1 * dayMs).toISOString(), template_key: 'family_onboard_day1' }, { send_at: new Date(now + 3 * dayMs).toISOString(), template_key: 'family_onboard_day3' }, { send_at: new Date(now + 7 * dayMs).toISOString(), template_key: 'family_onboard_day7' } ].map(r => ({ operator_id, recipient_email: familyEmail, recipient_name: familyName || firstName, template_key: r.template_key, send_at: r.send_at, source_table: 'clients', metadata: JSON.stringify({ client_name: `${firstName} ${lastName}`, family_name: familyName || firstName, assigned_psw: assignedPSW, agency_name: operator_id, agency_phone: '647-382-8047', portal_url: `https://proximitycares.ca/family.html?c=${portalSlug}` }) })); await supabase.from('scheduled_emails').insert(famRows); } catch (seqErr) { log('error', 'S04 family sequence error', { error: seqErr.message || String(seqErr), trace_id: req?._traceId }); } } } catch (rowErr) { results.failed.push({ name: `${firstName} ${lastName}`, error: rowErr.message }); } } res.json({ success: true, operator_id, ...results, total: results.onboarded.length }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'import-clients error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // POST /hq/import-bookings — Bulk booking CSV import // CSV columns (header row required): psw_name, client_name, date, time_in, duration_minutes // Returns: { imported, skipped, errors[] } — per-row error reporting app.post('/hq/import-bookings', upload.single('file'), async (req, res) => { try { const operator_id = req.body.operator_id || 'proximity-care'; if (!req.file) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'CSV file required' }); const raw = req.file.buffer.toString('utf8'); const lines = raw.split(/\r?\n/).map(l => l.trim()).filter(Boolean); if (lines.length < 2) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'CSV must have header row + at least one data row' }); // Parse header const header = lines[0].split(',').map(h => h.trim().toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z_]/g,'')); const idx = { psw_name: header.indexOf('psw_name'), client_name: header.indexOf('client_name'), date: header.indexOf('date'), time_in: header.indexOf('time_in'), duration_minutes: header.indexOf('duration_minutes') }; const missing = Object.entries(idx).filter(([,v]) => v === -1).map(([k]) => k); if (missing.length) return res.status(400).json({ error: `Missing CSV columns: ${missing.join(', ')}` }); // Load active PSWs and clients once for validation const { data: psws } = await supabase.from('psws').select('full_name').eq('operator_id', operator_id).eq('status', 'active'); const { data: clients } = await supabase.from('clients').select('first_name, last_name').eq('operator_id', operator_id).eq('status', 'active'); const pswNames = new Set((psws||[]).map(p => p.full_name?.toLowerCase())); const clientNames = new Set((clients||[]).map(c => `${c.first_name} ${c.last_name||''}`.trim().toLowerCase())); // Load existing bookings for conflict detection (O(n) Map) const { data: existing } = await supabase.from('bookings') .select('assigned_to, scheduled_date, scheduled_time, duration_minutes') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .eq('status', 'scheduled'); const conflictMap = new Map(); for (const b of existing||[]) { const key = `${b.assigned_to?.toLowerCase()}|${b.scheduled_date}`; if (!conflictMap.has(key)) conflictMap.set(key, []); conflictMap.get(key).push({ time: b.scheduled_time, dur: parseInt(b.duration_minutes||60) }); } const results = { imported: [], skipped: [], errors: [] }; const toInsert = []; for (let i = 1; i < lines.length; i++) { const cols = lines[i].split(',').map(c => c.trim().replace(/^"|"$/g,'')); const row = { psw_name: cols[idx.psw_name] || '', client_name: cols[idx.client_name] || '', date: cols[idx.date] || '', time_in: cols[idx.time_in] || '', duration_minutes: parseInt(cols[idx.duration_minutes]) || 60 }; // Validate if (!row.psw_name || !row.client_name || !row.date || !row.time_in) { results.errors.push({ row: i, data: row, reason: 'Missing required field' }); continue; } if (!pswNames.has(row.psw_name.toLowerCase())) { results.errors.push({ row: i, data: row, reason: `PSW not found: ${row.psw_name}` }); continue; } if (!clientNames.has(row.client_name.toLowerCase())) { results.errors.push({ row: i, data: row, reason: `Client not found: ${row.client_name}` }); continue; } if (!/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/.test(row.date)) { results.errors.push({ row: i, data: row, reason: 'Date must be YYYY-MM-DD format' }); continue; } if (!/^\d{2}:\d{2}$/.test(row.time_in)) { results.errors.push({ row: i, data: row, reason: 'time_in must be HH:MM format' }); continue; } // Conflict check — does this PSW already have a booking overlapping this slot? const key = `${row.psw_name.toLowerCase()}|${row.date}`; const existing_slots = conflictMap.get(key) || []; const newStart = parseInt(row.time_in.replace(':','')); const newEnd = newStart + Math.floor(row.duration_minutes / 60) * 100 + (row.duration_minutes % 60); const conflict = existing_slots.find(s => { const sStart = parseInt(s.time.replace(':','')); const sEnd = sStart + Math.floor(s.dur / 60) * 100 + (s.dur % 60); return newStart < sEnd && newEnd > sStart; }); if (conflict) { results.skipped.push({ row: i, data: row, reason: `Conflict: ${row.psw_name} already scheduled at ${conflict.time} on ${row.date}` }); continue; } toInsert.push({ operator_id, assigned_to: row.psw_name, client_name: row.client_name, scheduled_date: row.date, scheduled_time: row.time_in, duration_minutes: row.duration_minutes, booking_type: 'scheduled', status: 'scheduled', series_id: null }); // Add to conflict map so subsequent rows in same file see it if (!conflictMap.has(key)) conflictMap.set(key, []); conflictMap.get(key).push({ time: row.time_in, dur: row.duration_minutes }); } // Batch insert valid rows if (toInsert.length) { const { data: inserted, error: insertErr } = await supabase.from('bookings').insert(toInsert).select('id, assigned_to, client_name, scheduled_date, scheduled_time'); if (insertErr) throw insertErr; results.imported = inserted || []; } try { await supabase.from('system_logs').insert({ operator_id, event_type: 'bulk_booking_import', event_source: '/hq/import-bookings', status: 'success', notes: JSON.stringify({ imported: results.imported.length, skipped: results.skipped.length, errors: results.errors.length }), created_at: new Date().toISOString() }); } catch {} res.json({ success: true, imported: results.imported.length, skipped: results.skipped.length, errors: results.errors.length, details: results }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'import-bookings error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // POST /operator/post-close — fires operator welcome + config builder emails on close app.post('/operator/post-close', async (req, res) => { try { const { operator_id, agency_name, owner_name, owner_email, config_builder_url } = req.body; } }); // POST /psw/onboard/init — generate secure token and fire onboarding email app.post('/psw/onboard/init', async (req, res) => { try { const { applicant_id, operator_id = 'proximity-care' } = req.body; } catch (err) { res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // POST /visit/checklist-check — 8pm EST cron — checks visits AND checklist completion app.post('/visit/checklist-check', async (req, res) => { try { const operator_id = req.body.operator_id || 'proximity-care'; // Time gate — only execute between 7:45pm and 9:00pm Toronto time // Prevents duplicate alerts when called outside the intended window const force = req.body.force === true; // watchdog bypass if (!force) { const torontoHour = parseInt(new Date().toLocaleString('en-CA', { timeZone: 'America/Toronto', hour: 'numeric', hour12: false }), 10); const torontoMin = parseInt(new Date().toLocaleString('en-CA', { timeZone: 'America/Toronto', minute: 'numeric' }), 10); const nowMins = torontoHour * 60 + torontoMin; if (nowMins < 19 * 60 + 45 || nowMins > 21 * 60) { log('info', 'checklist-check.skipped.outside-window', { operator_id, torontoHour, torontoMin }); return res.json({ success: true, skipped: true, reason: 'outside_window', window: '19:45-21:00 Toronto' }); } } const today = new Date().toLocaleDateString('en-CA', { timeZone: 'America/Toronto' }); // Dedup guard — if an alert was already sent today, skip entirely // Covers edge case where Railway cron fires twice or endpoint is called manually mid-window if (!force) { const { data: alreadyRan } = await supabase .from('system_logs') .select('id') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .eq('event_type', 'checklist_check_alert') .gte('created_at', today + 'T00:00:00-04:00') .maybeSingle(); if (incompleteChecklist.length) issues.push(`${incompleteChecklist.length} visit${incompleteChecklist.length>1?'s':''} logged without completing the checklist`); if (!issues.length) { console.log(`S01 checklist-check: all clear for ${today}`); try { await supabase.from('system_logs').insert({ operator_id, event_type: 'checklist_check_run', event_source: '/visit/checklist-check', payload: { checked: clients.length, missed: 0, incomplete: 0, reason: 'all_clear' }, status: 'complete', created_at: new Date().toISOString() }); } catch {} return res.json({ success: true, checked: clients.length, issues: 0 }); } // Build alert email const missedRows = missedVisit.map((c, i) => ` ${c.assigned_psw} No visit logged · Client: ${c.first_name} ${c.last_name} ` ).join(''); const checklistRows = incompleteChecklist.map((name, i) => ` ${name} Visit logged · Checklist incomplete ` ).join(''); await sendEmail({ to: 'healthcareproximity@gmail.com', subject: `⚠ 8pm check — ${issues.join(' · ')} · ${today}`, html: `

    8PM VISIT CHECK · ${today}

    ${issues.join(' · ')}

    ${missedVisit.length ? `

    VISITS NOT LOGGED

    ${missedRows}
    ` : ''} ${incompleteChecklist.length ? `

    CHECKLISTS INCOMPLETE

    ${checklistRows}
    ` : ''}

    Call or message each PSW to confirm care was delivered and checklist completed.

    Proximity Care · 8pm automated check · 647-382-8047

    ${pswList}
    PSWExpiring

    Open HQ → PSWs tab to manage.

    ` }); } res.json({ success: true, checked: psws.length, alerts_sent: alertsSent }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'psw/expiry-check error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); } }); // POST /psw/cancel-shift — EC-7 — PSW-initiated shift cancellation app.post('/psw/cancel-shift', async (req, res) => { try { const { psw_name, pin, operator_id = 'proximity-care', booking_id, reason } = req.body; if ((count || 0) === 0 && op.owner_email) { // Fire churn check-in email immediately const tpl = FOLLOW_UP_TEMPLATES.operator_churn_day14; if (tpl) { const firstName = (op.owner_name || '').split(' ')[0] || 'there'; await sendEmail({ to: op.owner_email, subject: renderTemplate(tpl.subject, { name: firstName, agency_name: op.agency_name }), html: renderTemplate(tpl.html, { name: firstName, agency_name: op.agency_name }) }); alerted++; console.log(`Churn check-in sent for ${op.operator_id}`); } } } res.json({ success: true, checked: operators.length, alerted }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'churn-check error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── // CLIENT ONBOARDING PORTAL — 3 endpoints // POST /client/onboard/init — generate token, fire intake link email // GET /client/onboard/:token — validate token, return operator branding // POST /client/onboard/submit — intake submission → client row + S04 sequence // ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── // POST /client/onboard/init — HQ fires this to send family the intake link app.post('/client/onboard/init', async (req, res) => { try { const { operator_id = 'proximity-care', family_email, family_name, client_name, client_email, client_first_name, client_last_name } = req.body; // Accept either family_* or client_* field names const constructedClientName = [client_first_name, client_last_name].filter(Boolean).join(' ').trim(); const familyEmail = family_email || client_email; const familyName = family_name || constructedClientName || null; const clientNameValue = client_name || constructedClientName || null; if (!familyEmail) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'family_email (or client_email) required' }); const token = require('crypto').randomBytes(32).toString('hex'); const expiresAt = new Date(Date.now() + 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000).toISOString(); const { error: insertErr } = await supabase.from('client_onboard_tokens').insert({ token, operator_id, family_email: familyEmail, family_name: familyName, client_name: clientNameValue, expires_at: expiresAt }); if (insertErr) throw insertErr; const op = await getOperator(operator_id); const agencyName = op?.name || 'Proximity Care Services'; const intakeUrl = `https://proximitycares.ca/client-onboard.html?token=${token}`; const greeting = (familyName || '').split(' ')[0] || 'Hello'; const clientFirst = (clientNameValue || '').split(' ')[0] || 'your family member'; await sendEmail({ to: familyEmail, subject: `Complete your care intake — ${agencyName}`, html: `

    Proximity Care Services

    Care Intake

    Hi ${greeting},

    We are getting ${clientFirst}'s care ready. To move forward, we need you to complete a short intake form. It takes about 5 minutes and covers care needs, emergency contacts, and a care agreement.

    Once submitted, we will set up the family portal and you will receive your login PIN by email.

    Complete Care Intake →

    This link expires in 7 days. Questions? Call 647-382-8047.

    Proximity Care Services Inc. · Mississauga, Ontario · 647-382-8047

    ` }); console.log('client/onboard/init: token issued'); res.json({ success: true, token, intake_url: intakeUrl, expires_at: expiresAt }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'client/onboard/init error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // GET /client/onboard/:token — validate token, return branding for the portal page app.get('/client/onboard/:token', async (req, res) => { try { const { token } = req.params; const { data: tokenRec, error } = await supabase .from('client_onboard_tokens') .select('*') .eq('token', token) .gt('expires_at', new Date().toISOString()) .single(); if (error || !tokenRec) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid or expired link' }); const { data: opConfig } = await supabase .from('operator_config') .select('agency_name, brand_primary, brand_accent, owner_name, owner_phone') .eq('operator_id', tokenRec.operator_id) .single(); res.json({ success: true, token, operator_id: tokenRec.operator_id, family_email: tokenRec.family_email, family_name: tokenRec.family_name || null, client_name: tokenRec.client_name || null, agency_name: opConfig?.agency_name || 'Proximity Care Services', brand_primary: opConfig?.brand_primary || '#1B3A6B', brand_accent: opConfig?.brand_accent || '#b87010', owner_name: opConfig?.owner_name || 'Lance Salazar', owner_phone: opConfig?.owner_phone || '647-382-8047' }); } catch (err) { res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // POST /client/onboard/submit — full intake form submission app.post('/client/onboard/submit', async (req, res) => { try { const { token, operator_id = 'proximity-care', // Client identity first_name, last_name, date_of_birth, address, city, postal_code, // Care needs care_type, mobility_level, cognitive_status, medications, physician_name, physician_phone, // Emergency contacts emergency_contact_1_name, emergency_contact_1_phone, emergency_contact_1_relation, emergency_contact_2_name, emergency_contact_2_phone, emergency_contact_2_relation, // Family contact (portal access) family_name, family_email, family_phone, // Care notes / special instructions care_notes, // Agreement agreement_accepted, agreement_timestamp, // C8 — Referral source referral_source, referral_detail } = req.body; if (!token) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'token required' }); if (!first_name || !last_name) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Client name required' }); if (!family_email) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'family_email required' }); if (!agreement_accepted) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Care agreement must be accepted' }); // Validate token const { data: tokenRec, error: tokenErr } = await supabase .from('client_onboard_tokens') .select('*') .eq('token', token) .gt('expires_at', new Date().toISOString()) .single(); if (tokenErr || !tokenRec) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid or expired link' }); // Generate portal slug + PIN const slugBase = `${first_name}${last_name}`.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z]/g, ''); const slugSuffix = Math.floor(100 + Math.random() * 900); const portal_slug = `${slugBase}${slugSuffix}`; const portal_pin = String(Math.floor(1000 + Math.random() * 9000)); // Generate client_code const { count: existingClients } = await supabase .from('clients') .select('*', { count: 'exact', head: true }) .eq('operator_id', operator_id); const opPrefix = operator_id === 'proximity-care' ? 'PC' : operator_id.toUpperCase().slice(0, 3); const client_code = `${opPrefix}-C${String((existingClients || 0) + 1).padStart(3, '0')}`; // Build care notes summary for the client row const fullCareNotes = [ care_notes ? `Special instructions: ${care_notes}` : null, medications ? `Medications: ${medications}` : null, physician_name ? `Physician: ${physician_name}${physician_phone ? ' · ' + physician_phone : ''}` : null, emergency_contact_1_name ? `Emergency 1: ${emergency_contact_1_name} (${emergency_contact_1_relation || 'contact'}) ${emergency_contact_1_phone || ''}` : null, emergency_contact_2_name ? `Emergency 2: ${emergency_contact_2_name} (${emergency_contact_2_relation || 'contact'}) ${emergency_contact_2_phone || ''}` : null ].filter(Boolean).join(' | '); // Insert client row const { data: client, error: clientErr } = await supabase.from('clients').insert({ operator_id, client_code, portal_slug, portal_pin, first_name, last_name, date_of_birth: date_of_birth || null, address: address ? `${address}, ${city || ''}, ${postal_code || ''}`.trim().replace(/,\s*,/g, ',') : null, care_type: care_type || null, mobility_level: mobility_level || null, cognitive_status: cognitive_status || null, medications: medications || null, physician_name: physician_name || null, physician_phone: physician_phone || null, emergency_contact_1_name: emergency_contact_1_name || null, emergency_contact_1_phone: emergency_contact_1_phone || null, emergency_contact_1_relation: emergency_contact_1_relation || null, emergency_contact_2_name: emergency_contact_2_name || null, emergency_contact_2_phone: emergency_contact_2_phone || null, emergency_contact_2_relation: emergency_contact_2_relation || null, family_email, family_contact_name: family_name || null, family_phone: family_phone || null, care_notes: fullCareNotes || null, agreement_accepted: true, agreement_timestamp: agreement_timestamp || new Date().toISOString(), consent_given: true, consent_date: new Date().toISOString(), consent_version: '1.0', referral_source: referral_source || null, referral_detail: referral_detail || null, status: 'pending_activation', client_rate: 22, psw_rate: 19 }).select().single(); if (clientErr) throw clientErr; // Mark token used await supabase.from('client_onboard_tokens') .update({ used_at: new Date().toISOString() }) .eq('token', token); // Generate AI care plan from intake data let aiCarePlan = null; try { const carePrompt = [ `Client: ${first_name} ${last_name}`, date_of_birth ? `Date of birth: ${date_of_birth}` : null, care_type ? `Care type needed: ${care_type}` : null, mobility_level ? `Mobility: ${mobility_level}` : null, cognitive_status ? `Cognitive status: ${cognitive_status}` : null, medications ? `Current medications: ${medications}` : null, physician_name ? `Physician: ${physician_name}` : null, care_notes ? `Special instructions from family: ${care_notes}` : null, emergency_contact_1_name ? `Emergency contact: ${emergency_contact_1_name} (${emergency_contact_1_relation || 'contact'})` : null, ].filter(Boolean).join('\n'); const planResponse = await generateWithClaude( `Based on this client intake information, write a professional home care plan in plain prose. Include: 1) Overview of care needs, 2) Daily care priorities, 3) Safety considerations, 4) Communication notes for the PSW. Keep it practical, factual, and under 200 words. No markdown, no bullets, no asterisks — plain paragraphs only.\n\nClient intake:\n${carePrompt}`, 'You are a professional home care coordinator writing care plans for PSWs. Be specific, practical, and clinical. Plain prose only — no markdown formatting.' ); if (planResponse) { aiCarePlan = planResponse.replace(/[*_#`]/g, '').trim(); await supabase.from('clients') .update({ care_plan: aiCarePlan }) .eq('id', client.id) .eq('operator_id', operator_id); console.log('AI care plan generated'); } } catch(e) { log('error', 'AI care plan generation failed', { error: e.message || String(e), trace_id: req?._traceId }); } const portalUrl = `https://proximitycares.ca/family.html?c=${portal_slug}`; const clientFull = `${first_name} ${last_name}`; const greeting = (family_name || '').split(' ')[0] || 'Hello'; // Fire Day 0 welcome email with portal PIN await sendEmail({ to: family_email, subject: `Welcome to Proximity Care — your portal is ready`, html: `

    Proximity Care Services

    Intake Complete

    Hi ${greeting},

    We have received ${clientFull}'s care intake. Our team is reviewing it and will be in touch within 24 hours to confirm the care schedule and assign a PSW.

    In the meantime, your family portal is ready. You can use it to track visits, view the care plan, and message us any time.

    Your Portal Access

    PIN

    ${portal_pin}

    Open Family Portal →
    ${aiCarePlan ? `

    Your care plan: ${aiCarePlan}

    ` : ''}

    If you have any questions before we connect, reply to this email or call me at 647-382-8047.

    Warm regards,

    Lance Salazar

    Founder · Proximity Care Services · 647-382-8047

    Proximity Care Services Inc. · Mississauga, Ontario

    ` }); // Notify Lance await sendEmail({ to: 'healthcareproximity@gmail.com', subject: `New intake submitted: ${clientFull}`, html: `

    New Client Intake

    ${operator_id}

    Client

    ${clientFull}

    Family contact

    ${family_name || 'Not provided'} · ${family_email} · ${family_phone || 'no phone'}

    Care type

    ${care_type || 'Not specified'} · Mobility: ${mobility_level || 'not stated'} · Cognitive: ${cognitive_status || 'not stated'}

    Client code · Portal PIN

    ${client_code} · PIN: ${portal_pin}

    Review in HQ → Clients tab. Assign PSW and activate.

    ` }); // S04: Schedule family onboarding sequence Day 1, 3, 7 try { const now = Date.now(); const dayMs = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000; const famRows = [ { send_at: new Date(now + 1 * dayMs).toISOString(), template_key: 'family_onboard_day1' }, { send_at: new Date(now + 3 * dayMs).toISOString(), template_key: 'family_onboard_day3' }, { send_at: new Date(now + 7 * dayMs).toISOString(), template_key: 'family_onboard_day7' } ].map(r => ({ operator_id, recipient_email: family_email, recipient_name: family_name || first_name, template_key: r.template_key, send_at: r.send_at, source_table: 'clients', metadata: JSON.stringify({ client_name: clientFull, family_name: family_name || first_name, assigned_psw: 'your care team', agency_name: operator_id, agency_phone: '647-382-8047', portal_url: portalUrl }) })); await supabase.from('scheduled_emails').insert(famRows); } catch (seqErr) { log('error', 'S04 family sequence error', { error: seqErr.message || String(seqErr), trace_id: req?._traceId }); } console.log(`client/onboard/submit: portal ready, code=${client_code}`); res.json({ success: true, client_id: client.id, client_code, portal_slug, portal_pin, portal_url: portalUrl }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'client/onboard/submit error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── // SESSION 9 — SIGN IN / SIGN OUT + AVAILABILITY + PAY SUMMARY // POST /visit/checkin — PSW clocks in, creates in-progress visit row // POST /visit/checkout — PSW clocks out, completes visit, fires AI + notifications // POST /psw/availability — PSW writes their available days/shifts // GET /psw/pay-summary — hours × rate for current + past pay periods // GET /psw/schedule-upcoming — upcoming bookings for a PSW (date-filtered) // ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── // POST /visit/checkin — PSW arrives, creates in-progress visit app.post('/visit/checkin', async (req, res) => { try { const { psw_name, pin, operator_id = 'proximity-care', client_name, booking_id, latitude, longitude, accuracy, // B1: GPS accuracy in metres from client is_mock_location, // B1: client-side mock detection flag geofence_override_reason, // B2: override reason if out of range test_mode } = req.body; if (!psw_name || !pin) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'psw_name and pin required' }); if (!client_name) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'client_name required' }); // ── B1: GPS ACCURACY GATE ───────────────────────────────────────── // Reject low-accuracy GPS fix — no incumbent does this, first-mover advantage // accuracy = horizontal accuracy in metres from navigator.geolocation if (latitude && longitude && !test_mode) { if (typeof accuracy === 'number' && accuracy > 50) { return res.status(400).json({ error: 'GPS signal too weak. Move closer to a window and try again.', code: 'GPS_ACCURACY_LOW', accuracy_m: Math.round(accuracy), max_allowed_m: 50 }); } // B1b: Mock location detection if (is_mock_location === true) { log('warn', 'visit.checkin.mock_location', { psw_name, operator_id, ip: req.ip }); return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Location could not be verified. Please disable mock location apps and try again.', code: 'MOCK_LOCATION_DETECTED' }); } } // ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── const valid = await verifyPSW(psw_name, pin, operator_id); if (!valid) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid PIN' }); // EC-2 — Duplicate checkin prevention // First: check if same PSW + same client already has an in_progress visit today → resume it const today = torontoDate(); // Toronto local date (was UTC, caused day-rollover bug after 8 PM EST) const { data: sameClientVisit } = await supabase .from('visits') .select('id, time_in, checkin_time') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .eq('psw_name', psw_name) .eq('client_name', client_name) .eq('visit_date', today) .eq('status', 'in_progress') .maybeSingle(); if (sameClientVisit) { // Return existing visit so portal can resume — no new row created console.log(`EC-2: Duplicate checkin prevented, visit=${sameClientVisit.id}`); return res.json({ success: true, visit_id: sameClientVisit.id, time_in: sameClientVisit.time_in, checkin_time: sameClientVisit.checkin_time, resumed: true, message: 'Resuming existing visit' }); } // Second: check if PSW has a different client's visit still open — block with clear error const { data: otherVisit } = await supabase .from('visits') .select('id, client_name, checkin_time') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .eq('psw_name', psw_name) .eq('visit_date', today) .eq('status', 'in_progress') .maybeSingle(); if (otherVisit) { return res.status(409).json({ error: `You have an active visit open with ${otherVisit.client_name}. Check out before starting a new visit.`, visit_id: otherVisit.id, client_name: otherVisit.client_name, checkin_time: otherVisit.checkin_time }); } const now = new Date(); const timeIn = torontoHM(now); // HH:MM in Toronto time (was UTC, caused 4-hr skew) // Resolve client_id and check status — EC-4 blocks hospitalized const nameParts = client_name.trim().split(/\s+/); const { data: clientRow } = await supabase .from('clients') .select('id, family_email, family_contact_name, first_name, portal_slug, status, lat, lng') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .eq('first_name', nameParts[0]) .maybeSingle(); // EC-4 — block checkin if client is hospitalized or deceased ($9.7M NY OIG finding) if (clientRow?.status === 'hospitalized') { return res.status(409).json({ error: `${client_name} is currently marked as hospitalized. Visits cannot be logged for this client. Contact your coordinator before proceeding.`, client_status: 'hospitalized' }); } if (clientRow?.status === 'deceased') { return res.status(409).json({ error: `${client_name} is marked as deceased in the system. Contact your coordinator immediately.`, client_status: 'deceased' }); } // ── JOINT VISIT DETECTION ──────────────────────────────────────── // If another PSW already has an in_progress visit for this client today, // this is a joint visit. Link both rows with a shared joint_visit_id. const { data: existingJointVisit } = await supabase .from('visits') .select('id, joint_visit_id') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .eq('client_name', client_name) .eq('visit_date', today) .eq('status', 'in_progress') .neq('psw_name', psw_name) .maybeSingle(); let jointVisitId = null; if (existingJointVisit) { // Existing visit — use its joint_visit_id if set, otherwise generate one now jointVisitId = existingJointVisit.joint_visit_id || crypto.randomUUID(); // Patch the existing visit row with the joint_visit_id await supabase.from('visits') .update({ joint_visit_id: jointVisitId }) .eq('id', existingJointVisit.id); log('info', 'visit.checkin.joint', { psw_name, client_name, joint_visit_id: jointVisitId, operator_id }); } // ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── // ── TWO-PERSON VISIT WARNING ────────────────────────────────────── // If client requires two PSWs and this is a solo checkin (no joint partner), // log a warning and alert HQ. Checkin still proceeds — don't block care. if (!jointVisitId && clientRow?.requires_two_psw) { log('warn', 'visit.checkin.solo_on_two_psw_client', { psw_name, client_name, operator_id }); try { await supabase.from('system_logs').insert({ operator_id, event_type: 'visit.solo_on_two_psw_client', event_source: 'checkin', contact_name: client_name, status: 'warning', notes: `${psw_name} checked in solo for ${client_name} — this client requires 2 PSWs. Review scheduling.`, created_at: now.toISOString() }); } catch {} } // ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── const { data: visit, error: insertErr } = await supabase .from('visits') .insert({ operator_id, psw_name, client_name, client_id: clientRow?.id || null, visit_date: today, time_in: timeIn, checkin_time: now.toISOString(), status: 'in_progress', booking_id: booking_id || null, checkin_lat: latitude || null, checkin_lng: longitude || null, joint_visit_id: jointVisitId }) .select() .single(); if (insertErr) throw insertErr; // ── B2: GEOFENCE PASS / FAIL / OVERRIDE ──────────────────────────── if (latitude && longitude && clientRow?.lat && clientRow?.lng) { const toRad = d => d * Math.PI / 180; const R = 6371000; const dLat = toRad(clientRow.lat - latitude); const dLng = toRad(clientRow.lng - longitude); const a = Math.sin(dLat/2) * Math.sin(dLat/2) + Math.cos(toRad(latitude)) * Math.cos(toRad(clientRow.lat)) * Math.sin(dLng/2) * Math.sin(dLng/2); const distanceM = Math.round(R * 2 * Math.atan2(Math.sqrt(a), Math.sqrt(1-a))); // Configurable per-client radius (default 150m — generous for apartments/condo towers) const GEOFENCE_RADIUS_M = clientRow.geofence_radius_m || 150; const geofenceStatus = distanceM <= GEOFENCE_RADIUS_M ? 'pass' : 'fail'; // B2: Soft-block out-of-range without override reason if (geofenceStatus === 'fail' && !geofence_override_reason && !test_mode) { // Write fail status but return 409 so PSW portal can show override modal await supabase.from('visits') .update({ checkin_distance_m: distanceM, geofence_status: 'fail' }) .eq('id', visit.id); return res.status(409).json({ error: 'You appear to be outside the expected location.', code: 'GEOFENCE_FAIL', distance_m: distanceM, radius_m: GEOFENCE_RADIUS_M, requires_override: true, visit_id: visit.id // keep visit alive so override can patch it }); } // Pass or approved override — write final geofence fields const gfUpdate = { checkin_distance_m: distanceM, geofence_status: geofenceStatus === 'pass' ? 'pass' : 'override', checkin_accuracy_m: accuracy ? Math.round(accuracy) : null }; if (geofence_override_reason) { gfUpdate.geofence_override_reason = geofence_override_reason; gfUpdate.geofence_override_by = psw_name; log('info', 'visit.checkin.geofence_override', { psw_name, distance_m: distanceM, reason: geofence_override_reason, operator_id }); } await supabase.from('visits').update(gfUpdate).eq('id', visit.id); } else if (latitude && longitude) { // No client coords — write what we have, mark as unverified await supabase.from('visits') .update({ geofence_status: 'unverified', checkin_accuracy_m: accuracy ? Math.round(accuracy) : null }) .eq('id', visit.id); } // ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Notify family — PSW has arrived (BUILD 34: fire to all contacts, fall back to family_email) const checkinEmailPayload = { test_mode, subject: `${psw_name.split(' ')[0]} has arrived for ${clientRow?.first_name || nameParts[0]}'s visit`, html: `

    Proximity Care Services

    Visit Started

    Hi ${(clientRow?.family_contact_name || '').split(' ')[0] || 'Hello'},

    ${psw_name.split(' ')[0]} has checked in for ${clientRow?.first_name || nameParts[0]}'s visit at ${timeIn}.

    You will receive another email when the visit is complete, along with a care summary.

    Proximity Care Services Inc. · 647-382-8047

    ` }; if (clientRow?.portal_slug) { if (!test_mode) { const sent = await notifyFamilyContacts(clientRow.portal_slug, operator_id, 'checkin', checkinEmailPayload).catch(() => false); if (!sent && clientRow?.family_email) { await sendEmail({ ...checkinEmailPayload, to: clientRow.family_email }).catch(e => log('error', 'Checkin family notify failed', { error: e.message || String(e), trace_id: req?._traceId })); } } } else if (clientRow?.family_email && !test_mode) { await sendEmail({ ...checkinEmailPayload, to: clientRow.family_email }).catch(e => log('error', 'Checkin family notify failed', { error: e.message || String(e), trace_id: req?._traceId })); } // Web push — PSW has arrived if (clientRow?.id) { const pswFirst = psw_name.split(' ')[0]; const clientFirst = clientRow.first_name || nameParts[0]; if (!test_mode) sendPush('family', clientRow.id, { title: `${pswFirst} has arrived`, body: `Your caregiver just started today's visit.`, // C3: no time on lock screen url: clientRow.portal_slug ? `/family.html?c=${clientRow.portal_slug}` : '/family.html' }); } // Notify Lance — skip in test_mode (health console runs this every 30min) if (!test_mode) { await sendEmail({ to: 'healthcareproximity@gmail.com', subject: `✓ Check-in: ${psw_name} → ${client_name} at ${timeIn}`, html: `

    PROXIMITY HQ · CHECK-IN

    ${psw_name}

    Client: ${client_name}

    Time in: ${timeIn}

    Date: ${today}

    ${latitude && longitude ? `

    📍 View GPS Location

    ` : ''}
    ` }).catch(e => log('error', 'Checkin Lance notify failed', { error: e.message || String(e), trace_id: req?._traceId })); } // A1: Audit log — visit checkin auditLog(req, { action: 'checkin', entity_type: 'visit', entity_id: visit.id, actor_type: 'psw', actor_name: psw_name, changes: { visit_date: today, time_in: timeIn, client_name } }); res.json({ success: true, visit_id: visit.id, time_in: timeIn, checkin_time: visit.checkin_time }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'visit/checkin error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // POST /visit/checkout — PSW completes visit, fires AI summary + notifications app.post('/visit/checkout', async (req, res) => { try { const { psw_name, pin, operator_id = 'proximity-care', visit_id, tasks_completed, client_mood, incident_reported, incident_notes, observations, supply_needs, progress_note, test_mode } = req.body; if (!psw_name || !pin) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'psw_name and pin required' }); if (!visit_id) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'visit_id required' }); const valid = await verifyPSW(psw_name, pin, operator_id); if (!valid) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid PIN' }); // Fetch the in-progress visit const { data: visit, error: fetchErr } = await supabase .from('visits') .select('*') .eq('id', visit_id) .eq('psw_name', psw_name) .eq('status', 'in_progress') .single(); if (fetchErr || !visit) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Active visit not found' }); const now = new Date(); const timeOut = torontoHM(now); // Toronto time const checkinTime = new Date(visit.checkin_time); const wallClockMs = now - checkinTime; const hoursWorked = (wallClockMs / 3600000).toFixed(2); const minutesWorked = Math.round(wallClockMs / 60000); // Detect midnight-spanning visits: Supabase generated column uses ::time subtraction // which gives negative result when time_out < time_in (e.g. 23:00 in, 07:00 out). // Wall-clock ms from checkin_time is always correct regardless of day boundary. const timeInStr = visit.time_in || ''; const [inH, inM] = timeInStr.split(':').map(Number); const [outH, outM] = timeOut.split(':').map(Number); const timeInMins = (inH||0)*60 + (inM||0); const timeOutMins = (outH||0)*60 + (outM||0); const isMidnightSpanning = timeInStr && timeOutMins < timeInMins; // EC-1 — Sub-8-minute visit flag ($11.6M NY OIG finding) const force_checkout = req.body.force_checkout === true || req.body.force_checkout === 'true'; if (minutesWorked < 8 && !force_checkout) { return res.json({ success: false, sub_8_min: true, minutes_worked: minutesWorked, warning: `This visit is only ${minutesWorked} minute${minutesWorked !== 1 ? 's' : ''} long. Visits under 8 minutes will be flagged for review and may be blocked from invoicing. Are you sure you want to check out?` }); } // Build tasks string for AI const tasksArr = Array.isArray(tasks_completed) ? tasks_completed : []; const tasksStr = tasksArr.join(', ') || 'General care provided'; const allNotes = [observations, supply_needs].filter(Boolean).join(' | '); const incidentBool = incident_reported === true || incident_reported === 'true'; // Generate AI care summary (PHIPA: names anonymized via generateWithClaude) const summary = await generateWithClaude( `Write a brief 2-sentence professional care visit summary. Plain prose only — no markdown, no asterisks, no bold, no bullet points. PSW: ${psw_name}, Client: ${visit.client_name} Date: ${visit.visit_date}, Time: ${visit.time_in} to ${timeOut} (${hoursWorked} hours) Tasks completed: ${tasksStr} Client mood: ${client_mood || 'not recorded'} Incident reported: ${incidentBool ? 'YES — ' + (incident_notes || 'see notes') : 'No'} ${allNotes ? 'Additional notes: ' + allNotes : ''}`, 'You write concise professional care visit summaries for a home care agency. Be factual and brief. Never use markdown, asterisks, bold, or any formatting — plain prose only.', buildNameMap(visit.client_name, psw_name) ).catch(() => `${psw_name} completed a visit with ${visit.client_name} from ${visit.time_in} to ${timeOut}.`); // ── PHASE 5 — CARE SIGNAL DETECTION ── // Claude scans every checkout for 8 clinical risk signals let careSignals = null; try { // PHIPA: anonymize names before sending to Anthropic const signalNames = buildNameMap(visit.client_name, psw_name); const signalPromptRaw = `You are a clinical care signal detector for a home care agency. Analyze this visit and identify any care signals that need attention. Visit data: PSW: ${psw_name} Client: ${visit.client_name} Date: ${visit.visit_date}, Time: ${visit.time_in} to ${timeOut} Tasks completed: ${tasksStr} Client mood: ${client_mood || 'not recorded'} Observations: ${allNotes || 'none'} Incident reported: ${incidentBool ? 'YES — ' + (incident_notes || '') : 'No'} Visit summary: ${summary} Check for these 8 signal types: 1. fall_risk — any mention of falling, unsteady, balance issues, near-fall 2. pain — reports of pain, discomfort, grimacing, guarding 3. confusion — disorientation, memory issues, unusual behavior, agitation 4. medication_concern — missed meds, wrong dose, refusal, side effects 5. behavioral_change — significant change from baseline, withdrawal, aggression 6. appetite_hydration — not eating, not drinking, nausea, vomiting 7. skin_integrity — wounds, redness, pressure areas, skin breakdown 8. mobility_decline — increased difficulty moving, weakness, new limitations Return ONLY a JSON array. If no signals found, return []. Format: [{"type":"signal_type","severity":"HIGH"|"MED"|"LOW","detail":"one sentence describing the specific concern"}] HIGH = requires same-day action. MED = needs monitoring this week. LOW = note for care plan review.`; const { anonymized: signalPrompt } = phipaAnonymize(signalPromptRaw, signalNames); const signalRaw = await anthropic.messages.create({ model: 'claude-sonnet-4-20250514', max_tokens: 500, messages: [{ role: 'user', content: signalPrompt }] }); const signalText = (signalRaw.content[0]?.text || '').replace(/```json|```/g, '').trim(); const parsed = JSON.parse(signalText); if (Array.isArray(parsed) && parsed.length > 0) { careSignals = parsed; // Alert Lance immediately on HIGH severity signals const highSignals = parsed.filter(s => s.severity === 'HIGH'); if (highSignals.length > 0 && !test_mode) { await sendEmail({ to: 'healthcareproximity@gmail.com', subject: `🔴 Care Signal — ${visit.client_name} — ${visit.visit_date}`, html: `

    HIGH PRIORITY CARE SIGNAL

    ${visit.client_name}

    PSW: ${psw_name} · ${visit.visit_date}

    ${highSignals.map(s => `

    ${s.type.replace(/_/g,' ')}

    ${s.detail}

    `).join('')}
    ` }).catch(e => log('warn', 'async.silent.failed', { error: e?.message || String(e) })); } } } catch (signalErr) { log('error', 'Care signal detection error', { error: signalErr.message || String(signalErr), trace_id: req?._traceId }); } // Update visit row — includes new fields: meds_given, task_photos, voice_note_url const medsGiven = Array.isArray(req.body.meds_given) ? req.body.meds_given : (req.body.meds_given ? [req.body.meds_given] : []); const taskPhotos = Array.isArray(req.body.task_photos) ? req.body.task_photos : []; const voiceNoteUrl = req.body.voice_note_url || null; const { error: updateErr } = await supabase .from('visits') .update({ time_out: timeOut, checkout_time: now.toISOString(), tasks_completed: tasksArr, client_mood: client_mood || null, incident_reported: incidentBool, incident_notes: incident_notes || null, progress_note: progress_note || null, visit_summary: summary, meds_given: medsGiven.length ? medsGiven : null, task_photos: taskPhotos.length ? taskPhotos : null, voice_note_url: voiceNoteUrl, sub_8_min: minutesWorked < 8, status: 'completed', // Auto-set manual_hours_override for midnight-spanning visits to prevent negative hours_worked ...(isMidnightSpanning ? { manual_hours_override: parseFloat(hoursWorked) } : {}), care_signals: careSignals || null, updated_at: now.toISOString() }) .eq('id', visit_id); if (updateErr) throw updateErr; // Build 20 — short visit flag: if actual hours < 80% of scheduled duration try { const { data: relatedBooking } = await supabase .from('bookings').select('duration_minutes') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .eq('assigned_to', psw_name) .eq('scheduled_date', visit.visit_date) .eq('status', 'scheduled') .maybeSingle(); if (relatedBooking && relatedBooking.duration_minutes) { const scheduledHours = relatedBooking.duration_minutes / 60; const actualHours = parseFloat(hoursWorked); if (actualHours < scheduledHours * 0.8) { await supabase.from('visits').update({ short_visit: true }).eq('id', visit_id); if (test_mode) { log('info', 'checkout.short_visit.suppressed_test_mode', { psw_name, operator_id }); } else await sendEmail({ to: 'healthcareproximity@gmail.com', subject: `⚠ Short visit — ${psw_name} · ${visit.client_name} · ${actualHours}h of ${scheduledHours}h`, html: `

Care summary available in the portal.`, url: clientRow.portal_slug ? `/family.html?c=${clientRow.portal_slug}` : '/family.html' }); } // ── INSERT INCIDENT REPORT ROW ── if (incidentBool && incident_notes) { try { // Parse structured incident data from PSW portal // Format: "TYPE: 🤕 Fall / injury | description | 911 CALLED: Yes | FAMILY NOTIFIED: Yes" const iType = (() => { const m = (incident_notes || '').match(/TYPE:\s*([^|]+)/i); return m ? m[1].trim().replace(/^[^\w]+/, '') : 'General incident'; })(); const iDesc = (() => { const parts = (incident_notes || '').split('|'); // Description is usually the second part (after TYPE) const desc = parts.find((p, i) => i > 0 && !p.match(/^\s*(TYPE|911|FAMILY|COORDINATOR)/i)); return desc ? desc.trim() : incident_notes; })(); const called911 = /911 CALLED: Yes/i.test(incident_notes || ''); const familyNotif = /FAMILY NOTIFIED: Yes/i.test(incident_notes || ''); const coordNotif = /COORDINATOR NOTIFIED: Yes/i.test(incident_notes || ''); // Auto-severity: 911 called = HIGH, else MED const severity = called911 ? 'HIGH' : 'MED'; await supabase.from('incident_reports').insert({ operator_id, visit_id, client_name: visit.client_name, psw_name, visit_date: visit.visit_date, incident_type: iType, description: iDesc, called_911: called911, family_notified: familyNotif, coordinator_notified: coordNotif, severity, resolved: false, created_at: now.toISOString() }); log('info', 'incident.report.created', { operator_id, visit_id, psw_name, client: visit.client_name, severity }); } catch (incErr) { log('error', 'incident.report.insert.error', { error: incErr.message || String(incErr), trace_id: req?._traceId }); } } // ── INSERT MAR ENTRIES (from meds_given array) ── if (medsGiven.length > 0) { try { const marRows = medsGiven.map(medName => ({ operator_id, visit_id, client_name: visit.client_name, psw_name, visit_date: visit.visit_date, medication_name: medName, given: true, refused: false, time_given: timeOut, notes: null, created_at: now.toISOString() })); await supabase.from('mar_entries').insert(marRows); log('info', 'mar.auto.logged', { operator_id, visit_id, count: marRows.length }); } catch (marErr) { log('error', 'mar.auto.insert.error', { error: marErr.message || String(marErr), trace_id: req?._traceId }); } } // Alert Lance + auto-notify family on incident if (incidentBool) { // Notify family — gentle, no alarming details if (clientRow?.family_email) { const familyFirst = (clientRow.family_contact_name || '').split(' ')[0] || 'Hello'; const clientFirst = clientRow.first_name || visit.client_name.split(' ')[0]; if (!test_mode) await sendEmail({ to: clientRow.family_email, subject: `A note was logged during ${clientFirst}'s visit today`, html: `

    INCIDENT ALERT

    PSW: ${psw_name}
