    Lance Salazar
    Founder, Proximity Care Services

    Proximity Care Services Inc. · 647-382-8047

    ` }).catch(e => log('warn', 'async.silent.failed', { error: e?.message || String(e) })); } } // Low score (<=5) — alert Lance if (scoreNum <= 5) { const { data: client } = await supabase.from('clients').select('first_name, last_name').eq('id', client_id).single(); await sendEmail({ to: 'healthcareproximity@gmail.com', subject: `⚠ Low NPS score — ${client?.first_name || ''} ${client?.last_name || ''} — ${scoreNum}/10`, html: `

    NPS score of ${scoreNum}/10 received for client ${client?.first_name} ${client?.last_name}. Follow up today.

    ` }).catch(e => log('warn', 'async.silent.failed', { error: e?.message || String(e) })); try { await supabase.from('system_logs').insert({ operator_id: op, event_type: 'nps_low_score', event_source: '/family/nps-response', contact_name: client ? client.first_name + ' ' + client.last_name : '', payload: { score: scoreNum }, status: 'alert' }); } catch {} } // Redirect to a thank you page res.redirect('https://proximitycares.ca/family.html'); } catch (err) { log('error', 'nps-response error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).send('Error recording response'); } }); // ── CLIENT AVAILABILITY WINDOW CHECK ────────────────────────────── app.get('/hq/client-availability', async (req, res) => { try { const { operator_id = 'proximity-care', client_name, scheduled_time } = req.query; if (!client_name || !scheduled_time) return res.json({ success: true, warning: false }); const { data: client } = await supabase.from('clients').select('preferred_hours_start, preferred_hours_end, first_name, last_name').eq('operator_id', operator_id).ilike('first_name', client_name.split(' ')[0]).maybeSingle(); if (!client || !client.preferred_hours_start || !client.preferred_hours_end) return res.json({ success: true, warning: false }); const [sh, sm] = scheduled_time.split(':').map(Number); const [startH, startM] = client.preferred_hours_start.split(':').map(Number); const [endH, endM] = client.preferred_hours_end.split(':').map(Number); const scheduledMins = sh * 60 + sm; const startMins = startH * 60 + startM; const endMins = endH * 60 + endM; const outside = scheduledMins < startMins || scheduledMins > endMins; res.json({ success: true, warning: outside, preferred_start: client.preferred_hours_start, preferred_end: client.preferred_hours_end, message: outside ? `${client.first_name} prefers visits between ${client.preferred_hours_start} and ${client.preferred_hours_end}` : null }); } catch (err) { res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ── CLIENT INTAKE AI ───────────────────────────────────────────── // POST /hq/client-intake-ai // Accepts raw referral notes → Claude drafts full client profile app.post('/hq/client-intake-ai', async (req, res) => { try { const _hqSess = await validateHQToken(req); if (!_hqSess) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }); const { operator_id = 'proximity-care', referral_notes, family_name, client_name, family_email } = req.body; if (!referral_notes) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'referral_notes required' }); const promptRaw = `You are a care coordinator at a home care agency. A new client referral has come in. Based on the referral notes below, draft a complete client profile. Referral notes: ${referral_notes} ${family_name ? `Family contact: ${family_name}` : ''} ${client_name ? `Client name: ${client_name}` : ''} Return ONLY a valid JSON object with these exact fields (no markdown, no explanation): { "care_plan": "2-3 sentence care plan describing the client's needs and care approach", "goals": "1-2 sentences describing care goals", "daily_routine": "Brief description of daily routine and schedule preferences", "preferences": "Client preferences, communication style, personal notes", "medications": "List any medications mentioned, or empty string if none", "suggested_hours_per_week": number, "suggested_shift_length": number (hours), "notes": "Any red flags, special instructions, or coordinator notes", "urgency": "routine|urgent|immediate" }`; // PHIPA: anonymize client/family names before Anthropic const intakeNames = []; if (client_name) intakeNames.push({ real: client_name, code: 'CLIENT-A' }); if (family_name) intakeNames.push({ real: family_name, code: 'FAMILY-A' }); const { anonymized: intakePrompt } = phipaAnonymize(promptRaw, intakeNames); const response = await anthropic.messages.create({ model: 'claude-sonnet-4-20250514', max_tokens: 800, messages: [{ role: 'user', content: intakePrompt }] }); const raw = (response.content[0]?.text || '').replace(/```json|```/g, '').trim(); let profile; try { profile = JSON.parse(raw); } catch { throw new Error('Claude returned invalid JSON — try again'); } // Auto-generate portal slug from client name if (client_name) { const base = client_name.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, '-').replace(/^-|-$/g, ''); const { data: existing } = await supabase.from('clients').select('portal_slug').like('portal_slug', base + '%').eq('operator_id', operator_id); profile.suggested_slug = existing?.length ? `${base}-${existing.length + 1}` : base; } res.json({ success: true, profile }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'client-intake-ai error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ── PSW INTAKE AI ───────────────────────────────────────────────── // POST /hq/psw-intake-ai // Reads applicant record → Claude drafts PSW profile + match suggestions app.post('/hq/psw-intake-ai', async (req, res) => { try { const _hqSess = await validateHQToken(req); if (!_hqSess) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }); const { operator_id = 'proximity-care', applicant_id } = req.body; if (!applicant_id) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'applicant_id required' }); const { data: applicant } = await supabase .from('psw_applicants') .select('*') .eq('id', applicant_id) .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .maybeSingle(); if (!applicant) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Applicant not found' }); // Also get active clients for match suggestions const { data: clients } = await supabase .from('clients') .select('first_name, last_name, care_plan, goals, preferences') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .eq('status', 'active') .limit(10); const clientList = (clients || []).map(c => `${c.first_name} ${c.last_name}: ${(c.goals || c.care_plan || '').slice(0, 100)}` ).join('\n'); // PHIPA: anonymize applicant + client names before Anthropic const applicantFullName = applicant.full_name || applicant.first_name + ' ' + applicant.last_name; const pswIntakeNames = [{ real: applicantFullName, code: 'PSW-APPLICANT' }]; const clientCodeMap = {}; (clients || []).forEach((c, i) => { const fullName = `${c.first_name} ${c.last_name}`; const code = `CLIENT-${String.fromCharCode(65 + i)}`; pswIntakeNames.push({ real: fullName, code }); clientCodeMap[code] = fullName; }); const promptRaw = `You are an HR coordinator at a home care agency reviewing a PSW applicant after their interview. Applicant: ${applicantFullName} Experience: ${applicant.years_experience || 'Not specified'} years Certifications: ${applicant.certifications || 'Not specified'} Availability: ${applicant.availability || applicant.availability_json || 'Not specified'} Interview notes / application: ${applicant.notes || applicant.cover_letter || 'No notes recorded'} ${clientList ? `\nCurrent active clients:\n${clientList}` : ''} Return ONLY a valid JSON object (no markdown, no explanation): { "profile_summary": "2-3 sentence professional summary of this PSW for internal records", "strengths": "Key strengths based on their background", "suggested_shift_type": "days|evenings|nights|weekends|flexible", "suggested_client_matches": ["client name 1", "client name 2"] (from the active clients list, max 3, or empty array), "onboarding_notes": "Any notes for coordinator on onboarding this PSW", "readiness": "ready|needs_training|conditional", "readiness_note": "One sentence explaining readiness assessment" }`; const { anonymized: pswIntakePrompt, deAnonymize: deAnonPswIntake } = phipaAnonymize(promptRaw, pswIntakeNames); const response = await anthropic.messages.create({ model: 'claude-sonnet-4-20250514', max_tokens: 600, messages: [{ role: 'user', content: pswIntakePrompt }] }); // PHIPA: de-anonymize codes back to real names in response const raw = deAnonPswIntake((response.content[0]?.text || '').replace(/```json|```/g, '').trim()); let profile; try { profile = JSON.parse(raw); } catch { throw new Error('Claude returned invalid JSON — try again'); } profile.applicant_name = applicant.full_name || `${applicant.first_name || ''} ${applicant.last_name || ''}`.trim(); profile.applicant_email = applicant.email; res.json({ success: true, profile }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'psw-intake-ai error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ── AUTO MONTHLY INVOICE ────────────────────────────────────────── // POST /invoice/generate-pdf — S41 // Generates a professional invoice PDF for a client month // Returns: { success, pdf_base64, filename, invoice_number, total } app.post('/invoice/generate-pdf', async (req, res) => { try { const { operator_id = 'proximity-care', client_name, client_email, month, year, client_rate = 22, visits = [], invoice_number_override } = req.body; if (!client_name || !month || !year) { return res.status(400).json({ error: 'client_name, month, year required' }); } const monthNames = ['January','February','March','April','May','June','July','August','September','October','November','December']; const monthName = typeof month === 'number' ? monthNames[month - 1] : month; const yr = parseInt(year); // Load operator config for agency name const { data: opConfig } = await supabase.from('operator_config') .select('agency_name, owner_name, owner_email, owner_phone, province') .eq('operator_id', operator_id).maybeSingle(); const roundedHours = Math.round(totalHours * 100) / 100; const rate = parseFloat(client_rate); const subtotal = Math.round(roundedHours * rate * 100) / 100; const hst = Math.round(subtotal * 0 * 100) / 100; // PSW home care is HST exempt in Ontario const total = subtotal; // Invoice number: INV-YYYYMM-CLIENTINITIALS const initials = client_name.split(' ').map(w => w[0]||'').join('').toUpperCase().slice(0,3); const invoiceNum = invoice_number_override || `INV-${yr}${String(monthNames.indexOf(monthName)+1).padStart(2,'0')}-${initials}`; const invoiceDate = new Date().toLocaleDateString('en-CA', { timeZone: 'America/Toronto' }); const dueDate = new Date(yr, monthNames.indexOf(monthName) + 1, 15).toLocaleDateString('en-CA'); const pdfBuffer = await new Promise((resolve, reject) => { const PDFDoc = require('pdfkit'); const doc = new PDFDoc({ margin: 0, size: 'A4' }); const chunks = []; doc.on('data', c => chunks.push(c)); doc.on('end', () => resolve(Buffer.concat(chunks))); doc.on('error', reject); const W = 595, H = 842; const L = 48, R = W - 48; // ── HEADER BAND ── doc.rect(0, 0, W, 96).fill('#1a1a18'); doc.fillColor('#faf8f4').font('Helvetica-Bold').fontSize(15) .text(agencyName.toUpperCase(), L, 22); doc.fillColor('#a8bfc4').font('Helvetica').fontSize(9) .text('7075 Rexwood Rd, Mississauga, ON · ' + ownerPhone + ' · proximitycares.ca', L, 40); doc.fillColor('#6b6b68').font('Helvetica').fontSize(8).text('INVOICE DATE', metaX, 50, { width: 160, align: 'right', characterSpacing: 0.5 }); doc.fillColor('#faf8f4').font('Helvetica').fontSize(10).text(invoiceDate, metaX, 62, { width: 160, align: 'right' }); doc.fillColor('#6b6b68').font('Helvetica').fontSize(8).text('DUE DATE', metaX, 76, { width: 160, align: 'right', characterSpacing: 0.5 }); doc.fillColor('#b87010').font('Helvetica-Bold').fontSize(10).text(dueDate, metaX, 86, { width: 160, align: 'right' }); // ── BILLED TO ── const billY = 112; doc.fillColor('#6b6b68').font('Helvetica').fontSize(8).text('BILLED TO', L, billY, { characterSpacing: 0.8 }); doc.fillColor('#1a1a18').font('Helvetica-Bold').fontSize(13).text(client_name, L, billY + 14); if (client_email) { doc.fillColor('#6b6b68').font('Helvetica').fontSize(10).text(client_email, L, billY + 30); } // Bill from (right side) doc.fillColor('#6b6b68').font('Helvetica').fontSize(8).text('FROM', R - 200, billY, { width: 200, align: 'right', characterSpacing: 0.8 }); doc.fillColor('#1a1a18').font('Helvetica-Bold').fontSize(11).text(agencyName, R - 200, billY + 14, { width: 200, align: 'right' }); doc.fillColor('#6b6b68').font('Helvetica').fontSize(10).text(ownerName, R - 200, billY + 30, { width: 200, align: 'right' }); // ── DIVIDER ── const divY = client_email ? billY + 52 : billY + 44; doc.rect(L, divY, R - L, 0.5).fill('#e8e4dc'); // ── SERVICE PERIOD BANNER ── const periodY = divY + 12; doc.rect(L, periodY, R - L, 28).fill('#f2ede4'); doc.fillColor('#1e7d96').font('Helvetica-Bold').fontSize(10) .text('CARE SERVICES — ' + monthName.toUpperCase() + ' ' + yr, L + 12, periodY + 9); doc.fillColor('#6b6b68').font('Helvetica').fontSize(9) .text('Personal Support Worker Home Care', R - 260, periodY + 9, { width: 248, align: 'right' }); // ── VISIT TABLE ── const tableY = periodY + 40; // Header row doc.rect(L, tableY, R - L, 22).fill('#1a1a18'); doc.fillColor('#b87010').font('Helvetica-Bold').fontSize(8); const cols = [ [L + 8, 'DATE'], [L + 88, 'PSW'], [L + 230, 'TIME IN'], [L + 290, 'TIME OUT'], [L + 360, 'HOURS'], [L + 400, 'RATE'], [R - 56, 'AMOUNT'] ]; cols.forEach(([x, h]) => doc.text(h, x, tableY + 7)); let ry = tableY + 24; doc.font('Helvetica').fontSize(9); const fmtT = t => t ? String(t).slice(0,5) : '—'; billedVisits.forEach((v, i) => { if (ry > H - 140) { doc.addPage(); ry = 60; } const rowH = 18; if (i % 2 === 0) doc.rect(L, ry, R - L, rowH).fill('#faf8f4'); else doc.rect(L, ry, R - L, rowH).fill('#f5f0e8'); const hrs = parseFloat(v.manual_hours_override ?? v.hours_worked ?? 0); const amt = Math.round(hrs * rate * 100) / 100; doc.fillColor('#1a1a18').text(v.visit_date || '—', L + 8, ry + 4); doc.fillColor('#444').text((v.psw_name || '—').split(' ')[0], L + 88, ry + 4); doc.text(fmtT(v.time_in), L + 230, ry + 4); doc.text(fmtT(v.time_out), L + 290, ry + 4); doc.fillColor('#1e7d96').font('Helvetica-Bold').text(hrs.toFixed(2) + 'h', L + 360, ry + 4); doc.fillColor('#444').font('Helvetica').text('$' + rate.toFixed(2), L + 400, ry + 4); doc.fillColor('#1a1a18').font('Helvetica-Bold').text('$' + amt.toFixed(2), R - 56, ry + 4, { width: 50, align: 'right' }); doc.font('Helvetica'); ry += rowH; }); // ── TOTALS ── const totY = ry + 12; doc.rect(L, totY, R - L, 0.5).fill('#e8e4dc'); // Total hours row doc.rect(R - 200, totY + 8, 200, 20).fill('#f2ede4'); doc.fillColor('#6b6b68').font('Helvetica').fontSize(9).text('TOTAL HOURS', R - 195, totY + 13); doc.fillColor('#1e7d96').font('Helvetica-Bold').fontSize(11) .text(roundedHours.toFixed(2) + 'h', R - 60, totY + 11, { width: 54, align: 'right' }); // Subtotal doc.fillColor('#6b6b68').font('Helvetica').fontSize(9).text('SUBTOTAL', R - 195, totY + 36); doc.fillColor('#1a1a18').font('Helvetica-Bold').fontSize(11) .text('$' + subtotal.toFixed(2), R - 60, totY + 34, { width: 54, align: 'right' }); // HST exempt line doc.fillColor('#aaa').font('Helvetica').fontSize(8) .text('HST (Personal Support Services — Exempt)', R - 195, totY + 54); doc.fillColor('#aaa').fontSize(8).text('$0.00', R - 60, totY + 54, { width: 54, align: 'right' }); // TOTAL DUE box const totalBoxY = totY + 70; doc.rect(R - 200, totalBoxY, 200, 36).fill('#1a1a18'); doc.fillColor('#b87010').font('Helvetica-Bold').fontSize(10) .text('TOTAL DUE', R - 195, totalBoxY + 6); doc.fillColor('#faf8f4').font('Helvetica-Bold').fontSize(18) .text('$' + total.toFixed(2), R - 60, totalBoxY + 4, { width: 54, align: 'right' }); // ── PAYMENT INSTRUCTIONS ── const payY = totalBoxY + 50; doc.rect(L, payY, R - L - 210, 68).fill('#f2ede4'); doc.fillColor('#6b6b68').font('Helvetica').fontSize(8) .text('PAYMENT METHOD', L + 12, payY + 10, { characterSpacing: 0.5 }); doc.fillColor('#1a1a18').font('Helvetica-Bold').fontSize(12) .text('E-Transfer', L + 12, payY + 22); doc.fillColor('#1e7d96').font('Helvetica-Bold').fontSize(11) .text('lancesalazar56@yahoo.ca', L + 12, payY + 38); doc.fillColor('#6b6b68').font('Helvetica').fontSize(9) .text('Reference: ' + client_name.split(' ')[0] + ' ' + monthName, L + 12, payY + 54); // Due date reminder doc.rect(L, payY + 78, R - L - 210, 26).fill('#fff8ee'); doc.rect(L, payY + 78, 3, 26).fill('#b87010'); doc.fillColor('#b87010').font('Helvetica-Bold').fontSize(9) .text('Payment due by ' + dueDate + '. Questions? Call ' + ownerPhone, L + 10, payY + 85); // ── FOOTER ── doc.rect(0, H - 32, W, 32).fill('#1a1a18'); doc.fillColor('#6b6b68').font('Helvetica').fontSize(8) .text(agencyName + ' · 7075 Rexwood Rd, Mississauga, ON · ' + ownerPhone + ' · proximitycares.ca', L, H - 20); doc.fillColor('#444').fontSize(8) .text('Thank you for trusting us with your care.', R - 220, H - 20, { width: 220, align: 'right' }); doc.end(); }); const filename = `Proximity-Invoice-${invoiceNum}.pdf`; log('info', 'invoice.pdf.generated', { operator_id, client_name, invoice_number: invoiceNum, total }); res.json({ success: true, pdf_base64: pdfBuffer.toString('base64'), filename, invoice_number: invoiceNum, total, hours: roundedHours }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'invoice/generate-pdf error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // POST /invoice/auto-monthly // Generates invoices for all active clients for a given month (defaults to last month) app.post('/invoice/auto-monthly', async (req, res) => { try { const { operator_id = 'proximity-care', month: reqMonth, year: reqYear, dry_run, force } = req.body; const now = new Date(); // DATE GATE — only run on day 1 or 2 of the month unless forced or manually specifying month/year // Prevents daily emails when cron fires every 24h via setInterval const todayDay = parseInt(new Date().toLocaleDateString('en-CA', {timeZone:'America/Toronto'}).split('-')[2]); if (!reqMonth && !reqYear && !force && todayDay > 2) { return res.json({ success: true, message: `Date gate: day ${todayDay} — auto-invoice only runs on day 1-2`, invoices_generated: 0 }); } // DRY RUN — audit/test calls should never send emails if (dry_run) { return res.json({ success: true, message: 'dry_run — no invoices sent', invoices_generated: 0 }); } const targetDate = reqMonth && reqYear ? new Date(parseInt(reqYear), parseInt(reqMonth) - 1, 1) : new Date(now.getFullYear(), now.getMonth() - 1, 1); const month = targetDate.getMonth(); const year = targetDate.getFullYear(); const monthNames = ['January','February','March','April','May','June','July','August','September','October','November','December']; const monthName = monthNames[month]; const startDate = `${year}-${String(month + 1).padStart(2,'0')}-01`; const endDate = new Date(year, month + 1, 0).toISOString().slice(0, 10); console.log(`Auto-invoice: ${monthName} ${year} (${startDate} to ${endDate})`); const { data: clients } = await supabase .from('clients') .select('id, first_name, last_name, family_email, assigned_psw, client_rate, psw_rate, portal_slug') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .eq('status', 'active'); if (!clients || clients.length === 0) { return res.json({ success: true, message: 'No active clients', invoices_generated: 0 }); } // BUILD 28 — read operator default rates so fallback is per-operator not global const { data: opConfig } = await supabase .from('operator_config') .select('default_client_rate, default_psw_rate') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .maybeSingle(); const opClientRate = parseFloat(opConfig?.default_client_rate) || 22; const opPswRate = parseFloat(opConfig?.default_psw_rate) || 19; const results = []; for (const client of clients) { const clientName = `${client.first_name} ${client.last_name}`; const pswName = client.assigned_psw; if (!pswName) { results.push({ client: clientName, skipped: 'No assigned PSW' }); continue; } const { data: visits } = await supabase .from('visits') .select('*') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .eq('client_name', clientName) .in('status', ['complete','completed']) .eq('verified', true) .gte('visit_date', startDate) .lte('visit_date', endDate) .order('visit_date', { ascending: true }); if (!visits || visits.length === 0) { results.push({ client: clientName, skipped: 'No visits this month' }); continue; } // Per-client rate, fall back to operator default (not hardcoded global) const clientRate = parseFloat(client.client_rate) || opClientRate; const pswRate = parseFloat(client.psw_rate) || opPswRate; // Joint visit billing dedup — group by joint_visit_id, take max hours per group // Prevents double-billing when 2 PSWs both log hours for the same visit const billingVisits = (() => { const groups = {}; const order = []; visits.forEach(v => { const key = v.joint_visit_id || ('solo_' + v.id); if (!groups[key]) { groups[key] = []; order.push(key); } groups[key].push(v); }); return order.map(key => { const g = groups[key]; if (g.length === 1) return g[0]; // Joint visit — prefer manual_hours_override over generated hours_worked return g.reduce((best, v) => { const vH = parseFloat(v.manual_hours_override ?? v.hours_worked ?? 0); const bH = parseFloat(best.manual_hours_override ?? best.hours_worked ?? 0); return vH > bH ? v : best; }, g[0]); }); })(); // BILLING: always prefer manual_hours_override — hours_worked is GENERATED and ignores HQ edits const totalHours = billingVisits.reduce((sum, v) => sum + parseFloat(v.manual_hours_override ?? v.hours_worked ?? 0), 0); const roundedHours = Math.round(totalHours * 100) / 100; const clientTotal = Math.round(roundedHours * clientRate * 100) / 100; const { data: pswRow } = await supabase .from('psws') .select('email') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .eq('full_name', pswName) .maybeSingle(); try { const invoiceRes = await fetch('https://proximity-agent-production.up.railway.app/invoice/generate', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ operator_id, client_name: clientName, client_email: client.family_email, psw_name: pswName, psw_email: pswRow?.email || '', month: monthName, year: String(year), client_rate: clientRate, psw_rate: pswRate }) }); const invoiceData = await invoiceRes.json(); if (invoiceRes.ok) { results.push({ client: clientName, success: true, hours: roundedHours, client_total: clientTotal }); console.log(`Auto-invoice: ${clientName} — ${roundedHours}h — $${clientTotal}`); // ── MONTHLY CARE REPORT TO FAMILY ── if (client.family_email) { try { const clientFirst = client.first_name || clientName.split(' ')[0]; const pswFirst = pswName ? pswName.split(' ')[0] : 'your PSW'; const portalUrl = client.portal_slug ? `https://proximitycares.ca/family.html?c=${client.portal_slug}` : 'https://proximitycares.ca'; // Mood tally const moods = visits.map(v => v.client_mood).filter(Boolean); const moodCount = {}; moods.forEach(m => { moodCount[m] = (moodCount[m]||0)+1; }); const topMood = Object.entries(moodCount).sort((a,b)=>b[1]-a[1])[0]; const moodLine = topMood ? `${clientFirst} was most often feeling ${topMood[0]} this month.` : ''; // Task frequency const allTasks = []; visits.forEach(v => { const t = Array.isArray(v.tasks_completed) ? v.tasks_completed : []; allTasks.push(...t); }); const taskCount = {}; allTasks.forEach(t => { if(t) taskCount[t] = (taskCount[t]||0)+1; Math.round(parseFloat(manual_total) * 100) / 100 : Math.round(hours * rate * 100) / 100; periodStr = period_label || new Date().toLocaleString('en-CA', { month: 'long', year: 'numeric', timeZone: 'America/Toronto' }); } else { // Auto mode — pull from visits table const m = parseInt(month) || new Date().getMonth() + 1; const y = parseInt(year) || new Date().getFullYear(); periodStr = new Date(y, m-1).toLocaleString('en-CA', { month: 'long', year: 'numeric' }); const startDate = `${y}-${String(m).padStart(2,'0')}-01`; const endDate = new Date(y, m, 0).toISOString().split('T')[0]; const { data: v } = await supabase.from('visits') .select('visit_date,time_in,time_out,hours_worked,manual_hours_override,client_name') .eq('operator_id', operator_id).eq('psw_name', psw_name) .gte('visit_date', startDate).lte('visit_date', endDate) .in('status', ['completed', 'complete']) .order('visit_date', { ascending: true }); if (!v || !v.length) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'No completed visits found for this period' }); visits = v; rate = parseFloat(psw.psw_rate) || 19; // AUTHORITATIVE: manual_hours_override ?? hours_worked — never raw GPS only hours = Math.round(v.reduce((s, x) => s + parseFloat(x.manual_hours_override ?? x.hours_worked ?? 0), 0) * 100) / 100; total = Math.round(hours * rate * 100) / 100; } // Build visit rows for PDF — use manual_hours_override as authoritative const fmtTime = t => t ? const today = now.split('T')[0]; const { data: upcomingBookings } = await supabase .from('bookings').select('id, assigned_to, scheduled_date, scheduled_time') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .eq('client_name', clientName) .eq('status', 'scheduled') .gte('scheduled_date', today); if (upcomingBookings && upcomingBookings.length > 0) { await supabase.from('bookings') .update({ status: 'cancelled', cancelled_at: now, cancelled_by: changed_by, cancellation_reason: `Client status changed to ${status}` }) .in('id', upcomingBookings.map(b => b.id)); Do not proceed to this client's home. We will contact you with updates.` : `Your upcoming shifts with ${clientName} have been placed on hold. We will contact you with updates.`; await sendEmail({ to: pswRow.email, subject: subj, html: `

    Hi ${pswName.split(' ')[0]},

    ${body} Questions? Call Lance at 647-382-8047.

    Proximity Care Services Inc.

    ` }).catch(e => log('warn', 'async.silent.failed', { error: e?.message || String(e) })); } } } if (client.family_email) { const familySubj = status === 'hospitalized' ? `Your care coordinator has been notified — ${client.first_name}` : `Update regarding ${client.first_name}'s care`; const familyBody = status === 'hospitalized' ? `We have been notified that ${client.first_name} has been hospitalized. All scheduled visits have been suspended. Our team is here if you need anything — call 647-382-8047.` : `${status_reason || 'A temporary hold has been placed on upcoming visits.'} Please call us at 647-382-8047 if you have any questions.`; await sendEmail({ to: client.family_email, subject: familySubj, html: `

    Hi,

    ${familyBody}

    Proximity Care Services Inc. · 647-382-8047

    ` }).catch(e => log('warn', 'async.silent.failed', { error: e?.message || String(e) })); } } try { await supabase.from('system_logs').insert({ operator_id, event_type: 'client_status_change', event_source: '/hq/client/:slug/status', contact_name: `${client.first_name} ${client.last_name}`, payload: { status, status_reason, changed_by }, status: 'success', created_at: now }); } catch (_) {} console.log(`client/status: ${slug} → ${status} by ${changed_by}`); res.json({ success: true, slug, status }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'PATCH /hq/client/:slug/status error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── // BUILD 34 — MULTIPLE FAMILY CONTACTS // ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── // Helper — get all contacts for a client slug async function getFamilyContacts(client_slug, operator_id) { const { data } = await supabase .from('family_contacts') .select('*') .eq('client_slug', client_slug) .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .order('priority_order', { ascending: true }); return data || []; } // Helper — send to all relevant contacts async function notifyFamilyContacts(client_slug, operator_id, notifyType, emailPayload) { // notifyType: 'checkin' | 'summary' | 'missed_visit' const contacts = await getFamilyContacts(client_slug, operator_id); const field = `receives_${notifyType}`; const targets = contacts.filter(c => c[field] !== false && c.email); if (!targets.length) return false; // fall back to caller using family_email for (const contact of targets) { const personalised = { ...emailPayload, to: emailPayload.test_mode ? 'healthcareproximity@gmail.com' : contact.email, html: emailPayload.html.replace(/Hi [^,]+,/, `Hi ${contact.name.split(' ')[0]},`) }; await sendEmail(personalised).catch(e => log('error', 'family_contacts.notify.failed', { email: contact.email, error: e.message })); } }); // POST /hq/shift-reminder — Build 22 — nightly cron, fires shift reminders for tomorrow's bookings app.post('/hq/shift-reminder', async (req, res) => { try { const { operator_id = 'proximity-care', dry_run = false } = req.body; const { error } = await supabase.from('mar_entries').insert(rows); if (error) throw error; log('info', 'mar.logged', { operator_id, visit_id, client_name, psw_name, count: rows.length }); res.json({ success: true, inserted: rows.length }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'mar.error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // GET /hq/mar — Medication Administration Record log for HQ // Returns MAR entries for a client or date range // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ app.get('/hq/mar', async (req, res) => { try { const { operator_id = 'proximity-care', client_name, from_date, to_date, psw_name } = req.query; let q = supabase.from('mar_entries') .select('*') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .order('visit_date', { ascending: false }) .order('created_at', { ascending: false }) .limit(200); if (client_name) q = q.eq('client_name', client_name); // Aggregate: per-visit summary const byVisit = {}; (data || []).forEach(m => { if (!byVisit[m.visit_id]) byVisit[m.visit_id] = { visit_id: m.visit_id, client_name: m.client_name, psw_name: m.psw_name, visit_date: m.visit_date, meds: [] }; res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // POST /hq/incidents/:id/resolve — Mark incident resolved // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ app.post('/hq/incidents/:id/resolve', async (req, res) => { try { const { id } = req.params; res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // GET /hq/incidents — Open/all incident reports for HQ // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ app.get('/hq/incidents', async (req, res) => { try { const { operator_id = 'proximity-care', resolved, client_name, from_date, to_date } = req.query; } catch (err) { log('error', 'hq.incidents.error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // POST /visit/en-route — PSW tapped Sign In, notify family they're on the way // Fire-and-forget before GPS resolves. No visit row created. // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ app.post('/visit/en-route', async (req, res) => { try { const { psw_name, pin, operator_id = 'proximity-care', client_name, test_mode } = req.body; if (!psw_name || !pin || !client_name) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'psw_name, pin, client_name required' }); const valid = await verifyPSW(psw_name, pin, operator_id); if (!valid) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid PIN' }); const pswFirst = psw_name.split(' ')[0]; const nameParts = client_name.trim().split(/\s+/); const { data: clientRow } = await supabase .from('clients') .select('id, family_email, family_contact_name, first_name, portal_slug') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .eq('first_name', nameParts[0]) .maybeSingle(); if (!clientRow) return res.json({ success: true, sent: false, note: 'Client not found' }); const clientFirst = clientRow.first_name || nameParts[0]; const greeting = (clientRow.family_contact_name || '').split(' ')[0] || 'Hello'; const eta = new Date(Date.now() + 15 * 60000); const etaStr = eta.toLocaleTimeString('en-CA', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit', hour12: true, timeZone: 'America/Toronto' }); const payload = { test_mode, subject: `${pswFirst} is on the way to ${clientFirst}`, html: `

    Proximity Care Services

    PSW En Route

    Hi ${greeting},

    ${pswFirst} is on the way and will arrive for ${clientFirst}'s visit shortly — estimated around ${etaStr}.

    You will receive another notification when ${pswFirst} arrives and again when the visit is complete.

    Proximity Care Services Inc. · 647-382-8047

    ` }; let sent = false; if (clientRow.portal_slug && !test_mode) { sent = await notifyFamilyContacts(clientRow.portal_slug, operator_id, 'en_route', payload).catch(() => false); if (!sent && clientRow.family_email) { await sendEmail({ ...payload, to: clientRow.family_email }).catch(e => log('warn', 'async.silent.failed', { error: e?.message || String(e) })); sent = true; } } else if (clientRow.family_email && !test_mode) { await sendEmail({ ...payload, to: clientRow.family_email }).catch(e => log('warn', 'async.silent.failed', { error: e?.message || String(e) })); sent = true; } else if (test_mode) { await sendEmail({ ...payload, to: 'healthcareproximity@gmail.com' }).catch(e => log('warn', 'async.silent.failed', { error: e?.message || String(e) })); sent = true; } if (clientRow.id) { sendPush('family', clientRow.id, { title: `${pswFirst} is on the way`, body: 'Your caregiver is heading over now.', // C3: no ETA or address on lock screen url: clientRow.portal_slug ? `/family.html?c=${clientRow.portal_slug}` : '/family.html' }); } log('info', 'visit.en-route.sent', { operator_id, psw_name, client_name, sent }); res.json({ success: true, sent, eta: etaStr }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'visit.en-route.error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // POST /visit/geofence-check — Check PSW GPS vs client address // Returns distance_m + within_range + auto_checkin_eligible // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ app.post('/visit/geofence-check', async (req, res) => { try { const { psw_name, pin, operator_id = 'proximity-care', client_name, latitude, longitude } = req.body; if (!psw_name || !pin) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'psw_name and pin required' }); if (!latitude || !longitude) return res.json({ success: true, within_range: null, distance_m: null, note: 'No GPS coordinates provided' }); const valid = await verifyPSW(psw_name, pin, operator_id); if (!valid) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid PIN' }); const nameParts = (client_name || '').trim().split(/\s+/); const { data: clientRow } = await supabase .from('clients') .select('lat, lng, first_name') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .eq('first_name', nameParts[0]) .maybeSingle(); if (!clientRow?.lat || !clientRow?.lng) { return res.json({ success: true, within_range: null, distance_m: null, note: 'Client address not geocoded — geofence not available' }); } const toRad = d => d * Math.PI / 180; const R = 6371000; const dLat = toRad(clientRow.lat - latitude); const dLng = toRad(clientRow.lng - longitude); const a = Math.sin(dLat/2)**2 + Math.cos(toRad(latitude)) * Math.cos(toRad(clientRow.lat)) * Math.sin(dLng/2)**2; const distanceM = Math.round(R * 2 * Math.atan2(Math.sqrt(a), Math.sqrt(1-a))); const AUTO_CHECKIN_RADIUS = 200; // metres const WARN_RADIUS = 500; const within_range = distanceM <= WARN_RADIUS; const auto_checkin_eligible = distanceM <= AUTO_CHECKIN_RADIUS; log('info', 'geofence.check', { operator_id, psw_name, client_name, distance_m: distanceM, within_range, auto_checkin_eligible }); res.json({ success: true, distance_m: distanceM, within_range, auto_checkin_eligible, warn_radius: WARN_RADIUS, auto_radius: AUTO_CHECKIN_RADIUS }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'geofence.check.error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // GET /hq/gps-exceptions — Visits with GPS anomalies for HQ dashboard // Returns: out-of-range checkins + missing GPS where client has coords // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ app.get('/hq/gps-exceptions', async (req, res) => { try { const { operator_id = 'proximity-care', threshold_m = 500, days = 14 } = req.query; const since = new Date(Date.now() - parseInt(days) * 86400000).toISOString().slice(0, 10); // Out-of-range checkins const { data: outOfRange, error: oorErr } = await supabase .from('visits') .select('id, psw_name, client_name, visit_date, time_in, checkin_distance_m, checkin_lat, checkin_lng, entry_type') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .gte('visit_date', since) .in('status', ['complete','completed']) .gt('checkin_distance_m', parseInt(threshold_m)) .order('visit_date', { ascending: false }) .limit(50); if (oorErr) throw oorErr; // Missing GPS — visits with no checkin coords where client HAS coords const { data: clientsWithCoords } = await supabase .from('clients') .select('first_name, last_name') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .not('lat', 'is', null) .not('lng', 'is', null); const clientNamesWithCoords = (clientsWithCoords || []).map(c => `${c.first_name} ${c.last_name}`.trim()); const { data: missingGPS } = await supabase .from('visits') .select('id, psw_name, client_name, visit_date, time_in, entry_type') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .gte('visit_date', since) .in('status', ['complete','completed']) .is('checkin_lat', null) .order('visit_date', { ascending: false }) .limit(50); const missingFiltered = (missingGPS || []).filter(v => clientNamesWithCoords.some(n => n.toLowerCase().includes((v.client_name||'').split(' ')[0].toLowerCase())) ); // Group out-of-range by PSW const byPSW = {}; (outOfRange || []).forEach(v => { if (!byPSW[v.psw_name]) byPSW[v.psw_name] = { psw_name: v.psw_name, exceptions: [] }; byPSW[v.psw_name].exceptions.push(v); }); res.json({ success: true, out_of_range: outOfRange || [], missing_gps: missingFiltered, by_psw: Object.values(byPSW), threshold_m: parseInt(threshold_m), days: parseInt(days), total_exceptions: (outOfRange?.length || 0) + missingFiltered.length }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'hq.gps-exceptions.error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // POST /visit/vitals — Log vitals for a visit // Auto-flags if BP >140/90, O2 <95, temp >38.5 // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ app.post('/visit/vitals', async (req, res) => { try { const { psw_name, pin, operator_id = 'proximity-care', visit_id, client_name, blood_pressure_systolic, blood_pressure_diastolic, pulse, temperature, oxygen_saturation, notes } = req.body; if (!psw_name || !pin) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'psw_name and pin required' }); if (!visit_id) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'visit_id required' }); const valid = await verifyPSW(psw_name, pin, operator_id); if (!valid) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid PIN' }); // Auto-flag out of range readings const flags = []; if (blood_pressure_systolic > 140) flags.push('BP systolic elevated: ' + blood_pressure_systolic); if (blood_pressure_diastolic > 90) flags.push('BP diastolic elevated: ' + blood_pressure_diastolic); if (oxygen_saturation < 95) flags.push('O2 saturation low: ' + oxygen_saturation + '%'); if (temperature > 38.5) flags.push('Temperature elevated: ' + temperature + '°C'); const flagged = flags.length > 0; const { data, error } = await supabase.from('vitals').insert({ operator_id, visit_id, client_name: client_name || null, psw_name, visit_date: new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10), blood_pressure_systolic: blood_pressure_systolic || null, blood_pressure_diastolic: blood_pressure_diastolic || null, pulse: pulse || null, temperature: temperature || null, oxygen_saturation: oxygen_saturation || null, notes: notes || null, flagged, created_at: new Date().toISOString() }).select().single(); if (error) throw error; if (flagged) { log('warn', 'vitals.flagged', { operator_id, visit_id, client_name, psw_name, flags }); } else { log('info', 'vitals.logged', { operator_id, visit_id, client_name, psw_name }); } res.json({ success: true, flagged, flag_reasons: flags, vitals_id: data?.id }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'vitals.error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // GET /hq/vitals — Vitals history for HQ dashboard // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ app.get('/hq/vitals', async (req, res) => { try { const { operator_id = 'proximity-care', client_name, from_date, to_date, flagged_only } = req.query; let q = supabase.from('vitals').select('*').eq('operator_id', operator_id) .order('visit_date', { ascending: false }).order('created_at', { ascending: false }).limit(200); if (client_name) q = q.eq('client_name', client_name); if (from_date) q = q.gte('visit_date', from_date); if (to_date) q = q.lte('visit_date', to_date); if (flagged_only === 'true') q = q.eq('flagged', true); const { data, error } = await q; if (error) throw error; const flaggedCount = (data||[]).filter(v => v.flagged).length; res.json({ success: true, vitals: data || [], total: data?.length || 0, flagged_count: flaggedCount }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'hq.vitals.error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // POST /visit/handoff — Log handoff note from outgoing to incoming PSW // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ app.post('/visit/handoff', async (req, res) => { try { const { psw_name, pin, operator_id = 'proximity-care', visit_id, client_name, to_psw, note } = req.body; if (!psw_name || !pin) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'psw_name and pin required' }); if (!note) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'note required' }); const valid = await verifyPSW(psw_name, pin, operator_id); if (!valid) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid PIN' }); const { error } = await supabase.from('handoff_notes').insert({ operator_id, visit_id: visit_id || null, client_name: client_name || null, from_psw: psw_name, to_psw: to_psw || null, note, read: false, created_at: new Date().toISOString() }); if (error) throw error; // Notify receiving PSW if specified if (to_psw) { const msg = `Handoff note from ${psw_name} for ${client_name || 'your next visit'}: ${note.slice(0,100)}${note.length>100?'…':''}`; try { await supabase.from('psw_notes').insert({ operator_id, psw_name: to_psw, sender: 'system', message: msg, read: false, created_at: new Date().toISOString() }); } catch {} } log('info', 'handoff.logged', { operator_id, from_psw: psw_name, to_psw, client_name }); res.json({ success: true, notified: !!to_psw }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'handoff.error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // GET /psw/handoff-notes — Unread handoff notes for a PSW // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ app.get('/psw/handoff-notes', async (req, res) => { try { const { psw_name, pin, operator_id = 'proximity-care' } = req.query; if (!psw_name || !pin) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'psw_name and pin required' }); const valid = await verifyPSW(psw_name, pin, operator_id); if (!valid) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid PIN' }); const { data, error } = await supabase.from('handoff_notes') .select('*').eq('operator_id', operator_id).eq('to_psw', psw_name) .order('created_at', { ascending: false }).limit(20); if (error) throw error; // Mark as read const unreadIds = (data||[]).filter(n => !n.read).map(n => n.id); if (unreadIds.length) { try { await supabase.from('handoff_notes').update({ read: true }).in('id', unreadIds); } catch {} } res.json({ success: true, notes: data || [], unread_count: unreadIds.length }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'psw.handoff-notes.error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // POST /visit/forms/submit — Submit a compliance form for a visit // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ app.post('/visit/forms/submit', async (req, res) => { try { const { psw_name, pin, operator_id = 'proximity-care', visit_id, client_name, form_name, items } = req.body; if (!psw_name || !pin) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'psw_name and pin required' }); if (!form_name) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'form_name required' }); const valid = await verifyPSW(psw_name, pin, operator_id); if (!valid) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid PIN' }); const submittedAt = new Date().toISOString(); // Upsert — if form already exists for this visit, update it const { data, error } = await supabase.from('visit_forms').upsert({ operator_id, form_name, visit_id: visit_id || null, client_name: client_name || null, psw_name, items: items || [], submitted: true, submitted_at: submittedAt, created_at: submittedAt }, { onConflict: 'visit_id,form_name' }).select().single(); if (error) throw error; log('info', 'form.submitted', { operator_id, form_name, visit_id, psw_name, client_name }); res.json({ success: true, submitted_at: submittedAt, form_id: data?.id }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'form.submit.error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // GET /hq/forms — All visit forms for HQ // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ app.get('/hq/forms', async (req, res) => { try { const { operator_id = 'proximity-care', client_name, from_date, to_date, visit_id, submitted_only } = req.query; let q = supabase.from('visit_forms').select('*').eq('operator_id', operator_id) .order('created_at', { ascending: false }).limit(200); if (client_name) q = q.eq('client_name', client_name); if (visit_id) q = q.eq('visit_id', visit_id); if (from_date) q = q.gte('created_at', from_date); if (to_date) q = q.lte('created_at', to_date + 'T23:59:59'); if (submitted_only === 'true') q = q.eq('submitted', true); const { data, error } = await q; if (error) throw error; res.json({ success: true, forms: data || [], total: data?.length || 0 }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'hq.forms.error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // POST /hq/shift-offer/broadcast — Broadcast open shift to PSWs // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ app.post('/hq/shift-offer/broadcast', async (req, res) => { try { const { operator_id = 'proximity-care', client_name, scheduled_date, scheduled_time, duration_minutes, client_area, psw_names, broadcast_all = false } = req.body; if (!client_name || !scheduled_date) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'client_name and scheduled_date required' }); // Get PSWs to notify let targetPSWs = psw_names || []; if (broadcast_all || !targetPSWs.length) { const { data: allPSWs } = await supabase.from('psws') .select('name').eq('operator_id', operator_id).eq('status', 'active'); targetPSWs = (allPSWs || []).map(p => p.name).filter(Boolean); } // Create shift offer row const { data: offer, error } = await supabase.from('shift_offers').insert({ operator_id, client_name, scheduled_date, scheduled_time: scheduled_time || null, duration_minutes: duration_minutes || null, client_area: client_area || null, broadcast_to: targetPSWs, status: 'open', created_at: new Date().toISOString() }).select().single(); if (error) throw error; // Notify each PSW via psw_notes let notifiedCount = 0; for (const pswName of targetPSWs) { try { const msg = `Open shift available: ${client_name} on ${scheduled_date}${scheduled_time ? ' at ' + scheduled_time : ''}${duration_minutes ? ' (' + (duration_minutes/60).toFixed(1) + 'h)' : ''}. Tap to accept in your portal.`; await supabase.from('psw_notes').insert({ operator_id, psw_name: pswName, sender: 'system', message: msg, read: false, created_at: new Date().toISOString() }); notifiedCount++; } catch {} } log('info', 'shift-offer.broadcast', { operator_id, offer_id: offer?.id, client_name, notified: notifiedCount }); res.json({ success: true, offer_id: offer?.id, notified_count: notifiedCount, broadcast_to: targetPSWs }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'shift-offer.broadcast.error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // POST /hq/shift-offer/:id/cancel — Coordinator cancels an open broadcast // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ app.post('/hq/shift-offer/:id/cancel', async (req, res) => { try { const { id } = req.params; const { operator_id = 'proximity-care' } = req.body; const { data: offer } = await supabase.from('shift_offers') .select('*').eq('id', id).eq('operator_id', operator_id).maybeSingle(); if (!offer) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Offer not found' }); if (offer.status === 'filled') return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Cannot cancel a filled offer' }); const { error } = await supabase.from('shift_offers') .update({ status: 'cancelled', cancelled_at: new Date().toISOString() }) .eq('id', id).eq('operator_id', operator_id); if (error) throw error; log('info', 'shift-offer.cancelled', { operator_id, offer_id: id, client_name: offer.client_name }); res.json({ success: true, cancelled: true }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'shift-offer.cancel.error', { error: err.message || String(err) }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // POST /psw/shift-offer/respond — PSW accepts or declines a shift offer // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ app.post('/psw/shift-offer/respond', async (req, res) => { try { const { psw_name, pin, operator_id = 'proximity-care', offer_id, response } = req.body; if (!psw_name || !pin) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'psw_name and pin required' }); if (!offer_id || !response) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'offer_id and response required' }); if (!['accept','decline'].includes(response)) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'response must be accept or decline' }); const valid = await verifyPSW(psw_name, pin, operator_id); if (!valid) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid PIN' }); // Check offer still open const { data: offer } = await supabase.from('shift_offers') .select('*').eq('id', offer_id).eq('operator_id', operator_id).maybeSingle(); if (!offer) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Offer not found' }); if (offer.status !== 'open') return res.json({ success: true, status: offer.status, note: 'Offer already filled' }); if (response === 'accept') { const { error } = await supabase.from('shift_offers').update({ status: 'filled', accepted_by: psw_name, accepted_at: new Date().toISOString() }).eq('id', offer_id); if (error) throw error; // Notify coordinator via system_logs log('info', 'shift-offer.accepted', { operator_id, offer_id, psw_name, client_name: offer.client_name }); // Send coordinator notification try { await supabase.from('psw_notes').insert({ operator_id, psw_name: 'lance', sender: 'system', message: `${psw_name} accepted the open shift for ${offer.client_name} on ${offer.scheduled_date}${offer.scheduled_time ? ' at ' + offer.scheduled_time : ''}.`, read: false, created_at: new Date().toISOString() }); } catch {} res.json({ success: true, status: 'filled', accepted: true }); } else { // Log decline but keep offer open for others log('info', 'shift-offer.declined', { operator_id, offer_id, psw_name, client_name: offer.client_name }); res.json({ success: true, status: 'open', declined: true }); } } catch (err) { log('error', 'shift-offer.respond.error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // GET /hq/shift-offers — All shift offers for HQ // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ app.get('/hq/shift-offers', async (req, res) => { try { const { operator_id = 'proximity-care', status, from_date } = req.query; const { data, error } = await q; if (error) throw error; const open = (data||[]).filter(o => o.status === 'open').length; res.json({ success: true, offers: data || [], open_count: open, total: data?.length || 0 }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'hq.shift-offers.error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // GET /psw/shift-offers — Open shift offers visible to a PSW // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ app.get('/psw/shift-offers', async (req, res) => { try { const { psw_name, pin, operator_id = 'proximity-care' } = req.query; if (!psw_name || !pin) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'psw_name and pin required' }); if (!reason) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'reason required' }); const valid = await verifyPSW(psw_name, pin, operator_id); if (!valid) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid PIN' }); // Insert cancellation request const { error } = await supabase.from('cancellation_requests').insert({ operator_id, psw_name, booking_id: booking_id || null, client_name: client_name || null, scheduled_date: scheduled_date || null, scheduled_time: scheduled_time || null, reason, status: 'pending', created_at: new Date().toISOString() }); if (error) throw error; // Notify coordinator const msg = `${psw_name} cannot make their shift${client_name ? ' with ' + client_name : ''}${scheduled_date ? ' on ' + scheduled_date : ''}. Reason: ${reason}. Please review in HQ.`; try { await supabase.from('psw_notes').insert({ operator_id, psw_name: 'lance', sender: 'system', message: msg, read: false, created_at: new Date().toISOString() }); } catch {} log('info', 'cancellation-request.created', { operator_id, psw_name, client_name, reason }); res.json({ success: true, note: 'Request sent to coordinator. Your shift remains assigned until reviewed.' }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'cancellation-request.error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // GET /hq/cancellation-requests — Pending cancellation requests for HQ // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ app.get('/hq/cancellation-requests', async (req, res) => { try { const { operator_id = 'proximity-care', status = 'pending' } = req.query; let q = supabase.from('cancellation_requests').select('*').eq('operator_id', operator_id) .order('created_at', { ascending: false }).limit(50); if (status !== 'all') q = q.eq('status', status); const { data, error } = await q; if (error) throw error; res.json({ success: true, requests: data || [], pending_count: (data||[]).filter(r => r.status==='pending').length }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'hq.cancellation-requests.error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // POST /hq/cancellation-requests/:id/respond — Approve or reject cancellation // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ app.post('/hq/cancellation-requests/:id/respond', async (req, res) => { try { const { id } = req.params; const { operator_id = 'proximity-care', action, note } = req.body; if (!['approve','reject'].includes(action)) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'action must be approve or reject' }); const { data: req_row } = await supabase.from('cancellation_requests') .select('*').eq('id', id).eq('operator_id', operator_id).maybeSingle(); if (!req_row) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Request not found' }); await supabase.from('cancellation_requests').update({ status: action === 'approve' ? 'approved' : 'rejected', resolved_at: new Date().toISOString(), resolution_note: note || null }).eq('id', id); // Notify PSW const pswMsg = action === 'approve' ? `Your cancellation request for ${req_row.client_name || 'your shift'} on ${req_row.scheduled_date || 'the scheduled date'} has been approved. The shift will be reassigned.` : `Your cancellation request for ${req_row.client_name || 'your shift'} on ${req_row.scheduled_date || 'the scheduled date'} was not approved. Please plan to attend your shift.${note ? ' Note: ' + note : ''}`; try { await supabase.from('psw_notes').insert({ operator_id, psw_name: req_row.psw_name, sender: 'system', message: pswMsg, read: false, created_at: new Date().toISOString() }); } catch {} // If approved — auto-broadcast open shift if (action === 'approve' && req_row.booking_id) { await fetch(`http://localhost:${process.env.PORT||3000}/hq/shift-offer/broadcast`, { method: 'POST', headers: {'Content-Type':'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify({ operator_id, client_name: req_row.client_name, scheduled_date: req_row.scheduled_date, scheduled_time: req_row.scheduled_time, broadcast_all: true }) }).catch(e => log('warn', 'async.silent.failed', { error: e?.message || String(e) })); } log('info', 'cancellation-request.resolved', { operator_id, id, action, psw_name: req_row.psw_name }); res.json({ success: true, action, auto_broadcast: action === 'approve' }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'cancellation-request.respond.error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ── NO-SHOW CHECK — Railway cron hits POST /hq/noshow-check every 30 min ── app.post('/hq/noshow-check', async (req, res) => { try { const operator_id = req.body.operator_id || 'proximity-care'; const now = new Date(); // Toronto timezone for PSW shift comparisons const todayStr = now.toLocaleDateString('en-CA', { timeZone: 'America/Toronto' }); const torontoNow = new Date(now.toLocaleString('en-US', { timeZone: 'America/Toronto' })); const nowMins = torontoNow.getHours()*60 + torontoNow.getMinutes(); // Find bookings that started 30+ min ago with no checkin const { data: bookings } = await supabase .from('bookings') .select('id, assigned_to, client_name, scheduled_time, duration_minutes') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .eq('scheduled_date', todayStr) .eq('status', 'scheduled') .not('assigned_to', 'is', null); if (!bookings || !bookings.length) { try { await supabase.from('system_logs').insert({ operator_id, event_type: 'noshow_check_run', event_source: '/hq/noshow-check', payload: { checked: 0, noshows: 0, reason: 'no_bookings_today' }, status: 'complete', created_at: new Date().toISOString() }); } catch {} return res.json({ success: true, noshows: 0 }); } let flagged = 0; for (const b of bookings) { if (!b.scheduled_time) continue; const [h, m] = b.scheduled_time.split(':').map(Number); const shiftMins = h*60 + m; const minsLate = nowMins - shiftMins; if (minsLate < 30 || minsLate > 120) continue; // only flag 30-120 min window // Check if visit already started const { data: activeVisit } = await supabase .from('visits') .select('id') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .eq('psw_name', b.assigned_to) .eq('visit_date', todayStr) .not('time_in', 'is', null) .maybeSingle(); if (activeVisit) continue; // already checked in // Check if already flagged in last 2 hours const { data: recentLog } = await supabase .from('system_logs') .select('id') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .eq('event_type', 'noshow_alert') .eq('contact_name', b.assigned_to) .gte('created_at', new Date(now - 2*3600000).toISOString()) .maybeSingle(); const alertEmail = opRow?.owner_email || 'healthcareproximity@gmail.com'; await sendEmail({ to: alertEmail, subject: `⚠ No check-in — ${b.assigned_to} · ${b.client_name} · ${b.scheduled_time}`, html: `

    No Check-In Alert

    ${b.assigned_to} has not checked in for their ${b.scheduled_time} shift with ${b.client_name}.

    This is ${minsLate} minutes after the scheduled start time. Please follow up.

    ` }).catch(e => log('warn', 'async.silent.failed', { error: e?.message || String(e) })); // Log the alert try { await supabase.from('system_logs').insert({ operator_id, event_type: 'noshow_alert', event_source: '/hq/noshow-check', contact_name: b.assigned_to, payload: { client: b.client_name, scheduled_time: b.scheduled_time, mins_late: minsLate }, status: 'success' }); } catch {} flagged++; } try { await supabase.from('system_logs').insert({ operator_id, event_type: 'noshow_check_run', event_source: '/hq/noshow-check', payload: { checked: bookings.length, noshows: flagged }, status: 'complete', created_at: new Date().toISOString() }); } catch {} // ── P2: Joint visit partner no-show check ────────────────────────── // For any in-progress visits with joint_visit_id, check if a partner row exists. // If partner was supposed to be there (joint_booking exists) but never checked in — alert. const { data: inProgressJoints } = await supabase .from('visits') .select('id, psw_name, client_name, joint_visit_id, time_in') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .eq('visit_date', todayStr) .eq('status', 'in_progress') .not('joint_visit_id', 'is', null); for (const v of (inProgressJoints||[])) { // Check if the partner has also checked in const { data: partnerVisit } = await supabase .from('visits') .select('id') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .eq('joint_visit_id', v.joint_visit_id) .neq('psw_name', v.psw_name) .maybeSingle(); if (partnerVisit) continue; // partner checked in — all good // Check visit started 30+ min ago const checkinTime = new Date(v.time_in); const minsElapsed = (now - checkinTime) / 60000; if (minsElapsed < 30 || minsElapsed > 180) continue; // Check if already alerted const { data: existingAlert } = await supabase .from('system_logs') .select('id') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .eq('event_type', 'joint_partner_noshow') .eq('contact_name', v.client_name) .gte('created_at', new Date(now - 2*3600000).toISOString()) .maybeSingle(); if (existingAlert) continue; const { data: opRow2 } = await supabase .from('operators').select('owner_email, agency_name') .eq('operator_id', operator_id).maybeSingle(); const alertEmail2 = opRow2?.owner_email || 'healthcareproximity@gmail.com';     ⚠ Joint Visit — Partner No-Show

    ${v.psw_name} checked in for ${v.client_name} ${Math.round(minsElapsed)} minutes ago but the second PSW has not checked in.

    This client requires 2 PSWs. Please follow up immediately.

    ` }).catch(() => {}); try { await supabase.from('system_logs').insert({ operator_id, event_type: 'joint_partner_noshow', event_source: '/hq/noshow-check', contact_name: v.client_name, notes: `${v.psw_name} checked in solo for 2-person client ${v.client_name} — partner never arrived`, status: 'warning', created_at: new Date().toISOString() }); } catch {} flagged++; } // ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── res.json({ success: true, noshows: flagged, checked: bookings.length }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'noshow-check error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ── SAME-DAY SHIFT REMINDER — Railway cron hits POST /hq/shift-reminder-today every hour ── // Fires 60-90 min before shift start app.post('/hq/shift-reminder-today', async (req, res) => { try { // Allow internal cron dispatcher (WATCHDOG_PIN) or HQ session token const isCron = req.body.pin === WATCHDOG_PIN; const todayStr = torontoDate(); // Toronto time — Railway runs UTC, shift times are stored in Toronto time const _torontoTime = now.toLocaleTimeString('en-CA', { timeZone: 'America/Toronto', hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit', hour12: false }); } const { data: bookings } = await query; if (!bookings || !bookings.length) return res.json({ success: true, sent: 0, detail: 'No matching bookings' }); let sent = 0; for (const b of bookings) { if (!b.scheduled_time) continue; // Time window check — skip ONLY in cron mode (no booking_id) if (!booking_id) { const [h, m] = b.scheduled_time.split(':').map(Number); const shiftMins = h*60 + m; const minsUntil = shiftMins - nowMins;     Shift Starting Soon

    30 Minute Reminder

    Hi ${b.assigned_to.split(' ')[0]}, your shift starts in about 30 minutes.

    ${b.location ? `` : ''}
    Client${b.client_name}
    Time${b.scheduled_time}
    Location${b.location}

    Remember to check in on your PSW portal when you arrive.

    ` }).catch(e => log('warn', 'async.silent.failed', { error: e?.message || String(e) })); try { await supabase.from('system_logs').insert({ operator_id, event_type: 'shift_reminder_today', event_source: '/hq/shift-reminder-today', contact_name: b.assigned_to, payload: { client: b.client_name, scheduled_time: b.scheduled_time }, status: 'success' }); } catch {} sent++; } try { await supabase.from('system_logs').insert({ operator_id, event_type: 'shift_reminder_today_run', event_source: '/hq/shift-reminder-today', payload: { sent }, status: 'complete', created_at: new Date().toISOString() }); } catch {} res.json({ success: true, sent }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'shift-reminder-today error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ── DAILY DIGEST — Railway cron hits POST /hq/daily-digest at 8pm EST ── app.post('/hq/daily-digest', async (req, res) => { try { const operator_id = req.body.operator_id || 'proximity-care'; const todayStr = new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10); // Get all clients with family emails const { data: clients } = await supabase .from('clients') .select('id, first_name, last_name, family_email, family_contact_name, portal_slug, assigned_psw') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .not('family_email', 'is', null);     ${v.psw_name} · ${v.time_in||''}${v.time_out?' – '+v.time_out:''} (${v.hours_worked||0}h)

    Mood: ${v.client_mood}

    ` : ''} ${v.visit_summary ? `

    ${v.visit_summary}

    ` : ''} ${tasks ? `

    Tasks: ${tasks}

    ` : ''} ${meds ? `

    Medications: ${meds}

    ` : ''} ${v.incident_reported ? `

    ⚠ A note was logged — your coordinator has been notified.

    ` : ''}
    `; }).join(''); const nextShiftHtml = nextBooking ? `

    Next Scheduled Visit

    ${nextBooking.scheduled_date} at ${nextBooking.scheduled_time} · ${nextBooking.assigned_to}

    ` : ''; await sendEmail({ to: client.family_email, subject: `${clientFirst}'s daily care summary — ${todayStr}`, html: `

    Proximity Care Services

    Daily Care Summary · ${todayStr}

    Hi ${greeting},

    Here's a summary of ${clientFirst}'s care today — ${totalHours.toFixed(1)} hours total.

    ${visitSummaries} ${nextShiftHtml}
    View Full Portal →

    Proximity Care Services Inc. · 647-382-8047

    ` }).catch(e => log('error', 'digest.failed', { client: clientName, error: e.message })); try { await supabase.from('system_logs').insert({ operator_id, event_type: 'daily_digest', event_source: '/hq/daily-digest', contact_name: clientName, payload: { visits: todayVisits.length, hours: totalHours }, status: 'success' }); } catch {} sent++; } try { await supabase.from('system_logs').insert({ operator_id, event_type: 'daily_digest_run', event_source: '/hq/daily-digest', payload: { sent, date: todayStr }, status: 'complete', created_at: new Date().toISOString() }); } catch {} res.json({ success: true, sent, date: todayStr }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'daily-digest error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ── SENTIMENT — GET /hq/sentiment/:operator_id — per-client satisfaction trends ── app.get('/hq/sentiment/:operator_id', async (req, res) => { try { const operator_id = req.params.operator_id; const now = new Date(); const day30 = new Date(now - 30*86400000).toISOString().slice(0,10); const day60 = new Date(now - 60*86400000).toISOString().slice(0,10); const { data: clients } = await supabase .from('clients') .select('id, first_name, last_name') .eq('operator_id', operator_id); if (!clients || !clients.length) return res.json({ success: true, sentiment: [] }); const sentiment = await Promise.all(clients.map(async c => { const clientName = `${c.first_name||''} ${c.last_name||''}`.trim(); const { data: recent } = await supabase .from('visits') .select('satisfaction_rating, visit_date') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .eq('client_name', clientName) .not('satisfaction_rating', 'is', null) .gte('visit_date', day60) .order('visit_date', { ascending: false }); if (!recent || !recent.length) return { client_name: clientName, avg: null, trend: null, count: 0 }; const last30 = recent.filter(v => v.visit_date >= day30); const prev30 = recent.filter(v => v.visit_date < day30); const avg = (arr) => arr.length ? arr.reduce((s,v) => s + (v.satisfaction_rating||0), 0) / arr.length : null; const avgRecent = avg(last30); const avgPrev = avg(prev30); let trend = 'stable'; if (avgRecent && avgPrev) { if (avgRecent > avgPrev + 0.3) trend = 'up'; else if (avgRecent < avgPrev - 0.3) trend = 'down'; } return { client_name: clientName, client_id: c.id, avg: avgRecent ? Math.round(avgRecent * 10) / 10 : null, avg_prev: avgPrev ? Math.round(avgPrev * 10) / 10 : null, trend, count: last30.length, alert: avgRecent && avgRecent < 3.5 }; })); const agencyAvg = sentiment.filter(s => s.avg).reduce((sum, s, _, arr) => sum + s.avg / arr.filter(x=>x.avg).length, 0); res.json({ success: true, sentiment, agency_avg: agencyAvg ? Math.round(agencyAvg * 10) / 10 : null }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'sentiment error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // POST /psw/upload-photo — upload a task photo during visit checkout // Accepts base64 image, stores in Supabase visit-photos bucket, returns public URL app.post('/psw/upload-photo', async (req, res) => { try { const { psw_name, pin, operator_id = 'proximity-care', path, type } = req.body; } // Get public URL for the path const { data: urlData } = supabase.storage .from('visit-photos') .getPublicUrl(path); res.json({ success: true, signed_url: signedData.signedUrl, token: signedData.token, url: urlData?.publicUrl || `${process.env.SUPABASE_URL}/storage/v1/object/public/visit-photos/${path}` }); // Tightened system prompt — no internal details, no names, no PHI const systemPrompt = `You are a care assistant for ${agencyName}. A family member is asking about their loved one's care. Rules you must follow: - Answer ONLY based on the visit context provided. Never invent facts. - Do NOT reveal caregiver names, internal agency details, or any health information beyond what is in the context. - Keep answers under 3 sentences and warm in tone. - If you cannot answer from context, say so and suggest they call ${coordinatorPhone}. - Never discuss other clients, staff details, internal operations, or billing.`; const userMsg = `Visit context: ${(visit_context || 'No visits on file.').slice(0, 500)}\n\nFamily question: ${cleanQuestion}`; // PHIPA: anonymize with real names this time const { anonymized: anonUserMsg, deAnonymize: deAnonFamily } = phipaAnonymize(userMsg, namesArray); const response = await anthropic.messages.create({ model: 'claude-sonnet-4-20250514', max_tokens: 250, system: systemPrompt, messages: [{ role: 'user', content: anonUserMsg }] }); const reply = deAnonFamily(response.content[0]?.text || `I wasn't able to retrieve that information right now. Please call ${coordinatorPhone} directly.`); log('info', 'family.chat.success', { slug, operator_id: client.operator_id }); res.json({ success: true, reply }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'family/chat error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message, reply: 'Something went wrong. Please contact your coordinator directly.' }); } }); app.post('/family/private-note', async (req, res) => { try { const { slug, pin, note } = req.body; if (!slug || !note) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'slug and note required' }); // Verify family PIN const { data: client, error: clientErr } = await supabase .from('clients') .select('id, first_name, last_name, operator_id, family_contact_name, portal_pin') .eq('portal_slug', slug) .maybeSingle(); if (clientErr || !client) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Client not found' }); if (pin && client.portal_pin && String(client.portal_pin) !== String(pin)) { return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid PIN' }); } const clientName = `${client.first_name||''} ${client.last_name||''}`.trim(); // Insert into family_notes table const { data: noteRow, error: insertErr } = await supabase .from('family_notes') .insert({ operator_id: client.operator_id || 'proximity-care', client_slug: slug, client_name: clientName, note: note.trim(), from_name: client.family_contact_name || 'Family', visible_to: 'operator' }) .select() .single(); if (insertErr) throw insertErr; // Notify operator via email const { data: opRow } = await supabase .from('operators') .select('owner_email, agency_name') .eq('operator_id', client.operator_id || 'proximity-care') .maybeSingle(); const alertEmail = opRow?.owner_email || 'healthcareproximity@gmail.com'; await sendEmail({ to: alertEmail, subject: `Private note from ${clientName}'s family`, html: `

    ${clientName}

    From: ${client.family_contact_name || 'Family'}

    ${note.trim()}

    This note is private — only visible to you, not shown in the family portal.

    ` }).catch(e => log('warn', 'async.silent.failed', { error: e?.message || String(e) })); // Log to system_logs try { await supabase.from('system_logs').insert({ operator_id: client.operator_id || 'proximity-care', event_type: 'family_private_note', event_source: '/family/private-note', contact_name: clientName, payload: { note_id: noteRow.id, from: client.family_contact_name }, status: 'success' }); } }); // GET /hq/family-notes — operator reads all private family notes app.get('/hq/family-notes', async (req, res) => { try { const { operator_id = 'proximity-care', limit = 50 } = req.query; const { data: notes, error } = await supabase .from('family_notes') .select('*') .eq('operator_id', operator_id) .order('created_at', { ascending: false }) .limit(parseInt(limit)); } }); // ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── // BUILD 27 — STRIPE WEBHOOK // ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── app.post('/webhook/stripe', async (req, res) => { const sig = req.headers['stripe-signature']; const secret = process.env.STRIPE_WEBHOOK_SECRET; if (!secret) return res.status(500).json({ error: 'STRIPE_WEBHOOK_SECRET not set' }); // Verify signature let event; try { const hmac = crypto.createHmac('sha256', secret); const [tPart, v1Part] = (sig || '').split(',').reduce((acc, part) => { const [k, v] = part.trim().split('='); if (k === 't') acc[0] = v; if (k === 'v1') acc[1] = v; return acc; }, [null, null]); const payload = `${tPart}.${req.body.toString()}`; hmac.update(payload); const expected = hmac.digest('hex'); if (expected !== v1Part) throw new Error('Signature mismatch'); event = JSON.parse(req.body.toString()); } catch (err) { log('error', 'Stripe webhook signature error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid signature' }); } try { const obj = event.data?.object || {}; // Subscription created → create operator + fire Day 0 if (event.type === 'customer.subscription.created') { const customerId = obj.customer; const email = obj.metadata?.owner_email || obj.customer_email || null; const agencyName = obj.metadata?.agency_name || 'New Agency'; const ownerName = obj.metadata?.owner_name || ''; const operatorId = (agencyName.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, '-').replace(/^-|-$/g, '')) + '-' + Date.now().toString().slice(-4); console.log('Stripe webhook: subscription.created'); // Create operator row const now = new Date().toISOString(); const { error: opErr } = await supabase.from('operator_config').insert({ operator_id: operatorId, agency_name: agencyName, owner_name: ownerName, owner_email: email, stripe_customer_id: customerId, stripe_subscription_id: obj.id, active: true, tier: 'tier2', brand_primary: '#3d8a7a', brand_accent: '#c8a96e', onboarding_step: 0, created_by: 'stripe-webhook', created_at: now }); if (opErr) log('error', 'Stripe webhook: operator insert error', { error: opErr.message || String(opErr), trace_id: req?._traceId }); // Fire Day 0 welcome email if (email) { try { await fetch('https://proximity-agent-production.up.railway.app/operator/post-close', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ operator_id: operatorId, agency_name: agencyName, owner_name: ownerName, owner_email: email }) }); } catch (e) { log('error', 'Stripe webhook: post-close error', { error: e.message || String(e), trace_id: req?._traceId }); } } // Log try { await supabase.from('system_logs').insert({ operator_id: operatorId, event_type: 'stripe_subscription_created', event_source: '/webhook/stripe', contact_name: agencyName, payload: JSON.stringify({ customerId, email, operatorId }), status: 'complete', created_at: now }); } catch {} } // One-time payment completed (buy link) → create operator immediately if (event.type === 'checkout.session.completed') { const session = obj; const email = session.customer_details?.email || session.metadata?.owner_email || null;
