res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ── CALL SLOT HELPERS ───────────────────────────────────────────── function getAvailableSlots() { const slots = []; const now = new Date(); for (let d = 1; slots.length < 15 && d <= 21; d++) { const date = new Date(now); date.setDate(now.getDate() + d); const dow = date.getDay(); if (dow === 0 || dow === 6) continue; const label = date.toLocaleDateString('en-CA', { timeZone: 'America/Toronto', weekday: 'long', month: 'long', day: 'numeric' }); const iso = date.toISOString().slice(0, 10); ['10:00 AM', '1:00 PM', '3:00 PM'].forEach(time => { slots.push({ label: `${label} at ${time}`, value: `${iso}_${time.replace(/[: ]/g, '')}` }); }); } return slots.slice(0, 15); } function slotToDate(slotValue) { const [datePart, timePart] = slotValue.split('_'); const timeMap = { '1000AM': '10:00', '100PM': '13:00', '300PM': '15:00' }; const timeStr = timeMap[timePart] || '10:00'; return new Date(`${datePart}T${timeStr}:00-04:00`); } // GET /leads/call-slots app.get('/leads/call-slots', (req, res) => { res.json({ success: true, slots: getAvailableSlots() }); }); // POST /leads/book-call — family picks call slot from email link app.post('/leads/book-call', async (req, res) => { try { const { lead_id, slot, operator_id = 'proximity-care' } = req.body;     `); } catch (err) { log('error', 'confirm-interview error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).send('Error confirming — check Railway logs.'); } }); // ── AUTO-DEBUG ENGINE ────────────────────────────────────────────── // POST /hq/auto-debug // Pulls a file from GitHub, runs full CLAUDE.md debug protocol via Claude, // returns fixed file + diff summary. Human approves before push. app.post('/hq/auto-debug', async (req, res) => { try { const { repo, filepath, error_description, operator_id = 'proximity-care' } = req.body; if (!repo || !filepath) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'repo and filepath required' }); const GITHUB_TOKEN = process.env.GITHUB_TOKEN; const GITHUB_OWNER = 'lanceyslzr'; // ── STEP 1: Pull current file from GitHub ── const ghUrl = `https://api.github.com/repos/${GITHUB_OWNER}/${repo}/contents/${filepath}`; const ghRes = await fetch(ghUrl, { headers: { 'Authorization': `token ${GITHUB_TOKEN}`, 'Accept': 'application/vnd.github.v3+json', 'User-Agent': 'proximity-agent' } }); if (!ghRes.ok) throw new Error(`GitHub fetch failed: ${ghRes.status}`); const ghData = await ghRes.json(); const originalContent = Buffer.from(ghData.content, 'base64').toString('utf8'); const fileSha = ghData.sha; // ── STEP 2: Run CLAUDE.md debug protocol ── const debugSystemPrompt = `You are the Proximity Systems auto-debugger. You know every rule from CLAUDE.md and all session operating rules. ABSOLUTE RULES — check every one: 1. node --check must pass — no syntax errors 2. No duplicate function declarations anywhere in the file 3. No getElementById referencing IDs that do not exist in HTML (except dynamic ones created via createElement) 4. CSS source order: all base CSS first, then @media(1024px) → @media(900px) → @media(768px) → @media(600px). @media blocks MUST be last. 5. No direct api.anthropic.com calls from browser — must route through Railway 6. operator_id on ALL Supabase queries — no unscoped queries 7. Session restore only clears localStorage on HTTP 401 — never on 503 or network errors 8. No hardcoded operator_id 'proximity-care' in PSW portal — use pswOperatorId variable 9. hours_worked is a generated column — never UPDATE directly 10. thelifecareexperts.com — never touch, never modify 11. No escaped quotes inside template literals — use single quotes or restructure 12. No orphaned CSS classes — every class referenced in JS must exist in CSS 13. No duplicate const/let/var declarations at same scope 14. All Railway endpoints called from frontend must exist in server.js 15. Voice AI / Telnyx must never be claimed as live — Phase 2 only ROOT CAUSE RULE: Fix only the root cause. Never patch symptoms. Never add workarounds. OUTPUT RULE: Return the complete fixed file only. No explanation. No markdown fences. No partial output. Complete file or nothing.`; const userPrompt = `File: ${filepath} in repo: ${repo} Error or issue reported: ${error_description || 'General debug — run full audit'} Current file content: ${originalContent} Run the full debug protocol. Fix all issues found. Return the complete corrected file.`; const debugResponse = await anthropic.messages.create({ model: 'claude-sonnet-4-20250514', max_tokens: 8000, system: debugSystemPrompt, messages: [{ role: 'user', content: userPrompt }] }); const fixedContent = debugResponse.content[0]?.text || ''; if (!fixedContent || fixedContent.length < 100) throw new Error('Claude returned empty fix'); // ── STEP 3: Generate diff summary ── const originalLines = originalContent.split('\n').length; const fixedLines = fixedContent.split('\n').length; const lineDiff = fixedLines - originalLines; // Simple change detection — find lines that differ const origArr = originalContent.split('\n'); const fixArr = fixedContent.split('\n'); const changes = []; const maxCheck = Math.min(origArr.length, fixArr.length); for (let i = 0; i < maxCheck; i++) { if (origArr[i] !== fixArr[i]) { changes.push({ line: i + 1, before: origArr[i]?.trim().slice(0, 80), after: fixArr[i]?.trim().slice(0, 80) }); if (changes.length >= 10) break; } } // Store fixed content temporarily in Supabase for approval step const debugId = require('crypto').randomBytes(16).toString('hex'); await supabase.from('debug_queue').insert({ id: debugId, operator_id, repo, filepath, file_sha: fileSha, original_content: originalContent, fixed_content: fixedContent, error_description: error_description || 'Manual debug run', changes_summary: JSON.stringify(changes), created_at: new Date().toISOString(), approved: false }).catch(e => log('warn', 'async.silent.failed', { error: e?.message || String(e) })); // Table may not exist yet — non-fatal res.json({ success: true, debug_id: debugId, repo, filepath, original_lines: originalLines, fixed_lines: fixedLines, line_diff: lineDiff, changes_preview: changes, fixed_content: fixedContent, message: `Debug complete. ${changes.length} change areas found. Review and approve to push.` }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'auto-debug error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // POST /hq/auto-debug/push — Lance approves, pushes to GitHub app.post('/hq/auto-debug/push', async (req, res) => { const { pin } = req.body; if (pin !== WATCHDOG_PIN && req.headers['x-watchdog-pin'] !== WATCHDOG_PIN) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }); try { const { repo, filepath, file_sha, fixed_content, commit_message } = req.body; if (!repo || !filepath || !fixed_content || !file_sha) { return res.status(400).json({ error: 'repo, filepath, file_sha, and fixed_content required' }); } const GITHUB_TOKEN = process.env.GITHUB_TOKEN; const GITHUB_OWNER = 'lanceyslzr'; const encodedContent = Buffer.from(fixed_content).toString('base64'); const ghRes = await fetch(`https://api.github.com/repos/${GITHUB_OWNER}/${repo}/contents/${filepath}`, { method: 'PUT', headers: { 'Authorization': `token ${GITHUB_TOKEN}`, 'Accept': 'application/vnd.github.v3+json', 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'User-Agent': 'proximity-agent' }, body: JSON.stringify({ message: commit_message || `auto-fix: ${filepath} via Proximity debug engine`, content: encodedContent, sha: file_sha }) }); if (!ghRes.ok) { const errData = await ghRes.json().catch(() => ({})); throw new Error(`GitHub push failed: ${ghRes.status} — ${errData.message || ''}`); } const pushData = await ghRes.json(); const commitSha = pushData.commit?.sha?.slice(0, 7) || 'unknown'; // Notify Lance await sendEmail({ to: process.env.GMAIL_USER || 'healthcareproximity@gmail.com', subject: `Auto-fix pushed — ${filepath}`, html: `

    AUTO-FIX PUSHED

    ${filepath}

    Repo: ${repo}

    Commit: ${commitSha}

    ` }).catch(e => log('warn', 'async.silent.failed', { error: e?.message || String(e) })); res.json({ success: true, commit_sha: commitSha, message: `Pushed to ${repo}/${filepath} — deploying now` }); } catch (err) { log('error', 'auto-debug push error', { error: err.message || String(err), trace_id: req?._traceId }); res.status(500).json({ error: err.message }); } }); // ── DYNAMIC OPERATOR LIST — reads active operators from DB, 5-min cache ── let _operatorCache = { ids: [], fetchedAt: 0 }; const OPERATOR_CACHE_TTL = 5 * 60 * 1000; // 5 minutes async function getActiveOperators() { const now = Date.now(); if (_operatorCache.ids.length > 0 && (now - _operatorCache.fetchedAt) < OPERATOR_CACHE_TTL) { return _operatorCache.ids; } try { const { data, error } = await supabase .from('operator_config') .select('operator_id') .eq('active', true) .order('created_at', { ascending: true }); if (error) throw error; const ids = (data || []).map(r => r.operator_id).filter(Boolean); if (ids.length === 0) throw new Error('No active operators returned'); _operatorCache = { ids, fetchedAt: now }; log('info', 'operator.cache.refresh', { count: ids.length, operators: ids.join(',') }); return ids; } catch (err) { log('error', 'operator.cache.error', { error: err.message || String(err) }); // Safe fallback — never drop crons for proximity-care return _operatorCache.ids.length > 0 ? _operatorCache.ids : ['proximity-care']; } } // INFRA 1 — Sentry error handler (must be last middleware before app.listen) if (Sentry) { app.use(Sentry.Handlers.errorHandler()); } app.listen(PORT, () => { log('info', 'server.start', { port: PORT }); // ── INTERNAL CRONS ── // NOTE: shift-reminder-today and checklist-check are fired exclusively by // Railway cron via /system/run-crons. Internal setIntervals for those were // removed (S25) — they caused double-firing and duplicate emails. // noshow-check: runs every hour, endpoint handles time gating // Dynamically reads active operators from operator_config — auto-covers new agencies setInterval(async () => { try { const operators = await getActiveOperators(); log('info', 'internal.cron.noshow-check.start', { operators: operators.join(','), count: operators.length }); for (const op of operators) { await fetch(`http://localhost:${PORT}/hq/noshow-check`, { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ operator_id: op }) }).catch(e => log('warn', 'internal.cron.noshow-check', { error: e.message, operator_id: op })); } } catch (e) { log('error', 'internal.cron.noshow-check.crash', { error: e.message }); } }, 60 * 60 * 1000); // every 60 minutes // followup/run: S04 email sequence — every 5 minutes — dynamic multi-operator setInterval(async () => { try { const operators = await getActiveOperators(); for (const op of operators) { await fetch(`http://localhost:${PORT}/followup/run`, { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ operator_id: op }) }).catch(e => log('warn', 'internal.cron.followup', { error: e.message, operator_id: op })); } log('info', 'internal.cron.followup.complete', { operators: operators.join(',') }); } catch (e) { log('error', 'internal.cron.followup.crash', { error: e.message }); } }, 5 * 60 * 1000); // every 5 minutes // ── DAILY DIGEST — runs every 24 hours ── setInterval(async () => { try { const operators = await getActiveOperators(); for (const op of operators) { await fetch(`http://localhost:${PORT}/hq/daily-digest`, { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ operator_id: op }) }).catch(e => log('warn', 'internal.cron.daily-digest', { error: e.message, operator_id: op })); } log('info', 'internal.cron.daily-digest.complete', { operators: operators.join(',') }); } catch (e) { log('error', 'internal.cron.daily-digest.crash', { error: e.message }); } }, 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000); // every 24 hours // ── AUTO MONTHLY INVOICE — fires every 6 hours but endpoint date-gates to day 1-2 only ── // Using 6h interval instead of 24h so a server restart on the 1st doesn't miss the window. // The endpoint itself checks: if today > day 2 AND no manual month/year → skip. // This means at most 2-3 emails per month (day 1 AM, day 1 PM, day 2 AM) — not daily. setInterval(async () => { try { const torontoDay = parseInt(new Date().toLocaleDateString('en-CA', {timeZone:'America/Toronto'}).split('-')[2]); // every 6 hours — endpoint handles day gate // ── PSW EXPIRY CHECK — runs every 24 hours ── setInterval(async () => { try { const operators = await getActiveOperators(); for (const op of operators) { await fetch(`http://localhost:${PORT}/psw/expiry-check`, { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ operator_id: op }) }).catch(e => log('warn', 'internal.cron.psw-expiry', { error: e.message, operator_id: op })); } log('info', 'internal.cron.psw-expiry.complete', { operators: operators.join(',') }); try { await supabase.from('system_logs').insert({ operator_id: 'proximity-care', event_type: 'psw_expiry_run', event_source: 'cron', status: 'success', created_at: new Date().toISOString() }); const loginCutoff = new Date(Date.now() - 30 * 24 * 3600000).toISOString(); // Delete expired PSW sessions const { error: sessErr } = await supabase.from('psw_sessions') .delete() .lt('expires_at', new Date().toISOString()); if (attErr) log('warn', 'internal.cron.session-cleanup.attempts', { error: attErr.message }); log('info', 'internal.cron.session-cleanup.complete', { cutoff, loginCutoff }); } catch (e) { log('error', 'internal.cron.session-cleanup.crash', { error: e.message }); } }, 6 * 60 * 60 * 1000); // every 6 hours }); // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // POST /system/run-tests — Proximity Watchdog full integration test // PIN-gated. }); app.post('/system/run-tests', async (req, res) => { const { pin, operator_id = TEST_OPERATOR } = req.body; if (pin !== WATCHDOG_PIN) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid watchdog PIN' }); // Concurrent-run guard — prevent two simultaneous scans corrupting _watchdogRunning state if (_watchdogRunning) { return res.status(429).json({ error: 'Watchdog scan already in progress — wait for it to complete before starting a new one' }); } // Stream NDJSON — each line is one test result as it completes res.setHeader('Content-Type', 'application/x-ndjson'); res.setHeader('Transfer-Encoding', 'chunked'); res.setHeader('Cache-Control', 'no-cache'); res.setHeader('X-Accel-Buffering', 'no'); // prevent nginx/Railway proxy from buffering the stream res.setHeader('Connection', 'keep-alive'); res.flushHeaders(); // open the HTTP connection immediately — client sees the stream start right away const emit = (result) => { try { res.write(JSON.stringify(result) + '\n'); } catch(e) {} }; const run = async (id, group, name, fn) => { const t = Date.now(); try { const result = await fn(); const out = { id, group, name, latency: Date.now()-t, ...result }; emit(out); return out; } catch(e) { const out = { id, group, name, latency: Date.now()-t, status: 'crit', detail: e.message }; emit(out); return out; } }; // Track test data to clean up let testVisitId = null; let testLeadId = null; let testBookingId = null; _watchdogRunning = true; // suppress all outbound emails during this scan _watchdogStartedAt = Date.now(); const startTime = Date.now(); // Create a temporary internal HQ session for watchdog — scoped to this operator // This token is used for all HQ endpoint tests and is invalidated when scope ends const _watchdogToken = await createHQSession(operator_id); const _wdHQHeaders = { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'x-hq-token': _watchdogToken }; const _wdGETHeaders = { 'x-hq-token': _watchdogToken }; emit({ id: '__start', group: 'meta', name: 'Test run started', status: 'info', detail: `operator: ${operator_id} · ${new Date().toISOString()}` }); // ── LAYER 1: INFRASTRUCTURE ────────────────────────────────────── await run('infra-railway', 'Infrastructure', 'Railway server', async () => { const t = Date.now(); const r = await fetch(`${process.env.RAILWAY_PUBLIC_DOMAIN ? 'https://'+process.env.RAILWAY_PUBLIC_DOMAIN : 'http://localhost:'+(process.env.PORT||3000)}/`, { signal: AbortSignal.timeout(5000) }).catch(() => null); if (!r || !r.ok) return { status: 'crit', detail: 'Server not responding to self-check' }; return { status: 'ok', detail: `Server responding · ${Date.now()-t}ms` }; }); await run('infra-supabase', 'Infrastructure', 'Supabase connection', async () => { const { error } = await supabase.from('operator_config').select('operator_id').limit(1); if (error) return { status: 'crit', detail: `Supabase error: ${error.message}` }; return { status: 'ok', detail: 'Connection live · query returned' }; }); await run('infra-anthropic', 'Infrastructure', 'Anthropic API key', async () => { const key = process.env.ANTHROPIC_API_KEY; if (!key) return { status: 'crit', detail: 'ANTHROPIC_API_KEY not set in env' }; if (!key.startsWith('sk-ant-')) return { status: 'warn', detail: 'Key format unexpected' }; return { status: 'ok', detail: 'Key present and valid format' }; }); await run('infra-resend', 'Infrastructure', 'Resend API key', async () => { const key = process.env.RESEND_API_KEY; if (!key) return { status: 'crit', detail: 'RESEND_API_KEY not set in env' }; // Lightweight auth check — GET /api-keys doesn't send an email const r = await fetch('https://api.resend.com/api-keys', { headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${key}` }, signal: AbortSignal.timeout(5000) }).catch(() => null); if (!r) return { status: 'warn', detail: 'Resend unreachable' }; if (r.status === 401) return { status: 'crit', detail: 'Resend API key invalid' }; return { status: 'ok', detail: 'Resend key authenticated' }; }); await run('infra-stripe', 'Infrastructure', 'Stripe webhook secret', async () => { const secret = process.env.STRIPE_WEBHOOK_SECRET; if (!secret) return { status: 'crit', detail: 'STRIPE_WEBHOOK_SECRET not set — payments will not process' }; }); await run('session-cleanup-cron', 'S09 Crons', 'PSW session cleanup cron', async () => { // Verify psw_sessions and login_attempts tables exist for cleanup const { error: sErr } = await supabase.from('psw_sessions').select('id').limit(1); const { error: aErr } = await supabase.from('login_attempts').select('id').limit(1); if (sErr?.message?.includes('does not exist')) return { status: 'warn', detail: 'psw_sessions table missing — session cleanup cron will fail' }; const pass = !result.valid && result.error.includes('pin'); return pass ? { status: 'ok', detail: 'validateRequired helper active · missing field detection working' } : { status: 'warn', detail: 'validateRequired helper may not be working correctly' }; }); // ── CLEANUP ──────────────────────────────────────────────────── if (testLeadId) { await supabase.from('leads').delete().eq('id', testLeadId); } if (testVisitId) { await supabase.from('visits').delete().eq('id', testVisitId); } // ── FINAL SUMMARY ───────────────────────────────────────────── // Invalidate watchdog test token try { await supabase.from('hq_sessions').delete().eq('token', _watchdogToken); } catch {} emit({ id: '__done', group: 'meta', name: 'Test run complete', status: 'info', detail: `Completed in ${((Date.now()-startTime)/1000).toFixed(1)}s`, total_ms: Date.now()-startTime }); _watchdogRunning = false; // re-enable outbound emails _watchdogStartedAt = null; res.end(); }); // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // POST /system/run-crons — Multi-operator cron dispatcher // Railway hits this ONE endpoint on schedule. It reads all active // operators and fires every cron for each one automatically. // Replaces 5 separate Railway cron jobs with 1 dispatcher. // Auth: same WATCHDOG_PIN // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ app.post('/system/run-crons', async (req, res) => { const { pin, cron } = req.body; // cron = specific cron name, or omit for all if (pin !== WATCHDOG_PIN) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid PIN' }); const PORT_LOCAL = process.env.PORT || 3000; const BASE = `http://localhost:${PORT_LOCAL}`; // Read all active operators let operators = ['proximity-care']; // fallback try { const { data } = await supabase.from('operator_config').select('operator_id').eq('active', true); if (data && data.length) operators = data.map(r => r.operator_id).filter(Boolean); } catch (e) { log('warn', 'cron-dispatcher.operator-fetch-failed', { error: e.message }); } // Define all Railway cron jobs const CRONS = [ { id: 'shift-reminder', path: '/hq/shift-reminder', method: 'POST', body: op => ({ operator_id: op, dry_run: false }) }, { id: 'shift-reminder-today', path: '/hq/shift-reminder-today', method: 'POST', body: op => ({ operator_id: op, pin: WATCHDOG_PIN }) }, { id: 'noshow-check', path: '/hq/noshow-check', method: 'POST', body: op => ({ operator_id: op }) }, { id: 'daily-digest', path: '/hq/daily-digest', method: 'POST', body: op => ({ operator_id: op }) }, { id: 'checklist-check', path: '/visit/checklist-check', method: 'POST', body: op => ({ operator_id: op }) }, { id: 'auto-monthly', path: '/invoice/auto-monthly', method: 'POST', body: op => ({ operator_id: op }) }, { id: 'expiry-check', path: '/psw/expiry-check', method: 'POST', body: op => ({ operator_id: op }) }, { id: 'probation-check', path: '/psw/probation-check', method: 'POST', body: op => ({ operator_id: op }) }, { id: 'followup', path: '/followup/run', method: 'POST', body: op => ({ operator_id: op }) }, ]; const targetCrons = cron ? CRONS.filter(c => c.id === cron) : CRONS; const results = []; const startedAt = new Date().toISOString(); for (const c of targetCrons) { for (const op of operators) { const t = Date.now(); try { const r = await fetch(`${BASE}${c.path}`, { method: c.method, headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify(c.body(op)), signal: AbortSignal.timeout(30000) }); const d = await r.json().catch(() => ({})); results.push({ cron: c.id, operator: op, status: r.ok ? 'ok' : 'err', latency_ms: Date.now()-t, detail: d.error || d.sent || d.success || '' }); log('info', 'cron-dispatcher.fired', { cron: c.id, operator: op, status: r.ok ? 'ok' : 'err', latency_ms: Date.now()-t }); } catch (e) { results.push({ cron: c.id, operator: op, status: 'err', latency_ms: Date.now()-t, detail: e.message }); log('error', 'cron-dispatcher.error', { cron: c.id, operator: op, error: e.message }); } } } const errors = results.filter(r => r.status === 'err').length; log('info', 'cron-dispatcher.complete', { operators: operators.join(','), crons: targetCrons.map(c=>c.id).join(','), total: results.length, errors }); res.json({ success: true, started_at: startedAt, operators, crons_fired: targetCrons.map(c=>c.id), results, errors }); }); // GET /system/status — simple liveness check; confirms watchdog endpoint is reachable app.get('/system/status', (req, res) => { // Public OK — returns no data, just confirms server is up res.json({ status: 'ok' }); });
